LUK 13:1 Va temu eni mwa dighuki di batu, bamarughe oyi tsingule Djesu adimavyoghe: ave batu bamosi ba Ngalile, bamavaghulilaange paghu ombu Nzambi, Pilate akerume batu bandi ubaboke vane, mu usobene malungu mowu na ama paghu.
LUK 13:2 Djesu akebawake rye: «Dwitasi yiri, bise Ngalile beni abamaboku nane, bamabe bavayitsi ba mabi bavyoghulile bise Ngalile botsu?
LUK 13:3 Nesi, payi dwitasi nane, dumakedunze. Nyidulubusi yiri, payi dughakaluse mutsanu, dufu nane djowu.
LUK 13:4 Ka dighumi na yinane (18) yi batu abamaviku na ndaghu ndeki adjimarakughe o Siluwé, batu beni bamabe bavyoghulile bise Serusaleme djotsu uvaghe mabi?
LUK 13:5 Nesi, nyidulubusi: payi dughakaluse mitsanu myenu, dufu nane djowu.»
LUK 13:6 Djesu akebabukile nongu édjidji rye: «Umabe mutu amabe na mumange wuvaru o nungi andi. Akewende yilumbu mu uronde uyéboole mimange, tumbe misamabe.
LUK 13:7 Mbana, amavose na musatsi nungi rye: “Labati, bilime bike biryeru, nyiruyingi muyidokule mimange mu mumange éwuwu ngedili ne wumosi. Uwangi, wivayi fuyi mwenzili.”
LUK 13:8 Tumbe musalitsi akemuwaghule: “Fumu, lewusile yilime ayiyi, ngaghufutse byari byotsu na nyusobene butambe bweni na bu dibumbu.
LUK 13:9 Tangudji, wubure yilime ayiruyi. Payi wughabure, tukewuwaange.”»
LUK 13:10 Mu yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, Djesu amalonzaange musamu wu Nzambi o ghari ndaghu wowu dusambu.
LUK 13:11 Vane, vamabe mughetu wumaveghu bubomfi na yinyuni yibi mu dighumi na yinane (18) yi bilime. Amabelaange ngodju djimabe djimughorighe, asamabwérungulaange usimbughe.
LUK 13:12 Na Djesu emulabi, akemunengile, akemutsingule rye: «Mame, bubomfi bwaghu bumaghusulu.»
LUK 13:13 Akemusakighe makake. Vane-vane, nzime djikesungeme na akedodise Nzambi.
LUK 13:14 Tumbe yivunde yi ndaghu eni dusambu akenyoghe, mumbari Djesu amabeluse mutu mu yilumbu yowu yuvume. Akevose na yinombu rye: «Vadji bilumbu bisyamunu byusalile, kaboghu rughenganu bilumbu byébine mu yibelusu. Payi yilumbu yuvume tsatsabi, duyabwérughaange.»
LUK 13:15 Fumu anomuwulu, akemuwaghule: «Bapende nane djenu! Mu yilumbu yuvume, vagha mutu va ghari enu enyanguli ngombi vo buru andi mu umubeghe oghunu mambe mu yilumbu yeni?
LUK 13:16 Mughetu éwuwu, mwane Aberaame awu Dyabu amatsoyise mu dighumi na yinane (18) yi bilime mbé aghapatulu va makake mandi mu yilumbu yuvume?»
LUK 13:17 Djesu na evosi nane, bambeni bandi bakebase na yisoni. Yinombu yotsu yikesaghaange dibandu mambu amaboti maneni ame Djesu amadughusungu.
LUK 13:18 Djesu akebwévose: «Bukaghe bu Nzambi na yi bubaghunu? Na yime yi nyububaghusunu?
LUK 13:19 Bubaghunu na tsangu gheyi mutu eyekuke mu nungi andi. Ave djibendili, djipalisi mwiri wuneni wuvu na matayi na batsoli beyirunge muve mowu.»
LUK 13:20 Djesu akebwele uvose rye: «Na yi nyubaghusunu Bukaghe bu Nzambi?
LUK 13:21 Bubaghunu na yifunise ayi mughetu ebongi, akesobene mu ditingi di maghumi mabedji na byetsu biranu bi fufu mu ufunise pate-mape djotsu.»
LUK 13:22 Ave Djesu amabile mu nzile mu wende o Serusaleme, akenesikemange mu misyengi na mu mimbu mu yenelongaange musamu Nzambi.
LUK 13:23 Ave amenewendilaange, mutu wumosi akemuwivule bwena «Fumu, yike bu mwa pesu batu aboghobulu?» Djesu akebawaghule:
LUK 13:24 «Vovenanu mu ukote, va mune ndaghu awubandene. Mumbari nyidutsinguli, bapwele boronde ukote, tumbe baghorungule.
LUK 13:25 Ave Fumu ndaghu orelimine, mudibighe mune ndaghu, djenu adube o dulombili, dudukise mu yabutsu novose rye: “Fumu tudibulili.” Oduwaghule rye: “Ngedjabi awudwiruyisini!”
LUK 13:26 Mbana dumutsingule rye: “Djetu tumadji na tumanu va mosi naghu, na wumenelonzaange musamu mu manzile ma misyengi myetu.”
LUK 13:27 Obwébawaghule rye: “Ngédjabi odwiruyisini. Ndundyanu, ghusughanu vane djenu botsu bavayitsi ba mabi!”
LUK 13:28 Dulile na dughénighe minu ave dulabile Aberaame, Yisaake, Sakobe na babiyitsi botsu o Bukaghe bu Nzambi, mbana djenu dubwaghu o dulombili!
LUK 13:29 Batu borusenaange tandu na bande, o wisi epalili, no wisi eputumini. Botsane va mosi va mulambu o Bukaghe bu Nzambi.
LUK 13:30 Kaboghu,
LUK 13:31 Va djulu vane, baFarisi bamarughe mu uyilubuse Djesu rye: «Rambughe na wusughe vave, mumbari Yirode erondi ughuboke.»
LUK 13:32 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Wendanu, yetsingulanu yitsalele yéyine: “Nyisanzi bayisi, na nyibelusi bibedu na muni na mughese, mu yilumbu ayimuryeru nyumane yisalu.”
LUK 13:33 Tumbe, ubongile na muni, mughese na mune-mosi nyuyenewende, mumbari digha diwelimine yiri mubiyitsi akefwile yari yisusu patsi o Serusaleme.
LUK 13:34 Serusaleme, djenu bise Serusaleme, dwiboki babiyitsi na dwitindi mamani ombu bobésindughu ombu wenu. Kumbu kweni mbé nyironde udughukighe mu dughumbe nane koku eghukiyili noghumbe baane bandi otsi mapapi mandi, tumbe dusamagharu.
LUK 13:35 Kaboghu, ndaghu enu djusyale mududu. Tumbe dughobwéndabe tena duvose yiri “Nzambi apuyili myule ombu djandi oyiruyili mu dine di Fumu!”»
LUK 14:1 Mu yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, Djesu amakote o ndaghu yivunde yimosi yi baFarisi mu uyédji nandi. Botsu vane bamabe liyiyi mu ulabe adi Djesu ovaghe.
LUK 14:2 Vane, vamabe mutu amabe na matindi.
LUK 14:3 Djesu amabande uvose na akewivule milonzi mi mighaghe na baFarisi: «Divu diwelimine mu mughaghe Moyise, nine vo nesi, ubeluse mutu mu yilumbu yuvume?»
LUK 14:4 Basamamuwaghule, bakebe «swii». Kaboghu Djesu akeghelughe nobembe yibedu, akemubeluse mbana akemutsingule yiri yenewende o ndaghu andi.
LUK 14:5 Mbana akeghelughe ombu bobamamutsunaange, amabawivule: «Anyi va ghari enu, yike mwane andi vo ngombi andi ebonduyi o ghari yidune yilumbu yuvume, aghomupalise?»
LUK 14:6 Na djowu basamarungule umuwaghule.
LUK 14:7 Anolabe yiri botsu bamanengulu o mulambu, bamasolaange bitsighe biteghe bi bundumbe, amavose nongu édjidji:
LUK 14:8 «Yike mutu ewunengili o mulambu diwele, wuyatsutsile uyétsane o yitsighe yiteghe. Tangudji, va ghari botsu abamanengulu vakirughe mutu awu wuvyoghe dighobe,
LUK 14:9 na omadunengile djenu botsu babedji, yike eruyi mu wutsingule rye: “Muvyosi va yitsighe yaghu!” Ghureleme na yisonyi mu wende o yitsighe ayisuke o nzime.
LUK 14:10 Nesi, payi unengulu, léwende o yitsighe ayinzime. Mbana omadunengile, ave okotile, oghutsingule rye: “Mbatsi ami, rughe va yitsighe ayi bwedji wunu wusu.” Avane, wube na dighobe va ghari botsu abavu vane.
LUK 14:11 Nine,
LUK 14:12 Djesu amamwévose na awu amamunengile: «Payi wiveyi mulambu wu mwangulu vo wu tsisighe, uyanengile bambatsi baghu, baane ba ngudji baghu, biburu byaghu vo bisine abibambene naghu. Yike wivayi nane, djowu wandi borungule uwunengile na uwughabusile diboti adiwumabavaghe.
LUK 14:13 Nesi, payi wiveyi mulambu, nengile bidjaghe, bibomfi, bimbolutu na bidunge.
LUK 14:14 Yike wivayi nane, wulabe nzangu mba ngenze, batu bebane baghorungule uwughabusile. Byonyi byuwughabusulu vo Nzambi orambusile bo basungeme o dufu.»
LUK 14:15 Mu dyoni, mutu mosi amabe va tavule amavosile Djesu rye: «Ubwedji ombu mutu owudji mulambu o Bukaghe bu Nzambi!»
LUK 14:16 Djesu amamuwaghule na nongu édjidji rye: «Vamabe yilumbu, mutu wumosi amavaghe mulambu wuneni. Akenengile batu bapwele.
LUK 14:17 Diweru dyudji dinotole, akesindighe musatsi andi uyenengile bo mbé boyidji: “Tsyérughyanu, byotsu bimakunzeme!”
LUK 14:18 Tumbe botsu abane, bamavonde kokolu mumbari bamabe na bibinde. Awuteghe akemutsingule rye: “Nyitsisumbe nungi, nyileyedjilabe. Wuyanzyembe, kokolu tsyaghu.”
LUK 14:19 Wumosi akevose rye: “Nyibenodile dighumi di ngombi, nyileyetsi wétsighe, tandi.”
LUK 14:20 Wumosi wandi akemwévose: “Menu nyibonowele mughatsi ami, kaboghu ngodile temu.”
LUK 14:21 Vo musatsi amaghabuyile ombu yivunde yandi, amamutsingule bibinde byotsu bamamuveghe. Fumu ndaghu amanyoghe kabu na amavose na musatsi rye: Lenge! Wende mu mbure tsi mughungi na mu mimbambe mi musyengi na beghe bidjaghe, bibomfi, bidunge na bimbolutu!
LUK 14:22 Mu mwa pesu temu, musatsi amarughe na amamutsingule rye: “Fumu, nyimavaghe nane wutsinzingulile, tumbe vakisyale mambure.”
LUK 14:23 Kaboghu fumu andi akemutsingule rye: “Wende mu manzile, mu mighule bivaghe, ghome batu yi borughe mumba ndaghu ami djikebase.
LUK 14:24 Mbana nyighutsinguli, vagha mutu ne wumosi mu bo bamarele unengulu, baghobwémimbe mulambu éwuwu!”»
LUK 14:25 Binombu bineni bimawenda konge na Djesu. Amaghelughe nzime na amabitsingule rye:
LUK 14:26 «Payi mutu erondi unduke, aletonde pwele wuvyolile uronde tadji andi, ngudji andi, mughatsi andi, baane bandi, baane ba ngudji bandi, babaale vo baghetu, ne monyu andi. Patsi nane, aghorunguse ube mudukitsi ami.
LUK 14:27 Na wotsu aghonangule kurusu andi mu unduke, aghobe mudukitsi ami.
LUK 14:28 Payi mutu ane ditase dyurunge ndaghu ndeki, eletsane mu djabe durangu du mbongu na bisalulu nolabe yiri orungule umane.
LUK 14:29 Ave obandile usale yibughe payi aghamwérunguse udjimane, bobamamulabe ubande urunge, bomusyembaange,
LUK 14:30 novose rye: “Mutu éwuwu amabande urunge ndaghu na aghamwédjimanisile!”»
LUK 14:31 Na Djesu akebwévose rye: «Kaghe nyi, payi otoghe divite na kaghe susu, aghéletsane mu kelule yiri na dighumi di tosini baghore obenze uyébengusunu oyiruyi mu yimutoyise na maghumi mabedji ma tosini baghore?
LUK 14:32 Payi aghaane mangolu mawelimine, otinde bilumbi mu uvonde duvotsu pa kaghe eni akivale!
LUK 14:33 Kaboghu munongu mosi, wotsu aghorungule usile maboti mandi motsu, agha awelimine ube mudukitsi ami.»
LUK 14:34 Djesu akebwévose rye: «Musayi yime yiboti, tumbe payi musayi wumasambughe, yike yi yubwémughabusile mughangu?
LUK 14:35 Asane yisalu mu butambe vo o dibumbu, yike ubwaghu o dulombili. Wotsu avu na matudji limbaa, awulu!»
LUK 15:1 Babolitsi ba lepu na bavayitsi ba mabi bamabambene na Djesu mu uyéwulu malongi mandi.
LUK 15:2 BaFarisi na Milonzi mi mighaghe bamavosaange ba fundu rye: «Mutu éwuwu akegharungu udji va mosi na bango mabi!»
LUK 15:3 Tumbe, Djesu akebabukile nongu édjidji rye:
LUK 15:4 «Anyi va ghari enu, avu na kame bindombu, na akitsyemuse yimosi, aghesili maghumi-dufu na yifu (99) yi bindombu mu kumu, mu uyenerombe ayitsitsyemughe tena vo oyilabile?
LUK 15:5 Ave eyilabili, ebasi na nzangu, eyinanguli no yisunze va masambeke.
LUK 15:6 Anotole o ndaghu andi, akenengili bambatsi bandi na botsu ababambene nandi novose rye: “Rughanu, tusayanu: yindombu yami ayi mbé yimatsyemughe, yimalabene.”
LUK 15:7 Divu munongu mosi o djulu, ave muvayitsi mabi wumosi ekaluyili mutsanu, nzangu neni djibi o djulu uvyoghulile adji maghumi-dufu na yifu (99) yi batu basungeme abasane nzale ukalughe mutsanu.»
LUK 15:8 Djesu amamwébabukile nongu: «Payi mughetu ane dighumi di doli, yike etsyemusi dumosi, yi ovaghe? Obanze paghe, oghombule ndaghu, odurombe yari na yari tena odulabe.
LUK 15:9 Yike edulabi, enengili bambatsi bandi ababambene nandi nobatsingule rye: “Rughanu, tusayanu, doli dwami adu mbé dumatsyemughe, nyimadulabe.”
LUK 15:10 Munongu wumosi nyidutsinguli bwena: nzangu neni djibi ombu byanze bi Nzambi ave muvayitsi wumosi wu mabi ekaluyili mutsanu.»
LUK 15:11 Djesu amamwébabukile nongu mosi rye: «Vamabe dibaale dimabe na baane babedji ba babaale,
LUK 15:12 Awu ngebi amavose na tadji andi rye: “Tate, peyi dyami dikabu di disyale.” Tadji akebaghabile maboti mandi.
LUK 15:13 Bilumbu binovyoghe, ngebi akesumbise byandi byotsu, akenewende na mbongu tsyandi o malongu ma vale. Aghune, akenyambesene mbongu tsyandi tsyotsu mu monyu dimbunge.
LUK 15:14 Anonyambesene byotsu, dungosu du nzale dukabe o bulongu bweni na akebande ulabe maghughe na asamamwébe na ayi udji.
LUK 15:15 Akewende oyevonde dibaale di mwise bulongu bweni bisalu. Tumbe dibaale dyeni, akemutinde o masaku o wumabe yivange yandi yi bangulu mu ubakelisaange.
LUK 15:16 Djandi amarondaange ne udji bipupu bi bighudji bamaveghaange bangulu, tumbe vasamabe mutu amamugharusu.
LUK 15:17 Amabande urangimine na amavose rye: “Basatsi ba tate bedji bighudji usyalulu, mbana menu wunu utopulu nyi topulu na nzale.
LUK 15:18 Nyughabughe ombu tate na nyumutsingule rye Tate, nyimavaghe disumu va wusu Nzambi na va wusu awu.
LUK 15:19 Nyisa nyiwelimine wunengulu mwane aghu, tumbe mbongi na nane musalitsi aghu.”
LUK 15:20 Amareleme noghabughe ombu tadji andi. Tadji andi anomulabile, ne nane mbé akivale, akebase na yingebe. Akewende mbangu na nzangu mu uyémubumbe mu kingu.
LUK 15:21 Vane-vane, mwane akevose rye: “Tate, nyimavaghe disumu va wusu Nzambi na va wusu aghu. Nyisa nyiwelimine unengulu mwane aghu.”
LUK 15:22 Tumbe tadji akevose na basatsi bandi rye: “Lenganu nobeghe bikutu bi dufunu, mudwisyanu, muvakighyanu moru nomudwise bapondu.
LUK 15:23 Beghanu ngombi adjivonge, djibokyanu, lambanu, tudjanu na tusayanu,
LUK 15:24 mumbari mwane ami wuwu mbé amafu, amaghabughe monyu; mbé amatsyemughe, amalabene.” Bakebande usaghe.
LUK 15:25 Yivunde amabe o manungi. Ave amaghabuyile, anotole bebeli na ndaghu, amawulu nduku bisighu na miyinu.
LUK 15:26 Amanengile musatsi wumosi, amamuwivule dyambu adivyoyi.
LUK 15:27 Musatsi eni amamuwaghule rye: “Mwane ngudji aghu amaghabughe. Tadji aghu atsirume uboke ngombi djivonge, mumbari ngebi awu atsighabughe polu.”
LUK 15:28 Yivunde akebase na kabu, akebuse ukote o ndaghu. Tadji akepale, akeyemulende akekote.
LUK 15:29 Tumbe yivunde akewaghule tadji andi rye: “Labati, pwele bilime nyighusalili, ngekikuli ne dirume dyaghu dimosi. Ukapeghaange ne mwa tabe ‘vyaa’ nyikesaghe na bambatsi bami.
LUK 15:30 Tumbe mwane awu aghabuyilaange, djandi omadji maboti maghu na bimbembu, tsya djandi wumabokile ngombi adjivonge!”
LUK 15:31 Tadji akemuwaghule: “Aa! Ndewandi mwane ami, wudji nami temu djotsu, byotsu abivu nami, abyaghu wandi.
LUK 15:32 Kaboghu diwelimine yiri tudjanu nosaghe va mosi, mumbari mwane ngudji aghu:
LUK 16:1 Djesu etsinguli badukitsi bandi rye: «Yisine yimosi amabe na musatsi wumabe yivunde yi basatsi botsu. Batu bakemufunde bwena: “Musatsi aghu ebungi nonyambesene maboti maghu.”
LUK 16:2 Fumu maboti akenengile musatsi eni, akemuwivule yiri: “Yi nyiwulu bévosili mu ndedju? Nzinguli nane wikelisili maboti mami mumbari wughobwémakelise.”
LUK 16:3 Musatsi eni, akekéwivulaange: “Yivunde yami aghébwéronde yiri ngakelise maboti mandi. Yike tsyeni nyuvayile? Nyivayi manungi, ngaane mangolu; nyibi mu uvonde, nyube na yisoni.
LUK 16:4 Kaboghu nyimadjabe adi nyikivaghe ave nyikighusululu mu bisalu, mu udilu na batu nami mu mandaghu mowu.”
LUK 16:5 Musatsi eni amanengile mutu-mutu omabe na mughanu. Akewivule awuteghe: “Kweni winwani Fumu ami?”
LUK 16:6 Djandi akemuwake rye: “Kame mireghe mi matsi.” Musatsi akemutsingule: “La mughande, lenge utsane na rende maghumi maranu.”
LUK 16:7 Akebwéwivule wumosi wandi: “Ka ndedju, kweni winwani?” Dibaale dyeni akemuwake: “Kame saku tsi bighudji.” Musatsi akemutsingule: “La mughande, rende maghumi-dunana (80).”
LUK 16:8 Kaboghu, fumu maboti akesingisile musatsi eni yifutsi mu dyele adi djandi amadile. Labatyanu nane batu ba bulongu bwébubu babile na mele maneni, wuvyoghulile ne baane ba yidjalale.»
LUK 16:9 Djesu akebwese rye: «Nyidutsinguli, salisanu busine bwenu na mbongu tsi mfurulu, mu udile bambatsi, mumbari ave busukile, dudilu mu mandaghu ma Nzambi.
LUK 16:10 Odjivu awelimine udughusu mambu amagheyi na musighe, awelimine wandi udughusu amaneni. Djandi oyifuri vo udyonge mu mambu magheyi, ofure na udyonge wandi mu mambu amaneni.
LUK 16:11 Payi dusamabe dusigheme mu busine bu mfurulu, anyi oduveghe busine abu ngenze?
LUK 16:12 Na payi dusamabe dusungeme mu maboti ma ngane, anyi oduveghe maboti amajenu beni?
LUK 16:13 Vagha mutu orungule usalile fumu bedji: ovine wumosi, akeronde wune, vo oghobise wumosi na akelenze wune. Kaboghu, dughorungule usalile Nzambi nosalile mbongu va mosi.»
LUK 16:14 BaFarisi, na nzale mbongu, banowulu motsu ame Djesu amavosaange, bakemupedjingi.
LUK 16:15 Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Djenu dudji batu békelase yiri basungeme va wusu batu nenu, tumbe Nzambi edjabi mirime myenu. Motsu, ame bédodisi va misu ma batu, madji nzoruru va wusu Nzambi.
LUK 16:16 Mughaghe Moyise na mughande babiyitsi mimabe vane tena San-Batise. Ubandile va temu San-Batise, musamu wuboti wu Bukaghe bu Nzambi wisamunu. Mutu-mutu oghaghene mu uyékote wune.
LUK 16:17 Djulu na butambe byurungule utsyemughe mbangu-mbangu, tumbe ne yirendu yimosi mu mughaghe yighorungule utsyemughe.
LUK 16:18 Dibaale dyotsu adisanzi mughatsi andi na eweli wususu, etubi bukali. Mbana, wotsu eweli mughetu wusanzu na mulumi andi, djawandi etubi bukali.»
LUK 16:19 «Vamabe yisine yimadwaraange bikutu bi dufunu duneni. Bilumbu bi monyu andi wotsu, amabangaange mu nzangu, mumbari amabe na busine buvyoghulile.
LUK 16:20 Vamabe wandi yidjaghe dine dyandi Lasare, amabe na mapure. Batu bakimusunzaange kale yilumbu va mune ndaghu yisine yeni.
LUK 16:21 Lasare, amarondaange ubole nodji bikukuku abimabondughaange va tavule yisine. Tumbe bamondi bamayivendaange mapure mandi.
LUK 16:22 Mwa yilumbu, yidjaghe akefu, akebeghu na byanze va tulu Aberaame. Yisine wandi akefu, bakemutsighe.
LUK 16:23 Aghune bulungi bu mudji, yisine amatsoghaange pwele. O vale, amabilile Lasare va tulu Aberaame.
LUK 16:24 Wune disimu dimosi, yisine akeghamughe rye: “Tate ami Aberaame, nda ngebe. Sindighe Lasare aputiyi kodu mulembu andi mu mambe na andekisi diberi va dulimi, mumbari ngorungule wuwarile ditsoghe adidi o ghari mudji éwuwu.”
LUK 16:25 Tumbe Aberaame akemuwaghule rye: “Mwane ami, rangimine monyu aghu, wumabe mu maboti na maboti, mbana Lasare djandi amabe mu maghughe. Tumbe aghunu, Lasare yike wubembughu, ebembughu, mbana ndedju, temu awumaghughe djimatole.
LUK 16:26 Va ghari djetu nenu vadji mbengi neni, mumbari djenu aduvu wune, dughorungule usabughe awutuvu. Djetu wandi, tughorungule wusabughe awuduvu.”
LUK 16:27 Yisine akemutsingule bwena: “Tate Aberaame kokolu nyighulendi, kaboghu sindighe Lasare o ndaghu tadji ami.
LUK 16:28 Mumbari nyine baane ba ngudji baranu ba babaale. Lasare awendi mu uyébalubuse yiri bakérughe djowu wandi o mbure adjidji dji maghughe.”
LUK 16:29 Aberaame akemuwaghule rye: “Baane ba ngudji baghu bane musamu wu Moyise na awu babiyitsi awibalubusi, kaboghu bawughulu nowutsiyise!”
LUK 16:30 Yisine akemuwake rye: “Nesi tate Aberaame tsinane. Mutu awu mbé wumafu, awendi ombu wowu, ayebatsingule, tangudji bokalughe mutsanu.”
LUK 16:31 Aberaame akemutsingule djawandi rye: “Payi djowu baghagharu uwulu mambu ma Moyise na ma babiyitsi, baghogharu uwulu wandi musamu ne ame djandi omarambughe o dufu.”»
LUK 17:1 Djesu amatsingule badukitsi bandi rye: «Vobangaange mambu amorobisaange batu uvaghe mabi. Kamune maghughe-ma, ombu mutu owurombise bambatsi uvaghe mabi!
LUK 17:2 Mutu eni, yike erombisi ne ngebi mosi uvaghe mabi, mbé dyuwelimine mu djandi bakemutunge dimani dineni mu kingu nomubwaghe o mubu.
LUK 17:3 Kebenanu, payi mwane tadji aghu evayi dibi, mughabusi mu nzile. Na yike edinyongi, mutandi.
LUK 17:4 Payi eghuvayili dibi yisambwali yi kumbu mu yilumbu, na yikéghabuyi yisambwali yi kumbu wandi mu uyuvonde kokolu, mutandi.»
LUK 17:5 Bilumbi bimatsingule Fumu rye: «Warise yitu yetu mu Nzambi.»
LUK 17:6 Fumu akewaghule: «Payi yitu yenu yibaghunu na tsangu tsigheyi, durungule urume mwiri éwuwu yiri “kerubule, yekevare o mubu”, na wududedile.»
LUK 17:7 «Anyi, va ghari enu avu na musatsi, wivayi manungi vo wukelise bindombu, ave djandi eruyili o manungi, mu temu eni, akemutsingule rye: “Rughe, tsane na djange”?
LUK 17:8 Vyaaghe, dumutsingule yiri: “Léndambile bighudji, mbana yevinze bikutu, yinzunzile bighudji ngadji, nganu. Avane wusu, ndewandi wudji na wunu.”
LUK 17:9 Dusingisile musatsi mumbari atsisale byotsu abidutsimurume?
LUK 17:10 Munongu mosi nenu. Ave dwidughusulu motsu ame bédurumi, vosanu rye: “Djetu, tudji basatsi abaghékelisi dusingusulu, mumbari twidughusu yike yisalu ayimaturumu.”»
LUK 17:11 Ave Djesu amawendilaange o Serusaleme, amavyolaange va ndilu Samari na Ngalile.
LUK 17:12 Ave amatolile va dimbu dimosi, dighumi di bibedu bi nyámbi dimamubengusunu tumbe, basamabambene nandi.
LUK 17:13 Na bibedu byeni bikeghamughe rye: «Djesu, Fumu, tulabi wandi yingebe!»
LUK 17:14 Ave Djesu amabalabile, akebatsingule rye: «Wendanu, yekelasanu menu ombu bavaghulitsi ba paghu.» Ave bamayene wendilaange, mu nzile bamabelughe.
LUK 17:15 Wumosi va ghari owu, anolabe bwena amabelughe, akeghabusile mu nzile adji amavyole, akenedodisaange Nzambi na mighamu.
LUK 17:16 Akeghudume va wusu Djesu, mbami na tsi, na akemughabusile diboti. Mutu eni amabe mwise Samari.
LUK 17:17 Djesu akemuwivule: «Dighumi dyotsu ditsibelusu. Ka yifu yi bane yike wuka?
LUK 17:18 Mu djowu botsu, yike mweni éwuwu awutsidjabe uyighabusile diboti ombu Nzambi?»
LUK 17:19 Mbanane Djesu akemutsingule rye: «Releme, wendange, yitu yaghu yimaghughobule.»
LUK 17:20 BaFarisi bakewivule Djesu rye: «Temu yi, Nzambi obandile ulase bukaghe bwandi va ghari mukute andi?» Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Bukaghe bu Nzambi bughorughe nane yime ayulabene na misu.
LUK 17:21 Baghovose bwena: “Budji vave vo budji wuna”. Tumbe djabanu yiri na muni, Bukaghe bu Nzambi bumakote mu mirime myenu.»
LUK 17:22 Mbana Djesu aketsingule badukitsi bandi rye: «Mu bilumbu abyurughe, dube na nzale ulabe ne yilumbu yimosi yi Mwane Mutu, tumbe ne vane, dughoyilabe.
LUK 17:23 Ave batu bodutsingulilaange rye: “Adji vave!” Vo: “Adji wuna!” Duyabawulu, duyabaduke.
LUK 17:24 Kaboghu, yilumbu ayi Mwane Mutu oruyile, yube nane yivevedi yi kaki. Osundile ulabene, na yidjalale yandi yubase djulu djotsu kodu na kodu.
LUK 17:25 Tumbe, diwelimine yiri Mwane Mutu oletsoghusu pwele, na obusu na batu ba temu édjidji.
LUK 17:26 Adimalabene mu temu Nowe, dyumwébe munongu mosi mu yilumbu ayi Mwane Mutu oruyile.
LUK 17:27 Batu bamadjangaange, bamanwangaange, bamawelesenaange na bamawetsaange baane bowu tena yilumbu ayi Nowe amakotile mu bwatu buneni. Mvule mutsoghu djikenoghe, nidu djineni djikerughe na botsu abamasyale bakefu.
LUK 17:28 Yilumbu yi durughulu du Mwane Mutu, yumwébe munongu mosi nane va temu Lote mwise Sodome. Batu bamadjangaange na bamanwangaange; bamasumbaange na bamasumbisaange; bamavaraange na bamarungisaange.
LUK 17:29 Tumbe yilumbu ayi Lote amaghusuyile musyengi Sodome, Nzambi akenoyise mvule maghaghele ma mudji na batu botsu bakefu.
LUK 17:30 Dyoni dyube munongu mosi mu yilumbu ayi Mwane Mutu olabenine.
LUK 17:31 Mu temu eni, diwelimine yiri mutu wotsu owube o djulu ndaghu andi, ayasundughe mu uyébonge bime byandi o ghari ndaghu. Munongu mosi ombu mutu owube o manungi, kilikingi ayaghabughe o dimbu.
LUK 17:32 Rangiminanu mughatsi Lote!
LUK 17:33 Wotsu owuronde ughaghe monyu andi, owuvinde; tumbe owughutsyemuse, owudile.
LUK 17:34 Nyidutsinguli, mukolu eni, batu babedji bobe va tangi: wumosi obongu, awune osilu.
LUK 17:35 Baghetu babedji borokaange va mosi, wumosi obongu, awune osilu. [
LUK 17:36 Babaale babedji abobe o ghari nungi, wumosi obongu, awune osilu.]»
LUK 17:37 Badukitsi bakewivule Djesu rye: «Fumu, dyoni mbure yi dyuvyoyile?» Djesu akebawaghule rye:
LUK 18:1 Djesu amababukile nongu mu ubalase bwena bosambilaange na yikanane na baghodede.
LUK 18:2 Akebatsingule rye: «Vamabe nzonzi va musyengi, asamadumange Nzambi na asamaghobisaange mutu wotsu.
LUK 18:3 Mune musyengi eni, wumabe mukwili wumawendaange kadi yilumbu ombu nzonzi eni mu uyemutsotsaange rye: “Tabulili bunzonzi va ghari menu na bavinitsi bami.”
LUK 18:4 Vane kale, amalebusaange. Anokelonge, amavose rye: “Nénane ngédumi Nzambi na ngeghobisi mutu,
LUK 18:5 mu yiswebiri yi mukwili ewune, nyumutabulile bunzonzi mumbari akébwéyikomise muru.”»
LUK 18:6 Fumu akebwévose rye: «Ghulwatyanu adi nzonzi djibive amavose!
LUK 18:7 Tambusu na Nzambi, ovayile bunzonzi mu batu bandi abemulendi mu dusambu nyangu na mukolu! Tsiri nane? Ngenze, aghotsikedene mu ubawamuse.
LUK 18:8 Menu, nyidutsinguli, Nzambi obatabulile bunzonzi mbangu-mbangu. Tumbe ave Mwane Mutu oruyile, oyirasunu mwa dikabu di batu bavu na yitu va butambe?»
LUK 18:9 Djesu akemwébuke nongu ombu batu abekélabe bwena basungeme na belenzi basusu, akevose rye:
LUK 18:10 «Babaale babedji bamakote o ghari ndaghu Nzambi mu uyésambile. Wumosi amabe muFarisi, awune mubolitsi lepu.
LUK 18:11 MuFarisi, ave amasambililaange diteli, akebwaghaange mitsoki rye: “Tate Nzambi, nyiwughabusili diboti mumbari ngaa nane batu bamosi bavu badayi, bafutsi, bimbembu, vo nane mubolitsi éwuwu wu lepu.
LUK 18:12 Mu uwughobise, nyiwarili nzale nyongu bedji mu tsone, nyiwuveyingi yimosi mu dighumi yi maboti mami motsu.”
LUK 18:13 Kaboghu mubolitsi lepu anobe diteli, va mughule, asamarungusaange ne unangule misu na djulu, tumbe akedumange tulu andi na akevosaange rye: “Tate Nzambi ndabi ngebe muvayitsi mabi nane menu.”»
LUK 18:14 Djesu akemwévose rye: «Nine, nyidutsinguli, yotsu mubolitsi lepu eghabuyili o ndaghu andi, Nzambi amamutande nomusungighe, wuvenguse muFarisi.
LUK 18:15 Batu wandi bakebeghange baane bakali ombu Djesu mumbari akebasakighaange makake. Badukitsi bandi, banolabe nane, bakenyangilaange batu beni.
LUK 18:16 Djesu amanengile baane beni va mughule andi na akevose bwena: «Silanu baane urughe ombu ami na duyabaghandise, mumbari Bukaghe bu Nzambi, budji mu batu ababaghunu nowu.
LUK 18:17 Dingenze nyidutsinguli, wotsu aghodile Bukaghe bu Nzambi nane mwane ngebi, aghokote wune “vyaa”.»
LUK 18:18 Yivunde yimosi yi baSwife, yike wivule Djesu rye: «Mulonzi wuboti, tsyeni nyuvayile mu udile monyu mutubu?»
LUK 18:19 Djesu akemuwaghule rye: «Dibandu yi windengilili “Muboti”? Vagha mutu aboti, wuvengutse Nzambi pinze.
LUK 18:20 Widjabi marume ma Nzambi: “Wuyatube bukali, wuyaboke, wuyadaghe, wuyafurile mutu naghu dyambu. Ghobise tadji na ngudji aghu.”»
LUK 18:21 Yivunde yeni yi baSwife yikewaghule Djesu rye: «Ubongile bungebi bwami, dedi na vave nyikevu yivunde, nyighobisi mambu motsu.»
LUK 18:22 Djesu anomuwulu, akemuwaghule rye: «Vaki dyambu dimosi diwusyali udughusu: byotsu abivu naghu, bisumbisi, ghaabile bidjaghe mbongu na Nzambi owuveghe busine o djulu, mbana rughe, nduki.»
LUK 18:23 Dibaale dyeni, anowulu mambu meni, aketsore manyuru, mumbari amabe yisine yineni.
LUK 18:24 Djesu, anomulabe yiri amatsore manyuru, akevose rye: «Divure ombu djowu abavu na maboti mapwele mu ukote o Bukaghe bu Nzambi!
LUK 18:25 Nine, disavure ombu tsungu mu uvyoyile va dighole di tsongi; diweru dineni ombu yisine mu ukote mu Bukaghe bu Nzambi.»
LUK 18:26 Batu abamamuwulu, bamamuwivule rye: «Kaboghu, yike nyi, orungulu ughobulu?»
LUK 18:27 Djesu amabawaghule rye: «Adivu divure ombu batu, dighaa divure ombu Nzambi.»
LUK 18:28 Pyere akevose rye: «Labati, djetu, tumasile byotsu na tumawuduke.»
LUK 18:29 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Dingenze, nyidutsinguli, mutu wotsu, aghorungule usile ndaghu andi, mughatsi na baane bandi, baane ba ngudji bandi na biburu byandi byotsu dibandu Bukaghe bu Nzambi,
LUK 18:30 yi aghodile bipwele mu temu édjidji, na monyu mutubu mu temu adjiruyi.»
LUK 18:31 Djesu anonengile dighumi na badukitsi bandi babedji (12) va mughule andi, akebatsingule rye: «Wulwanu, o Serusaleme twiwendyanu, aghune motsu moyedughusu, ame babiyitsi bamarende mu dyambu di Mwane Mutu.
LUK 18:32 Djandi, owakusu va makake ma djowu abaghédjabi Nzambi. Batu beni, bomudese, bomusyenge na bomufute matedji.
LUK 18:33 Yikebemani wumudimbe na mikase mi batsilu, bomuboke. Mbana, mu yilumbu ayimuryeru, orambughe o dufu.»
LUK 18:34 Tumbe badukitsi basamawulu ne dimosi mu mambu ame Djesu amavosaange. Payi basamawulu, mumbari divindughulu dimabasweghu.
LUK 18:35 Djesu anobe bebeli na Seriku, vamabe yidunge yitsane va mughulu nzile yimabe muvondi.
LUK 18:36 Yidunge yeni anowulu nduku yinombu yi batu bamavyoghaange, amabawivule rye: «Yine yi? Dyambu yi?»
LUK 18:37 Batu bakemuwaghule rye: «Djesu mwise Nasarete evyoyi.»
LUK 18:38 Na djandi amaghamughe: «Djesu, mwane Davide, ndabi wandi yingebe!»
LUK 18:39 Batu abamavyoghaange va wusu andi, bakemughubisaange: Aa vole! Tumbe yidunge yeni akebwébwelaange ughamughe na mangolu: «Mwane Davide, ndabi wandi yingebe.»
LUK 18:40 Djesu, anosikeme, amarume rye: «Mumbeyilyanu.» Yidunge anobambene, Djesu akemuwivule rye:
LUK 18:41 «Yi wirondi ngawuvayile?» Djandi akemuwaghule rye: «Fumu, nyirondi ubwélabe nane va teghe.»
LUK 18:42 Djesu akemutsingule rye: «Tsyélabi! Yitu yaghu yimaghughobule.»
LUK 18:43 Sundila, misu ma yidunge make tyemune, na akeduke Djesu noyeneyitsange Nzambi. Batu botsu na bédilabi, djowandi bakeyitse Nzambi.
LUK 19:1 Djesu anokote o musyengi Seriku, akewunaange.
LUK 19:2 Va musyengi eni, vamabe dibaale, dine dyandi Sase; djandi amabe yivunde yi babolitsi ba lepu na amabe yisine.
LUK 19:3 Amarondaange ulabe na udjabe Djesu. Abilange aghufi, na yinombu yimabe yivyoghulile, asamarungule umulabe.
LUK 19:4 Sase, anolabe nane, akerele mbangu o wusu, akemate mu mwiri awumabe vane mughule nzile adji Djesu amavyoyilaange mu umulabe burange.
LUK 19:5 Ave Djesu amatolile va mbure eni, anonangule misu na djulu, akemulabe na akemutsingule rye: «Sase, lenge nosundughe! Na nyangu, yilatsi mu ndaghu aghu.»
LUK 19:6 Sase anosundughe maswasu, akedile Djesu na nzangu djotsu mu ndaghu andi.
LUK 19:7 Botsu abamadilabe, bamaningaange novose rye: «Mutu éwuwu amayekote novyose yilatsi o ndaghu muvayitsi mabi nane wune!»
LUK 19:8 Sase anoreleme va wusu Fumu, aketsingule rye: «Fumu, la yasi yi maboti mami, nyuyighabile bidjaghe. Payi nyimadyonge mutu, nyumuvanine kumbu djine.»
LUK 19:9 Djesu akewaghule rye: «Na muni, dughobutsu dumakote o ghari ndaghu édjidji, mumbari djawandi adji muteghule Aberaame.
LUK 19:10 Mwane Mutu amarughe mu uyirombe noghobule abatsyemughe.»
LUK 19:11 Abamabe vane, banowulu mambu meni, Djesu akebwele nongu mosi mumbari mbé ake bebeli na Serusaleme. Na batu beni bamatasaange yiri na mapape, Nzambi orughe mu uyibyatsu kaghe va ghari owu.
LUK 19:12 Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Dibaale dimosi di mukute awumabe na didume, amawende o bulongu bu vale bakeyémubyatse kaghe bulongu bwandi, mbana mbé oghabusile.
LUK 19:13 Ne akewende, akenengile dighumi di bidjeti byandi, akewakise kadi mutu dyandi dikabu di mbongu. Akebatsingule rye: “Salisanu mbongu tena nyughabughe.”
LUK 19:14 Bise bulongu bwandi, basamadironde, baketinde batu o nzime kodu mu uyemutsingule rye: “Djetu, tugherondi urumusu na kaghe nane djandi.”
LUK 19:15 Dibaale dyeni akebyatsu kaghe o bulongu bweni. Anoghabughe o mulingu andi, akenengile bidjeti byandi abe amawakise mbongu mu bawivule nane bamatsisalisile.
LUK 19:16 Yidjeti ayiteghe akebambene na akevose rye: “Fumu, wumapeghe yikuru yimosi yi mbongu, va djulu yoni, nyitsidile dighumi di bikuru.”
LUK 19:17 Kaghe eni, akemutsingule rye: “Diboti, wudji musatsi wungenze, wutsiwelemine mu mambu amagheyi, kaboghu nyuwubyatse mu dighumi di misyengi.”
LUK 19:18 Yidjeti ayi mubedji yike rughe, akevose rye: “Fumu, wumapeghe yikuru yimosi yi mbongu, va djulu yoni, nyitsidile bikuru biranu.”
LUK 19:19 Kaghe akemutsingule rye: “Ndedju, nyuwubyatse mu misyengi miranu.”
LUK 19:20 Yidjeti ayine yike rughe novose rye: “Fumu, la yikuru yaghu, nyimayisweghe va disite di tsande.
LUK 19:21 Nyimabe na ghome aghu, mumbari wudji mutu wurange: wibongi abi ndedju wughésunzi; wifuli abi ndedju wughévari.”
LUK 19:22 Kaghe akemutsingule rye: “Mu posulu ndebeni nyiwusosisi, musatsi mubi nane ndedju! Wumadjabaange yiri nyidji mutu wurange: nyibongi abi nyisamasunze na nyifuli abi nyisamavare.
LUK 19:23 Wumadjabe nane, mbé wumayesunze mbongu tsyami ombu bakoli, mbana ave mbé nyimaghabuyile, mbé nyimayitsibonge na bapite va djulu?”
LUK 19:24 Na aketsingule botsu abamabe vane rye: “Mupatulyanu yikuru ayivu nandi, na yiveyanu ombu djandi awavu na dighumi.”
LUK 19:25 Batu beni, bamasimine novose rye: “Fumu, ka djandi akane dighumi di bikuru!”
LUK 19:26 Kaghe akebawaghule rye: “Menu nyidutsinguli: mutu wotsu awuvu na yime, bomubwese; tumbe wotsu aghaane yime, bomupatule nesi mwa pesu adjivu nandi.
LUK 19:27 Tumbe bambeni bami abasamaronde yiri nyike byatsu nane kaghe owu, bambeyilyanu vave na batabulyanu bakingu va wusu ami.”»
LUK 19:28 Djesu anomane uvose, akerele va wusu na akemate o Serusaleme.
LUK 19:29 Ave amabambeninaange na mimbu ma Betefase na Betani, anobe bebeli na mukongu winengulu «mukongu wu miri mi Olive», akesindighe badukitsi bandi babedji na akebatsingule rye:
LUK 19:30 «Wendanu o dimbu adivu va wusu enu. Ave dutolile, durasune mwane yibulu atungu, awuskatsanunu na mutu. Munyangulyanu na mumbeyilyanu wunu.
LUK 19:31 Payi mutu atsiduwivule rye: “Mumbari yi dwimunyangulili?” Duke muwaghule rye: “Fumu ane nzale woni.”»
LUK 19:32 Djowu abasindughu bakewende, na bakerasunu byotsu nane Djesu amabatsingulile.
LUK 19:33 Ave bamanyangulilaange mwane yibulu yeni, ba fumu, bakebawivule rye: «Dibandu yi dwinyangulili mwane yibulu?»
LUK 19:34 Bakebawaghule rye: «Fumu ane nzale woni.»
LUK 19:35 Banobeghe yibulu yeni ombu Djesu, bakene walange bikutu byowu va djulu yibulu, na bakematise Djesu.
LUK 19:36 Ave Djesu amayene wendilaange, mu nzile djotsu, batu bakeyene walange bikutu byowu.
LUK 19:37 Mu temu eni Djesu amabe bebeli na ukote o Serusaleme. Amavindeminange adu mukongu miri mi baOlive, binombu bi batu na badukitsi bandi, mu nzangu adjimavyoghulile mu djowu, bakesaghange nododise Nzambi na mighamu mineni. Bamasaghaange, dibandu bimaghe bineni abi djowu bamalabe.
LUK 19:38 Mu duyitsu dwowu, bakevosange rye: «Nzambi aveyi myule ombu kaghe adjiruyi mu dine di Fumu! Duvotsu o djulu na bundumbe ombu Nzambi!»
LUK 19:39 Yinombu yi baFarisi yimabe mukonge, baketsingule Djesu rye: «Mulonzi, votse badukitsi baghu!»
LUK 19:40 Djesu akebawake rye: «Nyidutsinguli, payi djowu batsivole, mamani moghamughe mu uyitse Nzambi.»
LUK 19:41 Djesu na ebambini na musyengi Serusaleme, na ewulabilili, akelile.
LUK 19:42 Na akevose rye: «Serusaleme, nyinyongi mu ndedju, wusamadjabe nane mbé wumadilile duvotsu mu yilumbu yéyine, aa temu dji mavyoghe na dyoni dimawusweghu.
LUK 19:43 Kaboghu, mu bilumbu abyurughe, bambeni baghu borungise bivaghe mu mighule myaghu, bowutsyenge na bowubandesene yari na yari.
LUK 19:44 Bowunighe ndedju Serusaleme na batu baghu botsu. Mu ndedju, baghowusile ne dimani dimosi va djulu disusu, mumbari wusamakelule temu adji Nzambi mbé amawuwamusile.»
LUK 19:45 Djesu anokote o ghari yivaghe yi ndaghu Nzambi, akesanze bakoli.
LUK 19:46 Akebatsingule rye: «Bisonu bi Nzambi bivosi rye: Ndaghu ami djube ndaghu dusambu. Tumbe djenu dumadjikaluse yike yiswemunu yi bikongu.»
LUK 19:47 Bilumbu byotsu, Djesu akelonzaange va dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi. Bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, milonzi mi mighaghe na bivunde abimarumisaange mikute bakerombange tonu djubokile Djesu.
LUK 19:48 Tumbe, basamadile tonu, mumbari mukute wotsu wumabe limbaa, mu uwulu malongi mandi.
LUK 20:1 Mwa yilumbu, Djesu amalonzaange batu, akebatsingulaange musamu wuboti va dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi. Bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, milonzi mi mighaghe na bivunde bi baSwife bimosi bakebarasune vane.
LUK 20:2 Bivunde byeni bakemuwivule rye: «Awuni widilile musughe mu udughusu mambu mémane? Tutsinguli, anyi amawuveghe musughe ewune?»
LUK 20:3 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Menu wandi nyuduwivule yivu:
LUK 20:4 Anyi amasindighe San nomuveghe musughe wu ubatise batu? Amasindughu na Nzambi vo na batu?»
LUK 20:5 Batu beni, bakevosange va ghari djobeni rye: «Yike twisingi yiri Nzambi amamurume, djandi otuwivule rye: “Ka mumba yi dusamasingile ame San amavose?”
LUK 20:6 Yike twimuwaghuli yiri musughe eni ombu batu wiruyili, mukute wotsu wututinde mamani mu utuboke, mumbari batu beni bédjabi yiri San amabe mubiyitsi.»
LUK 20:7 Batu beni, bakewaghule Djesu rye: «Djetu, tughedjabi anyi amamuveghe musughe mu ubatise batu.»
LUK 20:8 Na Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Menu wandi, ngodutsingule mu musughe nyi nyimavayili.»
LUK 20:9 Djesu anomane uvose, akemwébukile mukute nongu rye: «Dibaale amavare nungi dji miri mi vinye, akedjisile va makake ma bisyele mu udjikelise, na amawende mu mulingu yitsingu.
LUK 20:10 Temu dighumbe djinotole, fumu nungi akesindighe musatsi andi wumosi ombu bisyele abimasyale na nungi, Bakemuveghe dyandi dikabu di milunde mi vinye. Tumbe bisyele byeni bakedimbe musatsi eni kube na bakemughabuse myowu pavele.
LUK 20:11 Fumu nungi, akesindighe awu mubedji, bisyele byeni bakedimbe wune wandi kube, bakemusyenge na bakemughabuse myowu na myowu.
LUK 20:12 Akebwésindighe awu mutatu, awune wandi, bakemutsungule na bakemusyanze.
LUK 20:13 Fumu nungi akekewivule: “Tsyeni ngavale? Nyusindighe mwane ami murime, tangudji bomughobise.”
LUK 20:14 Tumbe ave bisyele byeni bamalabile mwane andi, baketsingusunaange rye: “Lanu mungo disyale! Tumubokyanu, tuke byalile nungi.”
LUK 20:15 Bisyele, bakemughange, bakemupalise o ghari nungi na bakemuboke.» Djesu akebawivule rye: «Mu dyoni, yike yi fumu nungi obavaghe?
LUK 20:16 Djandi, orughe na oboke bisyele byeni bine, na owakise nungi andi va makake ma bisyele bisusu.» Batu banowulu nane, bakemuwake rye: «Tsatsabi, dighorungule ube nane!»
LUK 20:17 Djesu anobaghengile, akebawivule rye: «Divindughulu di Bisonu bi Nzambi, tsyeni diwendili? Labatyanu: “Dimani adimabwaghu na barungitsi ba mandaghu, yike dine diwarisi nziku yibughe?”
LUK 20:18 Wotsu oduku dibaku mu dimani dyeni, oberughe na otsungughe. Djandi awu dimani dyeni dyubonduyile, onyighemughe.»
LUK 20:19 Milonzi mi mighaghe na bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu bakerombange nane borungulile wughange Djesu mumbari bamatasaange yiri djowu, Djesu amatsokiyilaange mu nongu eni. Tumbe basamamughaange mumbari bamadumange mughungi.
LUK 20:20 Batu bamabe numi-numi na Djesu. Bakemutindile batu abamafuraange ube basatsi ba Nzambi. Batu beni bamarombaange ubaghule batonu mu malongi ma Djesu mu umughange, na umuwakise ombu yidjeti yi baRome mu umusosise.
LUK 20:21 Batu beni abamatindu, bakemuwivule yivu rye: «Mulonzi, twidjabi yiri wivosi nolonze na dusungughu; wughévayi dupasu va ghari batu, tumbe wilonzi na ngenze nzile Nzambi.
LUK 20:22 Tutsinguli nine vo nesi, diwelimine mu ufute lepu ombu Kaghe Sesare?»
LUK 20:23 Tumbe Djesu anobaghule dyele adi mbé bamusoghe, akebawaghule rye:
LUK 20:24 «Mbeyilyanu fure. Yinzi yi nyi? Na dine di nyi bisonughu mu fure eni?» Bakemuwaghule rye: «Bi Kaghe Sesare.»
LUK 20:25 Djesu amabatsingule rye: «Ghabusilanu Kaghe Sesare abivu abyandi, mbana abi Nzambi, bi Nzambi.»
LUK 20:26 Djowu bamakambulu mu posulu tsyandi na basamadile tonu mu umuveghe mbele. Bakevole «swii».
LUK 20:27 Dighuki di baSadisi abamabe na bakemi mu durambughulu du abafu, banobambene na Djesu, bakemuwivulaange rye:
LUK 20:28 «Mulonzi, Moyise, mu mighaghe mi Nzambi, amatusoniyile rye: “Dibaale adiwele, payi aghaabure, yike efu, ngebi andi obyalile mukwili na bobure va yivinze yi awu amafu.”
LUK 20:29 Vamabe yisambwali yi baane ba ngudji ba babaale. Awuteghe akewele na akefu, asamabure.
LUK 20:30 Nduke tsomi [akewele mukwili, akefu djandi wandi asamabure.]
LUK 20:31 Awu muryeru akemwébyalile mukwili eni, akefu djandi wandi, asamabure. Mu yisambwali yotsu ayi mabyalile mukwili, yikefu, yi samasile baane.
LUK 20:32 O nzitu, mughetu wandi akefu.
LUK 20:33 Yilumbu ayi babaale beni borambuyile o dufu, anyi obe mulumi mughetu eni? Mumbari amabe mughatsi djowu botsu.»
LUK 20:34 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Mu butambe bwébubu, baghetu na babaale béwelisini,
LUK 20:35 tumbe bamosi abe Nzambi elabi yiri bawelimine mu urambughe o dufu nodile monyu awurughe, djowu baghomwéwele.
LUK 20:36 Kaboghu, dufu mbé dughobwébabembe, mumbari bobe nane byanze bi Nzambi. Djowu bobe baane ba Nzambi, na djandi obarambuse o dufu nobaveghe monyu.
LUK 20:37 Moyise amavose kengili yiri Nzambi orambuse abafu. Ave amavosile mu yilombi yi yivale yi mudji Nzambi, amanengile Fumu “Nzambi dji Aberaame, Nzambi dji Yisaake na Nzambi dji Sakobe.”
LUK 20:38 Agha Nzambi dji bamvumbi, tumbe Nzambi adji djowu abavu monyu, mumbari djowu badji monyu dibandu djandi.»
LUK 20:39 Dighuki di milonzi mi mighaghe baketsingule Djesu rye: «Mulonzi, wutsivose dingenze.»
LUK 20:40 Na djowu, basamamwérungule umuwivule bivu bisusu.
LUK 20:41 Djesu akewivule milonzi mi mighaghe rye: «Dibandu yi batu bévosili rye: “Kirisete, adji mwane Davide?”
LUK 20:42 Davide etubuli djabeni mu mughande Nyimbu rye: “Fumu Nzambi etsinguli Fumu ami rye: Tsane va mabaale mami,
LUK 20:43 tena nyukutighe bambeni baghu, otsi makulu maghu.”
LUK 20:44 Payi Davide enengili Yibyatsi yi Nzambi “Fumu andi”, ka tsyeni omwébile mwane andi?»
LUK 20:45 Mughungi wotsu wunobe limbe mu umuwululu, Djesu aketsingule badukitsi bandi rye:
LUK 20:46 «Kebenanu na milonzi mi mighaghe, djowu aberondingi bu uyenelingaange mu bikutu bisakeme, djowu aberondingi usimbungu na dighobe mu mambure ma mighungi, djowu aberondingi utsane mu bitsighe abiteghe mu mandaghu ma tsambu na mbure tsi mimengu amineni,
LUK 20:47 djowu bédyongi nodayile bakwili, djowu bévayi tsambu tsisakeme mu ukelase yiri basungeme. Mu tonu adjine, Nzambi obakilisi pwele uvyoghulile bamosi.»
LUK 21:1 Ave Djesu amabile o ghari ndaghu Nzambi, anoghengile batu abamasunzaange myenzili myowu, amalabe bisine abimapodulaange myowu mu yevi.
LUK 21:2 Akebwélabe mukwili awuvu yidjaghe, djawandi amayisunzange doli bedji mu yevi yeni.
LUK 21:3 Djesu amavose rye: «Ngenze nyidutsinguli, yidjaghe yi mukwili éwuwu, atsivyoghulile botsu uveghe.
LUK 21:4 Payi nyivosi nane, mumbari bisine byeni, bamapodulaange mbongu atsimabe tsibavyoghulile. Tumbe mukwili ewune, mu budjaghe bwandi, atsipodule byotsu abimabe nandi.»
LUK 21:5 Ave mwa batu bamavosilaange nonyungile ndaghu Nzambi, adjimarungusu na mamani mabwedji na bime abimaveghungu ombu Nzambi, Djesu akevose rye:
LUK 21:6 «Bilumbu byurughe, byotsu bine dwinyungili, byupanzu, va ghosyale ne dimani va djulu dimani nandi.»
LUK 21:7 Djowu bamamuwivule rye: «Mulonzi, temu yi mambu meni molabenine? Na yilimbe yi, tudjabile yiri mambu memane makilabene na mapape?»
LUK 21:8 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Dukebene yiri batu bakedudunze. Mumbari bapwele borughe mu dine dyami na boyidufure yiri “Menu la Kirisete” na “Temu adji Nzambi amasikighe djikebebeli.” Tumbe duyabaduke.
LUK 21:9 Ave duwululu nduku mavite, duyabe na ghome, mumbari mambu motsu mane mbé molelabene. Tumbe, tsi yiri disukusulu di bulongu.»
LUK 21:10 Na amamwébatsingule rye: «Malongu na malongu motoghe; bulongu na bukaghe butoghe.
LUK 21:11 Butambe wandi buregheme, na mu mambure mapwele, vobe bivunge na dungosu du nzale, vobe mambu mavure, ameveyi ghome noreyimise, na bilimbe bimuvingu byulabene o djulu.
LUK 21:12 Tumbe, ne motsu mane makelabene, boledughaange, bakedutsoyise na boduwakise va makake ma bivunde bi mandaghu ma tsambu ma baSwife, bakedukotise o tsughu, bodubeghe va wusu bakaghe na va wusu bidjeti. Boduvayile motsu mane dibandu dine dyami.
LUK 21:13 Moni moduvaghulu mumbari dukebe bambedji bami.
LUK 21:14 Banu na duvotsu mu mirime myenu na duyadume mu motsu ameduyevose mu ukekaghule.
LUK 21:15 Mumbari mebeni nyuduveghe bighume na dyele adi bavinitsi benu baghorungule ughaghene vo udukalile.
LUK 21:16 Djenu, dusumbusu tangudji na biburu byenu, vo baane ba ngudji benu vo na botsu ba yibandu yenu na bambatsi benu. Batu beni boboke bapwele va ghari enu.
LUK 21:17 Djenu, duvinu na botsu dibandu dine dyami.
LUK 21:18 Tumbe ne dunange dumosi mu myuru myenu doghodokughe.
LUK 21:19 Ladibandu, mu duwarulu dwenu, dughobule myonyu myenu.»
LUK 21:20 Djesu amabatsingule rye: «Ave dulabile baghore ba bambeni ukande Serusaleme, djabanu yiri dutsyemughulu dwandi duke beli.
LUK 21:21 Kaboghu, botsu abobe o yinange yi Sudé barini o mikongu, abobe va ngangele Serusaleme bapali. Djowu abobe mu misiru, bayaghabughe o mimbu.
LUK 21:22 Mumbari, mu temu eni, mukilu Nzambi wudughusu mu motsu nane Bisonu byandi bivosili.
LUK 21:23 Kamune maghughe-ma ombu baghetu abobe na mimi na djowu abonwisaange mu temu eni, mumbari bulongu bube mu manyoni maneni na kabu Nzambi djulabene va ghari mukute eni.
LUK 21:24 Bapwele boboku na didjenge, bamosi bobongu nobeghu nane bavighe, mu misyengi myotsu. Na malongu masusu amaghedjabi Nzambi, monighe Serusaleme tena temu owu djusuke.»
LUK 21:25 Djesu amamwévose rye: «Volabene bilimbe mu nyangu, mu tsungi na mu bambwelili. Malongu motsu, mu butambe mobe na keri dibandu nduku neni dji mibidji mi mubu.
LUK 21:26 Batu boghangu na ghome neni, ave botasilaange adyodyulabene mu butambe, mumbari Nzambi okungise byotsu na mbulighe neni djube o djulu.
LUK 21:27 Mbana, bolabe Mwane Mutu eruyi na mangolu na bundumbe va ghari madudumbi.
LUK 21:28 Ave mambu meni molabenine, waranu na nangulanu myuru myenu, mumbari dudjeghusu dwenu duke bebeli.»
LUK 21:29 Mbana Djesu akebabukile nongu rye: «Ghengilatyanu mwiri bafighe na miri misusu.
LUK 21:30 Ave mifulili, dwidjabi yiri temu mvule djikebebeli.
LUK 21:31 Munongu mosi, ave dulabile mambu meni, djabanu yiri na mapape Nzambi oyibyame nane kaghe.
LUK 21:32 Ngenze, nyidutsinguli rye: dukulu dwedudu, dugholefu payi motsu mane, makalabene.
LUK 21:33 Djulu na butambe byuvyoghe, tumbe bighume byami bighovyoghe “vyaa”.»
LUK 21:34 Djesu amamwévose rye: «Lubughanu, duyasingene na mimengu, na malangi na manyoni ma myonyu myenu mumbari dukesutusu mu yilumbu yi mufundu.
LUK 21:35 Mu yilumbu yeni, batu botsu bosutusu nane banyame o ghari mbuse.
LUK 21:36 Moghanu na sambilenganu Nzambi temu tsyotsu mumbari, dukebe na mangolu morinine mambu motsu marange, na ave Mwane Mutu oruyile, akidurasunu duware.»
LUK 21:37 Ave nyangu, Djesu amalonzaange batu o ghari ndaghu Nzambi. Tumbe, akevyosilaange mukolu o mukongu wu miri mi Olive.
LUK 21:38 Bilumbu byotsu, batu bamawendaange o ndaghu Nzambi mu uyéwulu malongi ma Djesu.
LUK 22:1 Temu mumengu mape maghambu dufunusu, winengulu Pake, djimabambenaange.
LUK 22:2 Bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na milonzi mi mighaghe bamarombaange uboke Djesu, tumbe bamabe na ghome mughungi.
LUK 22:3 Dyabu akekote o murime Sudase, omanengulungu Yikalyote, djandi amabangaange mu yinombu yi dighumi na badukitsi babedji (12).
LUK 22:4 Sudase amawende mu uyéwulusunu na bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na bivunde bi baghore abamakelisaange ndaghu Nzambi mu udjabe nane ovayile mu usumbise Djesu.
LUK 22:5 Bivunde bakebase na nzangu, bakewulusunu mu umuveghe mbongu.
LUK 22:6 Sudase akesinge, akerombaange temu nane obawakisile Djesu ne yinombu yi batu yikedjabe.
LUK 22:7 Yilumbu yi mumengu mape magha dufunusu, ayi mbé bobokile mwane yindombu wu mumengu Pake, yimatole.
LUK 22:8 Djesu akesindighe Pyere na San, akebatsingule rye: «Wendanu, ye tutsonzilanu mulambu Pake, tukidji.»
LUK 22:9 Pyere na San bakemuwivule rye: «Wuke wirondi tuketsonziyile mulambu eni?»
LUK 22:10 Djesu abamawaghule rye: «Wulwanu, ave dukotile mu musyengi, dubengune na mutu eyenebeghe tsuve mambe, mudukyanu o ndaghu adji oyekote.
LUK 22:11 Mbana tsingulanu mungo ndaghu rye: “Mulonzi atsitusindighe ombu aghu, wuketulase yibuku yi ndaghu ayi djandi na badukitsi bandi bolile mulambu Pake.”
LUK 22:12 Djandi odulase yibuku yi ndaghu ndeki yeneni yitsonzughu kale, avane duvayile mulambu.»
LUK 22:13 Badukitsi banowende, bakerasune bime byotsu bitsonzughu nane Djesu amabatsingulile na bakelambe mulambu Pake.
LUK 22:14 Temu djinotole, Djesu na bilumbi byandi bakevyoghe va tavule mu udji.
LUK 22:15 Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Nyitsirondaange pwele uledji mulambu éwuwu Pake nenu ne ngatsoghe.
LUK 22:16 Dingenze nyidutsinguli, ngobwéwudji tena yilumbu ayi Nzambi obwévayile mulambu eni o bukaghe bwandi.»
LUK 22:17 Akebonge dimoyi di malamu ma milunde mi vinye, akeghabusile Nzambi diboti, akevose rye: «Bonganu dimoyi dyédidi; mutu-mutu anwangi.
LUK 22:18 Nyidutsinguli yiri ubandile na muni, ngomwenu malamu memame ma vinye tena yilumbu ayi Bukaghe bu Nzambi buruyile.»
LUK 22:19 Akemwébonge dipe, anoghabusile Nzambi diboti, akedibukule, akeghabile bilumbi byandi na akebatsingule rye: «Dipe dyédidi, dunyuru dwami aduvaghulu mu yibile yenu. Djanu mumbari duketangiminaange.»
LUK 22:20 Banomane udji dipe, Djesu akemwébawakise dimoyi na akevose rye: «Dimoyi dyédidi, dinonge adighone na Nzambi mumbari malungu mami mowiteme mu djenu.
LUK 22:21 Kaboghu, djabanu yiri mutu owunzumbise, adji netu vave tavule.
LUK 22:22 Ngenze, nenane Mwane Mutu ofwile mu duvangu du Nzambi, kamune maghughe mutu owumusumbise olabe!»
LUK 22:23 Badukitsi bakebande wuwivusenaange: «Anyi va ghari etu orunguse uvaghe dyambu nane dine?»
LUK 22:24 Va djulu vane, badukitsi bakemwébe na mutsundu wuneni, mu udjabe anyi va ghari owu orungule ube yivunde ayughobusu.
LUK 22:25 Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Bakaghe ba malongu masusu bérumisi nodyamise batu ba misyengi myowu. Nane bivunde abivu na musughe mu djowu bérondi unengulungu: “Bambatsi ba mughungi.”
LUK 22:26 Duyabe nane djowu. Tumbe, oyirondi ube yivunde va ghari enu, mbé okesunze nane mwane ngebi; mbana oyirondi urumise, mbé okevaghule nane musalitsi bambatsi.
LUK 22:27 Kaboghu, anyi avu yivunde, djandi wune odjivu va tavule vo djandi oyikevaghule mu usalile bambatsi? Tsi djandi wune odjivu va metse? Tumbe menu, nyidji va ghari enu nane musalitsi.
LUK 22:28 Djenu, dudji djowu bane abatsiware nami mu purulu.
LUK 22:29 Ladibandu menu, nyiduveyili musughe wu urume Bukaghe bu Nzambi nane Tate ami ambyatsile.
LUK 22:30 Nyivayile nane, mumbari dukedji, nonu va metse mami mu bukaghe bwami. Na dutsanusu mu bitsighe bi bukaghe mu utabule bunzonzi bu dighumi na bifumbe bibedji bi mukute Yisrayele.»
LUK 22:31 Djesu akenengile Simu Pyere: «Simu, Simu, wulu: lanu, Dyabu erondi wudumange djenu botsu nane bésayili uresi mukakesene bipupu na misu.
LUK 22:32 Tumbe menu, nyitsisambile mu ndedju mumbari yitu yaghu yikedede. Na ndedju, mu yilumbu ayiwughabusile dinonge nami, warise baane ba tadji baghu.»
LUK 22:33 Pyere akemutsingule rye: «Fumu, nyitsonzeme uwende naghu o tsughu tena o dufu.»
LUK 22:34 Djesu akemuwaghule rye: «Ndedju Pyere, nyighutsinguli: na muni, ne koku akevose, wukale kumbu yiryeru bwena wughenzyabi.»
LUK 22:35 Mbana, Djesu akebawivule rye: «Ave nyimadusindiyili nenane nyisamaduveghe mbongu, komi vo bapondu, dumaghambu na yime?» Badukitsi bakewaghule rye: «Vyaaghe.»
LUK 22:36 Yike Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Avave, wotsu avu na mbongu abongi, dedi mosi awu avu na komi, abongi na wotsu awu aghaane didjenge, asumbisi yidjungi yandi mu usumbe didjenge.
LUK 22:37 Nyidutsinguli, nane Bisonu bi Nzambi bivosili mu menu: “Mutu éwuwu amatalu va ghari bikongu.” Kaboghu dyambu adivu adyami, dike beli nolabene.»
LUK 22:38 Badukitsi bakemutsingule rye: «Fumu, tune madjenge mabedji.» Djesu akewaghule rye: «Avotsu, amane mawelimine.»
LUK 22:39 Djesu anopale o musyengi, mu yuku yandi, akewende o mukongu wu baOlive. Badukitsi bandi bakemuduke.
LUK 22:40 Ave bamatolile va mbure eni, Djesu akebatsingule rye: «Sambilanu mumbari dukebe mu dumangu.»
LUK 22:41 Djesu akekakene mwa pesu nowu, akekutume, akebande usambile.
LUK 22:42 Amavose rye: «Tate, payi wirondi, bonge na kakesene dimoyi dyédidi di maghughe nami. Mu dyoni, diyadughusu nane nyirondili, tumbe nane ndedju wirondili.» [
LUK 22:43 Vane-vane, yanze yimosi yimarughe o djulu, mu uyimuwarise.
LUK 22:44 Djesu, anoghangu na keri, aketsore manyuru. Akebwese usambile na mangolu na dirughume dyandi dikedekaange va butambe nane maberi ma malungu.]
LUK 22:45 Djesu anomane usambile, akeghabughe ombu badukitsi, akebarasune bilu, batsore manyuru na manyonyi.
LUK 22:46 Djesu akebasimbule, akebawivule: «Dibandu yi dwiwendili yilu? Relemanu na sambilanu mumbari dukébe mu dumangu.»
LUK 22:47 Djesu wuvose mbé akivose, sundile yinombu yi batu yikebarasune. Sudase awu amabe wumosi va ghari dighumi na badukitsi babedji (12), djandi amabe yibeghe ndonge. Akebambene na Djesu, akemubumbe na akemufwife.
LUK 22:48 Djesu akemuwivule rye: «Sudase, mu ufwife waghu, wisumbisili Mwane Mutu?»
LUK 22:49 Abamasyale na Djesu, ave bamalabile dyodikivyoghe, bakewivule Djesu rye: «Fumu, tupalisi madjenge mu utoghe nowu?»
LUK 22:50 Wumosi va ghari owu, akepalise didjenge, aketabule ditudji di mabaale di musalitsi wu yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu.
LUK 22:51 Tumbe Djesu akevose rye: «Dundanu, avotsu.» Na amabembe ditudji di musalitsi na akemubeluse.
LUK 22:52 Mbana Djesu aketsingule bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na bivunde bi baghore na bivunde bi baSwife abamarughe owuyimughaange rye: «Dumarughe na madjenge na mangwangu nane bwena yikongu dwiyighaange.
LUK 22:53 Bilumbu byotsu, nyibetsi nenu o ghari ndaghu Nzambi, dughaakangaange. Temu adjidji, djike djenu adji mangolu ma pisime mesalili mukolu.»
LUK 22:54 Na béghangi Djesu, bakemubeghe o ndaghu yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu. Pyere akenebadukaange va ghegheyi.
LUK 22:55 Batu beni, banobanze mudji va ngangele dulombili, Pyere wandi akeyétsane va ghari owu.
LUK 22:56 Musatsi wumosi wu mughetu wu yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu akemulabe atsane va mughule mudji, akemutsune «pii» na akevose rye: «Dibaale dyédidi wandi abetsi na Djesu!»
LUK 22:57 Tumbe Pyere akeghale nomutsingule rye: «Mughetu, menu ngémudjabi.»
LUK 22:58 Mwa pesu temu, mutu mosi anomulabe, akemutsingule rye: «Ndewandi, wudji nowu!» Tumbe Pyere akewaghule rye: «Nesi, menu nga nowu.»
LUK 22:59 Mwa diweru dinovyoghe, mutu wususu akebwétsiyise bwena: «Nyitasi yiri, dingenze, dibaale dyédidi abetsi nandi mumbari djawandi adji mwise Ngalile.»
LUK 22:60 Pyere akemuwaghule rye: «Ngedjabi adi wirondi uvose.» Ave Pyere amavosilaange, koku wandi novose.
LUK 22:61 Fumu anoghelughe, yiswisu yandi na yi Pyere bikebengune. Sundile Pyere akerangimine adi Fumu amamutsingule: «Na muni, ne koku akevose, ndedju wukale kumbu yiryeru bwena wughenzyabi.»
LUK 22:62 Pyere, anopale o dulombili, amalile «rodoo» na munyongu wotsu.
LUK 22:63 Batu abamakelisaange Djesu, bamamupedjingi na bamamudimbaange.
LUK 22:64 Djowu, banomudibighe yinzi bakemuwivulaange rye: «Bighe na tutsinguli anyi atsighudimbe?»
LUK 22:65 Na bakebwélaange umusyenge nomutsingulaange mambu mamosi mabive.
LUK 22:66 Mune kedi, fundu dji bivunde bi mukute, bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na milonzi mi mighaghe bamaghukume, bakebeghe Djesu va wusu fundu dji banzonzi ba baSwife.
LUK 22:67 Awune, bakemuwivule rye: «Ndedju, la Kirisete? Tutsinguli.» Djandi akebawaghule rye: «Yike nyidutsinguli, djenu dughosinge.
LUK 22:68 Payi nyitsiduwivule yivu, djenu dughokwaghule.
LUK 22:69 Ubandile vave, Mwane Mutu obe atsane o mabaale ma Nzambi-Pungu.»
LUK 22:70 Djowu botsu bakeghamughe va mosi rye: «Kaboghu ndedju, wudji Mwane Nzambi?» Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Djenubeni dumatubule: Nine, menu.»
LUK 22:71 Bakevose rye: «Twisane nzale bambedji! Djetubeni tumaghulwanu, mambu amatsipale va munu andi.»
LUK 23:1 Yinombu yotsu yi batu yikereleme, mu ubeghe Djesu va wusu yidjeti bamanengilaange Pilate.
LUK 23:2 Avane, djowu botsu bamamufwengile na bamatsingule Pilate rye: «Dibaale dyédidi, tutsimurasunu esibisi batu ba bulongu bwetu na ebaghandisi uvane lepu ombu Kaghe Sesare, na evosi yiri djabeni la Kirisete mbana adji Kaghe.»
LUK 23:3 Pilate akemuwivule rye: «Ndedju la Kaghe baSwife?» Djesu akemuwaghule: «Ndebeni widivosi.»
LUK 23:4 Pilate aketsingule bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na yinombu rye: «Menu ngelabi mbele djufwengiyile mutu éwuwu.»
LUK 23:5 Tumbe batu beni bakemwéghamungaange na mangolu rye: «Mu ndonzulu andi, djandi esibisi mukute bakebuse ughobise mighaghe mi kaghe Sesare. Mutu eni atsivaghe nane mu yinange yotsu yi Sudé, ubandile o yinange yi Ngalile, tena wunu tuvwanu.»
LUK 23:6 Ave Pilate amawululu nane, akewivule rye: «Mutu éwuwu, mwise Ngalile?»
LUK 23:7 Batu bakewaghule Pilate bwena Djesu adji mwise Ngalile. Pilate akemutinde ombu kaghe Yirode mwane Atipa. Kaghe adjimarumisaange yinange yi Ngalile na va temu eni, mbé aki o Serusaleme.
LUK 23:8 Yirode akebase na nzangu ave amalabile Djesu mumbari yilemee amarondaange ubengune nandi. Mumba amawulu didume dyandi na amatasaange yiri Djesu omulase mwa yimaghe.
LUK 23:9 Yirode akemuwivule pwele bivu, tumbe Djesu asamamuwaghule ne yimosi.
LUK 23:10 Vane mbure eni, bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na milonzi mi mighaghe bamabe djowu andi na kabu, bakemufwengiyilaange pwele mambu.
LUK 23:11 Yirode na baghore bandi bakepedjingi nosyenge Djesu. Bakemudwise yikutu yi bukaghe na bakemughabuse ombu Pilate.
LUK 23:12 Vane kale Yirode na Pilate bamabangaange bambeni, tumbe mu yilumbu yéyine, bakebwéghabusile bumbatsi.
LUK 23:13 Pilate akeghukighe bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, bidjeti bimosi na mughungi,
LUK 23:14 akebatsingule rye: «Djenu dutsimbeyile dibaale dyédidi na djandi esibisi mukute na kande. Labatyanu, nyitsimusosisile va wusu enu, tumbe ngalabe mbele andi mu mambu ame djenu dwimufwengilili.
LUK 23:15 Ne Yirode djawandi, aghalabe dibi mu Djesu yiri akeboku. Ladibandu atsimughabusile ombu etu. Mutu éwuwu aghaane dyambu adyumurombise dufu.
LUK 23:16 Kaboghu nyurume bakemudimbise bwandi na batsilu mbana bakemudunde.» [
LUK 23:17 Mu kadi mumengu Pake, Pilate amabangaange na yufu yupalisaange mwise tsughu wumosi.]
LUK 23:18 Tumbe yinombu ayimabe vane, wikeghamughe va mosi rye: «Bokise dibaale dyédidi, tupalisili Barabase.»
LUK 23:19 Mu disibise adi Barabase amarombise mu musyengi eni, na uboke awu amabokile mutu, adine dimamukotise o tsughu.
LUK 23:20 Pilate, mu nzale udunde Djesu, akemwébawivule adi mubedji.
LUK 23:21 Tumbe mughungi wukebwéghamughe na mangolu: «Mughomini, mughomini va kurusu.»
LUK 23:22 Pilate akemwébawivule adi muryeru rye: «Dibi dika, mutu éwuwu atsivaghe? Ngelabi dyambu adi djandi obokulu. Menu, nyumudimbise wandi mbana, nyumudunde.»
LUK 23:23 Tumbe mughungi wukebwelaange ughamughe o djulu yiri Djesu aghomunu va kurusu. Yike mu posulu owu, dufu du Djesu dukesikughu.
LUK 23:24 Vane-vane, Pilate akesinge adi mughungi wumarondaange.
LUK 23:25 Pilate akebapalisile mutu awubamavondaange awu amasunzu o tsughu dibandu disibise na bukongu bwandi, na akebawakise Djesu bakemuvaghe adi bamarondaange.
LUK 23:26 Ave bamabeyilaange Djesu, bakebengune na dibaale dinengulu Simu mwise musyengi Sirene amarughesenaange o manungi. Baghore bakemusikighe na bakemughome yiri akenangule kurusu mbana akenedukaange Djesu va nzime.
LUK 23:27 Yinombu yineni yi batu yikenebadukaange. Va ghari mughungi eni vakebe mwa dighuki di baghetu bamenelilaange nonyongaange dibandu mukilu wu Djesu.
LUK 23:28 Djesu akebaghengile na akebatsingule rye: «Baghetu ba Serusaleme, duyalile mu menu, lilenganu mu djenubeni na mu baane benu.
LUK 23:29 Lanu, bilumbu byurughe ave batu bovosilaange rye: “Ubwedji ombu bingume, ombu djowu abasekalebure na djowu abasamanwise.”
LUK 23:30 Mu temu eni, batu bovosaange na mikongu na milandu yiri: “Tuvikyanu na tughumbyanu.”
LUK 23:31 Labatyanu, mu mwiri awu monyu bamavaghe mambu mabive, ka mu mukanzu, tsyeni bovayile?»
LUK 23:32 Vane-vane, bakebeghe bikongu bibedji bakiboku va mosi na Djesu.
LUK 23:33 Ave bamatolile va mbure adjimanengulungu «Dubengili», baghore bakeghomine Djesu va kurusu. Yike bakeghomine bikongu byeni mu tsyowu kurusu, wumosi o mabaale, awune o maghetu mandi.
LUK 23:34 [Mwa pesu temu, Djesu akevose rye: «Tate, batandi mumbari baghedjabi adi bévayi.»] Baghore beni bakesole mutu mu udjabe anyi odile yikutu yi Djesu. Mu uyidile, bakevaghe dusolu du yese.
LUK 23:35 Mughungi wumabe wughukeme na wukeghengilaange. Tumbe bivunde bi baSwife, bakepedjingi Djesu na bakevosange rye: «Amaghobule basusu, tsyé akeghobuli djabeni payi adji Kirisete awu Nzambi amasole!»
LUK 23:36 Baghore wandi bakebambene, bakemupedjingi na Bakemuveghe dingibe dingani akenu.
LUK 23:37 Bakevose rye: «Payi wudji Kaghe baSwife, tsyékeghobule ndebeni!»
LUK 23:38 Mu yasi yi dusimbi ayimaghomunu va kurusu o djulu muru andi, bamasonighe: «Awuwu, Kaghe baSwife.»
LUK 23:39 Yikongu yimosi ayimaghomunu va kurusu va mughule Djesu, akemubangulaange novose rye: «Ndedju, meta wudji Kirisete? Tsyékeghobule ndebeni na tughobuli!»
LUK 23:40 Yikongu ayi mubedji ayimaghomunu wandi mu djandi kurusu, akesyembe mbatsi na akemutsingule rye: «Nenane wutsiveghulu mukilu nane mutu éwuwu, ndedju wughédumi Nzambi?
LUK 23:41 Mu djetu naghu, tuwelimine mudile fute édjidji mu mambu ame tumavaghe. Tumbe djandi, aghavaghe dyambu dibi.»
LUK 23:42 Mbana yikongu yeni akevose rye: «Djesu, wuyandibene ave wuruyile mu uyibyame nane kaghe.»
LUK 23:43 Vane-vane, Djesu akemuwaghule rye: «Dingenze nyighutsinguli, na muni, wukote nami o Bukaghe bu Nzambi.»
LUK 23:44 Va mwangulu, nyangu djikevole na pisime djikedughunu mu butambe bwotsu tena murekemunu wu wisi.
LUK 23:45 Dimengi di nyangu dinotsyemughe, pisime djikebase mu butambe, dumbu du mbure adji Syeme va dikotulu di ndaghu Nzambi dukepasighe va ghari.
LUK 23:46 Djesu akeghamughe mughamu wuneni, akevose rye: «Tate, nyiwakisi Yinyuni yami va makake maghu.» Anomane uvose nane, akefu.
LUK 23:47 Yivunde yi baghore anolabe adimavyoghe, akedodise Nzambi novose: «Dingenze, mutu éwuwu abetsi asungeme.»
LUK 23:48 Yinombu yi batu yimarughe pwele, yinolabe adimavyoghe, yikeneghabughe mu mimbu mowu, bakene dumange batulu dibandu munyongu wuneni mu mirime.
LUK 23:49 Bambatsi botsu ba Djesu na baghetu abamawendaange nandi, ubongile o Ngalile, bamabe bavengeme djowu mbure na bakeghengilaange nane mambu mamavyoyilaange.
LUK 23:50 Vamabe mutu dine dyandi Sosefe, amabe na musighe, asungeme, akevivaange durughulu du Bukaghe bu Nzambi. Djandi, amabe yivunde wandi va ghari fundu dji banzonzi ba baSwife na amabe mwise musyengi wu Arimate mu yinange yi Sudé. Asamasobene ditase na bambatsi mu uboke Djesu.
LUK 23:52 Dibaale dyeni, akewende, mu uyélabe yidjeti Pilate, akemuveghe musughe mu ubonge dunyuru du Djesu. Pilate akemugharusu.
LUK 23:53 Sosefe akesunduse dunyuru du Djesu va kurusu, akedupote va tsande na akedusunze o ngile adjimatimu o ghari tali o mbé wukatswighulu mutu.
LUK 23:54 Amadivaghe, mu yilumbu ayiduki yilumbu ayireli yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, ayi batu basamasalilaange.
LUK 23:55 Baghetu abamenedukaange Djesu, ubongile o Ngalile, bakesobene konge na Sosefe na bakewende o ngile. Awune bamalabe nane bamasunzile dunyuru du Djesu.
LUK 23:56 Banomane, bakeghabughe mu mandaghu, muyetsonzighe matsi na miyombu muyeghotse dunyuru du Djesu. Djowu, bamaghobise mughaghe awighandisi baSwife usale mu yilumbu yuvume.
LUK 24:1 Mu yilumbu yiteghe yitsone, va matebughulu ma wisi, baghetu bamawende o ngile na birure bi matsi na miyombu ami bamatsonzighe.
LUK 24:2 Ave bamatolile, bakerasunu dimani adi bamakibiyile ngile dimavengughu va mughule.
LUK 24:3 Bakekote, basamarasunu dunyuru du Fumu Djesu.
LUK 24:4 Baghetu, bakesutu. Sundile, babaale babedji badware bikutu bikadimi, bakelabene va wusu owu.
LUK 24:5 Baghetu, bakeghangu na ghome, baketsokighe misu na tsi. Babaale beni bakebawivule rye: «Dibandu yi dwirombili odjivu monyu va ghari djowu abamafu?
LUK 24:6 Asa vave, tumbe amarambughe o dufu. Kaboghu, rangiminanu ame amadutsingulanga ave mbé akivu o Ngalile.
LUK 24:7 Avane, amavosaange rye: “Diwelimine yiri Mwane Mutu owakusu va makake ma bavayitsi ba mabi, oghomunu va kurusu, mbana mu yilumbu ayimuryeru, orambughe o dufu”.»
LUK 24:8 Vane-vane, baghetu beni bamarangimine mambu ame Djesu amabatsingulaange.
LUK 24:9 Banoghusughe o ngile, bakeghabughe muyetsingule dighumi na yilumbi yimosi na badukitsi botsu.
LUK 24:10 Mu yinombu yi baghetu beni, vamabe Mari mwise musyengi wu Maghedale, Sane na Mari ngudji Sake, na baghetu bamosi. Djowu bane, abamayétsingule bilumbi nane bamayerasunine o ngile.
LUK 24:11 Tumbe bilumbi byeni baketasange yiri motsu ame baghetu bamabatsingule, amofure na basamamavayile yitu.
LUK 24:12 Vane-vane, Pyere akereleme, akatiremughe mbangu nowende o ngile. Anodokemine, akelabe yike matsande vatsi, na akeghabughe o ndaghu andi, akekambulu mu dyambu adi amayerasunu o ngile.
LUK 24:13 Mune yilumbu yeni, badukitsi babedji bamawende o musyengi Yimayise, dimbu dimabe dikakene mu dighumi na take bedji na Serusaleme.
LUK 24:14 Djowu bakenevosange mu mambu motsu amamavyoghe.
LUK 24:15 Ave bamenevosilaange notsunde mu mambu meni, Djesu akebambene na akesobene konge nowu.
LUK 24:16 Batu beni bamamulabaange, tumbe Nzambi akebavaghe muvuyisini yiri bakemujabe.
LUK 24:17 Djesu akebawivule rye: «Dyambu yi dwiyenetsundile mu nzile?» Djowu, bakesikeme na munyongu wotsu.
LUK 24:18 Wumosi va ghari owu, enengilu Kolopase, akemuwaghule rye: «Bu ndedju pinze awitsani va musyengi Serusaleme awughadjabe motsu amatsivyoghe mu bilumbu byébibi?»
LUK 24:19 Djesu akebawaghule rye: «Ayii?» Djowu botsu bakemukanzuyile rye: «Dyambu aditsivyoghe mu Djesu mwise Nasarete. Amabe mubiyitsi wuneni avosange na mangolu nodughusungu bisalu bineni, va wusu Nzambi na va wusu batu.
LUK 24:20 Bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na bidjeti byetu, bamamusumbise yiri akekilusu na akeghomunu va kurusu.
LUK 24:21 Djetu botsu mbé tukane yitu bwena djandi o mbé oyighobule mukute Yisrayele. Tumbe labatyanu, yilumbu ayiyi yike yi muryeru, mambu memane mamalabenine.
LUK 24:22 Dingenze, baghetu bamosi va ghari etu, bamatusutusu ave bamawendile kedi neni o ngile.
LUK 24:23 Banotole, basamarasunu yibindi yi Djesu. Bakeghabughe, bakebeghe tsangu bwena Byanze bitsibatsingule yiri Djesu adji monyu.
LUK 24:24 Ladibandu, babaale bamosi abamabe netu, bamawendile djowandi o ngile, bakérasunu nane baghetu bamayitutsingulile bwena basamalabe yibindi yandi.»
LUK 24:25 Djesu akevose nowu rye: «Dughejabi dyambu, durange usinge, na mirime myenu mighale, mu ughangise motsu ame babiyitsi bamadutsingule!
LUK 24:26 Diwelimine yiri Kirisete mbé oletsoghusu ne akekote mu bundumbe bwandi.»
LUK 24:27 Vane-vane, Djesu akebande ubatsingule motsu ame Bisonu bi Nzambi bimavose mu djabeni: ubongile mu mighande mi Moyise tena mu Bisonu bi babiyitsi botsu.
LUK 24:28 Yike bebi bebeli na dimbu adi bamawendaange, Djesu akevaghe nane djandi evyoyi kwase.
LUK 24:29 Mubedji ewune, bamamughome nomutsingule rye: «Wisi wumatsime, sikeme wukevyose mukolu netu.» Djesu amakote nowu o ndaghu.
LUK 24:30 Ave bamavyoyile va metse, Djesu akebonge dipe, akeghabusile Nzambi diboti, akedibukule na akebaveghe.
LUK 24:31 Vane-vane, misu mowu mamadibughe na bamamudjabe. Tumbe Djesu akesundile, utsyemughe va wusu owu.
LUK 24:32 Badukitsi beni bakewivusunaange rye: «Tutsighulungu nane yusile mu mirime myetu ave atsiyene tuvosilaange mu nzile, na ave atsiyene tuvindiyilaange Bisonu bi Nzambi!»
LUK 24:33 Badukitsi beni, bakereleme, bakesogheme o Serusaleme. Bakeye rasune dighumi na yilumbi yimosi na badukitsi botsu abamabe baghukeme nowu.
LUK 24:34 Banobarasune, baketsingule badukitsi babedji rye: «Ame tutsighulu mangenze, Fumu adji monyu! Dingenze, atsilabene na Simu!»
LUK 24:35 Badukitsi babedji bakemwébatsingule adimalabe mu nzile na nane bamadjabile Djesu ave amabukulile dipe.
LUK 24:36 Ave bamavosilaange, Djesu djabeni akesundile upale va ghari owu na akebatsingule rye: «Duvotsu dubi nenu!»
LUK 24:37 Banoghangu na keri, baketsaghemughe, mumbari bamatasaange yiri ditengu dimapale va ghari owu.
LUK 24:38 Tumbe Djesu, akebawivule rye: «Dibandu yi, dwitsaghemuyili na mumbari yi, dubile na bakemi mu mirime myenu bwena nyidji monyu?
LUK 24:39 Ghengilanu makake na matambi mami: dughélabi bwena menu? Ghengilanu na mbembyanu, ditengu aghaane dunyuru nane menu.»
LUK 24:40 Anobatsingule nane, akebalase makake na matambi mandi.
LUK 24:41 Djowu ne nane basamalesinge, dibandu nzangu na usutu awu bamasutu. Djesu akebawivule rye: «Avave, dughaane mwa yighudji yi udji?»
LUK 24:42 Bakemuveghe yibuku yi nyame mambe djighoku na yasi yi yisile yi budji.
LUK 24:43 Djesu akeyibonge, akeyidji va misu mowu.
LUK 24:44 Mbana, akebatsingule rye: «Lanu, adi nyimadutsingulaange mbé ngi va ghari enu: mambu motsu amamasonughu mu menu mu mughaghe wu Moyise, mu bisonu bi babiyitsi na mu mughande Nimbu, mbé moledughusu.»
LUK 24:45 Yike Djesu, akebadibule dudjabu, mumbari bakewulu notsiyise Bisonu bi Nzambi.
LUK 24:46 Mbana akemwébatsingule rye: «Disonughu yiri Kirisete, otsoghusu na mu yilumbu ayimuryeru, osimbughe va ghari djowu abafu.
LUK 24:47 Mu malongu motsu, ubandile o musyengi Serusaleme, musamu wu dukalusu du mutsanu na wu dutandulu du mabi ma batu, mbé wusamunu mu dine dyandi.
LUK 24:48 Djenubeni, dudji bambedji ba mambu meni.
LUK 24:49 Tumbe menu, nyudutindile pangini adji Tate ami amadulonge. Kaboghu, tsananu vave musyengi éwuwu tena dubase na mangolu ameruyi o djulu.»
LUK 24:50 Djesu akebabeghe o yari musyengi Betani. Avane, akenangule makake na djulu, akesambile Nzambi na akebaveghe myule.
LUK 24:51 Ave amabaveyilaange myule, akekakene nowu, akematusu o djulu.
LUK 24:52 Badukitsi beni nabemani wumuyitse, bakeghabusile o Serusaleme na nzangu neni.
LUK 24:53 Na temu tsyotsu bamabengunange va dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi mu umuyitsaange na mu umudodisaange.
ACT 1:1 Mundumbe Tofile, mu mughande ami wuteghe, nyimawulase motsu ame Djesu amadughusungu nolonzaange vane dibandu
ACT 1:2 tena yilumbu ayi amamatile o djulu. Mu yilumbu yeni, na mangolu ma Yinyuni Yisyeme, amaveghe marume mu botsu abe amasole mube bilumbi.
ACT 1:3 Va djulu dufu dwandi, amalabene monyu nowu. Mu maghumi-mana (40) ma bilumbu, amabalasaange yi ngenze adji monyu. Mu temu eni, amalonzaange mambu ma Bukaghe bu Nzambi.
ACT 1:4 Ave amabile nowu va mulambu, amabatsingule rye: «Syalanu wune musyengi Serusaleme, na dukelise pangini adji Tate amadulonze, adji mebeni nyimadutsingule kale.
ACT 1:5 San amabatise na mambe, tumbe djenu, mu mwa pesu bilumbu, dubatusu mu Yinyuni Yisyeme.»
ACT 1:6 Djowu bamaghukeme na bamawivule Djesu rye: «Fumu, mu temu edjine wubyatsu kaghe mukute Yisrayele, mumbari wukeghabughe bulongu buneni nane va teghe?»
ACT 1:7 Amabawaghule rye: «Dyambu dyenu tsiri udjabe batemu na maweru ame Tadji ami amatsonzighe mu ditase dyandi.»
ACT 1:8 Tumbe dudile mangolu, Yinyuni Yisyeme yusundughe mu djenu, na dube bambedji bami ubandile o musyengi Serusaleme, o yinange yi Sudé, o yinange Samari teno masukusulu ma butambe.
ACT 1:9 Yike emani uvose moni, amamatusu o djulu na va wusu owu, amatsyemughe o ghari madudumbi.
ACT 1:10 Nenane djowu bamatsuninaange o djulu ave Djesu amenematilaange, babaale babedji na bidwaru biveme bamasundile wulabene nowu.
ACT 1:11 Na bamavose nowu rye: «Bise Ngalile, dibandu yi dwisutulu na ughengile o djulu? Djesu adjitsimatusu o djulu va ghari enu, oghabughe munongu mosi nane atsimatile.»
ACT 1:12 Bilumbi bamadusughe mukongu awinengulu Olive, na bakeghabughe o musyengi Serusaleme. Mukongu eni umabe va dyasu diveghu musughe ulinge yilumbu yi duvumu yi baSwife.
ACT 1:13 Banotole o musyengi Serusaleme, bakemate o yibuku yi ndaghu ayi djulu, nane na kale. Vamabe Pyere, San, Sake na Andere, Filipe na Tome, Batelemi na Mati, Sake mwane Alefé, Simu awu benengili Selote, na Sudase mwane Sake.
ACT 1:14 Djobotsu bamabengunungu temu na temu va mosi mu dusambu, na baghetu, na Mari ngudji Djesu, na baane ba ngudji ba Djesu.
ACT 1:15 Mu bilumbu byeni, Pyere amareleme va ghari owu. Durangu du botsu dumabe kame na maghumi-mabedji (120). Na akevose rye:
ACT 1:16 «Baane ba tadji, diwelimine yi pangini adjimabighu mu Bisonu bi Nzambi djuduwusu. Mu Bisonu byeni, Yinyuni Yisyeme amavose vane kale mu munu Davide, mu dyambu di Sudase, awu amabe yibeghe ndonge yi abamarughe o uyighaange Djesu.
ACT 1:17 Dibaale dyédine, amabe wumosi va ghari etu, na amasalaange va mosi netu.
ACT 1:18 Na mbongu atsi amadile mu bukongu bwandi, amasumbe nungi andi. O ghari nungi eni amaberuyile maghuwusu, modji andi wuke pasighe na misopu myotsu mikebe layini va tsi.
ACT 1:19 Batu botsu ba musyengi Serusaleme bamadiwulu, la dibandu o mbembu owu, bamanengilile nungi eni “Akeldama” diwendi yiri: “Nungi malungu”.»
ACT 1:20 Na Pyere amabwele rye: «Mu mughande Nyimbu, disonu rye: “Batu badusuyi mu ndaghu andi, na vayabe mutu wutsane mu djoni.” Na disonu rye: “Mutu mususu abongi mbure andi.”
ACT 1:21 Vengu tusolanu wumosi va ghari botsu abamayenewendaange konge netu, temu djotsu Fumu Djesu amanangilaange bulongu netu.
ACT 1:22 Amabe netu ubandile temu adji San amabatisile Djesu, tena yilumbu ayi amamatile o djulu. Kaboghu, mutu mosi mu yinombu mbé obe mbedji netu, dji durambughu du Djesu o dufu.»
ACT 1:23 Bamalase batu babedji: Sosefe awu bamanengilaange «Baresabase», dine dyandi dimosi «Susutuse» na Matyase.
ACT 1:24 Bakevaghe dusambu dwedudu: «Fumu, widjabi mirime mi botsu. Tulasi ndebeni, anyi mu mubedji éwuwu, wusole.
ACT 1:25 Djandi obe yilumbi, na obonge yisalu va yivinze yi Sudase, omayisile mughabughe o mbure adjimabe djandi.»
ACT 1:26 Va djulu vane, bakebwaghe mbande, na Matyase akebwesu mu yinombu yi dighumi na yilumbi yimosi.
ACT 2:1 Ave yilumbu yi mumengu Patekote yimatolile, bango yitu bamabe baghukeme mbure mosi.
ACT 2:2 Sundila, nduku djimarughe o djulu, djimabe nane mungudi wuneni. Nduku eni djimabase ndaghu adji bamabe baghukemine.
ACT 2:3 Kaboghu, bakelabe ndimi nane milutsu mi mudji. Tsikekakunu, tsikesundughe na tsiketsane mu kale mutu.
ACT 2:4 Botsu bamabasu na Yinyuni Yisyeme na bamabande uvose mambembu masusu, nane Yinyuni amaveyilaange kale mutu mumavose.
ACT 2:5 O Serusaleme, wumabe baSwife bamayitsaange Nzambi, bamarughesene mu malongu motsu ma butambe.
ACT 2:6 Ave bamawululu nduku eni, yinombu yi batu yikeghukeme. Yimakambulu tinde ukambulu, mumbari kale mutu amabaghulungu uvose mu dilongu dyandi.
ACT 2:7 Bamasutu na bakebanyungilaange, novosaange rye: «Batu bebabe, bise Ngalile!
ACT 2:8 Yike tsyeni twibaghululu, uvose dilongu di mutu-mutu?
ACT 2:9 Va ghari etu, bamosi bise Patese, Medese, Elame, Mesopotami, o Sudé na Kapadose, basusu bise Pon na Asi,
ACT 2:10 Firisi, Pafili, Yisipete, bamosi o musyengi wu Libi adji bambene na Sirene, na botsu abamarughesene o Rome,
ACT 2:11 bise Kerete na Arabi. Va ghari etu, bane bamaburu baSwife, abane wandi bamarughesene o malongu masusu, bamavayile Nzambi baSwife yitu. Yike tsyeni twibaghululu uvose maboti ma Nzambi mu mambembu metu.»
ACT 2:12 Botsu bamasutu na bamaghambu na dyuvose. Bamakewivulaange yiri: «Adidi tsyé diwendili?»
ACT 2:13 Tumbe basusu, bamapedjingi botsu abamasinge Nzambi novose rye: «Badji mu malangi!»
ACT 2:14 Pyere na dighumi na yilumbi yimosi, bamareleme va ghari mughungi, na Pyere akevose rye: «Bise Sudé, na djenu botsu abe dwitsani o Serusaleme, wulwanu adivyoyi na dyo ngadutsingule, limbighanu matudji.
ACT 2:15 Batu beni babe bagha balange nane dwitasili, mumbari wisi aki kedi.
ACT 2:16 Tumbe vave, adimavosu na mubiyitsi Sowele:
ACT 2:17 “Mu bilumbu bi musitu, me Nzambi, nyuveghe Yinyuni yami mu batu botsu. Baane benu babaale na ba baghetu bobighaange. Minzambu myenu myulabaange biryaryamu, mba binunu byenu byudoraange bandosi.
ACT 2:18 Nine, mu bilumbu byébine, nyusunze Yinyuni yami, mu basalitsi bami botsu ba babaale na ba baghetu. Djowu botsu bobighaange.
ACT 2:19 Menu nyulase bimaghe o djulu, na bilimbe mu butambe, vobe malungu, mudji, na dimungi di nzumbili.
ACT 2:20 Nyangu djutsime nokalughe piseme, na tsungi djubenge nane malungu, ne yilumbu yi Fumu yike rughe, yilumbu ayube yineni mba yirange.
ACT 2:21 Yike batu botsu abonengile Fumu, boghobulu.”
ACT 2:22 Bise Yisrayele, wulwanu adi menu ngadutsingule. Djesu mwise Nasarete amabe mutu awu Nzambi amadulase munongu andi. Amadivaghe ave amamuveyile musughe wuvaghe bimaghe na bilimbe bi mangolu. Djandi amadughusu va ghari enu nane djenubeni dwididjabili.
ACT 2:23 Nane djabeni Nzambi amakunzile mu dughanu dwandi ne mambu meni makelabene, djenu dumaghangise Djesu na batu baghane yitu, bakemughomine nomuboke va kurusu.
ACT 2:24 Tumbe Nzambi amamudjeyise mu maghughe ma dufu, akemughabuse monyu, mumbari Djesu mbé aghorungule ughangu na mangolu ma dufu.
ACT 2:25 Kaghe Davide amavose mu djandi rye: “Nyimalabaange Fumu va wusu ami, o mabaale mami, mumba ngéregheme.
ACT 2:26 Ladibandu, murime ami wumabile mu nzangu, na munu ami wiwimbili na yinyunge. Ne dunyuru dwami dube dubase na yitu,
ACT 2:27 mumbari Fumu aghonzile o bulongu bu bobafu, na wughogharu bwé Yibyatsi yaghu Yisyeme, yikebungene wusulemughe o ghari mbine.
ACT 2:28 Wumandase manzile amebeyi o monyu, wumbase na nzangu ave nyubile va wusu aghu.”
ACT 2:29 Baane ba tadji, menu nine musughe wudutsingule na bureti mu dyambu di kaaghe etu Davide. Djandi amafu, na amatswighu na mbine andi djikilabene tena vave, va ghari etu.
ACT 2:30 Djandi amabighe mumba amadjabaange yiri Nzambi amaleve pesi mu djabeni bwé, wumosi mu bateghule bandi obe yivinze yandi va yitsighe yi bukaghe.
ACT 2:31 Mu posulu eni, Davide amabighe durambughulu du Kirisete o dufu. Adine amavosile rye: “Asamamusile o bulongu bu bobafu, na dunyuru dwandi dusamabole o ghari mbine.”
ACT 2:32 Djesu eni nyiranguni, Nzambi amamughabuse monyu. Djetu botswanu tudji bambedji.
ACT 2:33 Tate Nzambi amamatise Djesu o mabaale mandi. Djandi amamuveghe Yinyuni Yisyeme ayimavangenu. Djawandi amatupuyile yoni, adine dwilabi nowulu vave.
ACT 2:34 Davide djabeni asamamate o djulu, tumbe amavose rye: “Fumu Nzambi amatsingule Fumu ami yiri: Yitsane omabale mami,
ACT 2:35 tena nyusunze bavinitsi baghu otsi makulu maghu.”
ACT 2:36 Mukute wotsu wu Yisrayele widjabi na bureti yiri Nzambi amamubyatse Fumu na Kirisete. Djesu édjine adji dutsi ghomine noboke va kurusu.»
ACT 2:37 Bapikile ba botsu abamawulu mbembu édjine baketsyemughe, na bamawivule Pyere na bilumbi bimosi yiri: «Bane ba tadji, yike tsyeni turungule wuvayile?»
ACT 2:38 Pyere amabawaghule rye: «Fungulanu nodunde mabi menu, na kale mutu mbé obatusu mu dine di Djesu Kirisete. Vaghanu nane, mabi menu motandu, na dukedile Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 2:39 Nzambi amaghane wudivaghe ombu bane benu, djenubeni, na botsu abetsani o malongu mavale, batu botsu nane Fumu Nzambi obanengilile.»
ACT 2:40 Pyere amabwévose pwele mambu, na amabawarise novose rye: «Singanu dughobutsu mumbari monyu enu, wukekakene na mutsanu wubive wu bulongu bwébubu!»
ACT 2:41 Botsu abamawulu nosinge mbembu Pyere, bamabatusu. Mu yilumbu yeni, tangudji tosini-yiryeru (3 000) tsi batu bamasobene nowu mu yinombu.
ACT 2:42 Temu tsyotsu, bamawulungu ndonzulu bilumbi na musighe, bakebeghange monyu dibure-ngudji, bamadjangaange nosambilaange va mosi.
ACT 2:43 Kale mutu amawulungu keri, mumbari Nzambi amadughusungu pwele bilimbe na bimaghe mu nzalusulu bilumbi.
ACT 2:44 Bango yitu botsu bamabangaange mbure mosi na bamaghabenaange byotsu abimabangaange byowu.
ACT 2:45 Bamasumbisaange maboti mowu, na bakeghabenaange badoli djobotsu, nane kale mutu amabilaange na nzale.
ACT 2:46 Bilumbu byotsu, na murime mosi, bamaghukemange o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi. Bameneghabaange bighudji mu mandaghu mowu na bamadjangaange na nzangu na murime pwelele.
ACT 2:47 Bamayitsaange Nzambi na mukute wotsu wumabanyungilaange. Na Fumu amabwesaange kale yilumbu mu yinombu yowu botsu abe amaghobulaange.
ACT 3:1 Mwa yilumbu, va murekemunu wisi, Pyere na San bamawendaange o ndaghu Nzambi, va diweru di dusambu.
ACT 3:2 Lake, bamatsyetaange dibaale dimaburu yikoyi, awu amasunzungu kadi yilumbu va dikotulu di ngande ndaghu Nzambi, va mune ndaghu awinengulu «Diwuyi Diboti». Djandi amavondaange mbongu na yingebe, ombu djowu abamakotaange o ghari ndaghu Nzambi.
ACT 3:3 Anolabe Pyere na San bwé yikukote bakekote o ghari ngande eni, dibaale dyeni, akebavonde mbongu.
ACT 3:4 Pyere djone San bakemughengise na bakemutsingule yi: «Tutsuni.»
ACT 3:5 Djandi akebatsune, amatase yiri odile mwa yime mu djowu.
ACT 3:6 Tumbe Pyere akemutsingule rye: «Ngane badoli vo lore, tumbe ayivu nami, nyighuve yoni. Mu dine di Djesu Kirisete mwise Nasarete, releme na wende!»
ACT 3:7 Akemughaange mu dikake dyandi di mabaale, akemurelighe. Vane-vane, matambi mandi na bapanzi bandi bikesundile wuware,
ACT 3:8 akereleme fungelini na akebande uwende. Amakote nowu o ghari ngande ndaghu Nzambi, amayenewendaange djabeni, amayenedumughaange, noyitsaange Nzambi.
ACT 3:9 Mukute wotsu wumamulabe uwende, noyitse Nzambi.
ACT 3:10 Bamamudjabaange yiri djandi awu amabangaange atsane va Diwuyi Diboti di ndaghu Nzambi, mu vondaange mbongu. Banolabe adimamuruyile, batu bamakambulu na bamasutu.
ACT 3:11 Tumbe djandi, asamamwékakene na Pyere na San. Mukute wotsu wumawende mbangu wukebakande o dulombili du ngande ndaghu Nzambi, o Pyasu dji Salemu, bamasutu.
ACT 3:12 Ave Pyere amalabile nane, akevosile mughungi yi: «Batu ba Yisrayele, mumba yi dumasutulu mu aditsilabene? Yi dwitutsunini, nane bwé mu mangolu metu vo yitu yetu, mutu éwuwu atsirelemine?
ACT 3:13 Nesi, tumbe Nzambi Aberaame, adji Nzambi Yisaake, Nzambi Sakobe na Nzambi baghulu betu, amabase Djesu musalitsi andi na bundumbe. Djesu eni adji dumasumbise ombu Pilate na dumamughale va wusu andi. Nenane Pilate mbé amudjeyisile.
ACT 3:14 Yine dumamughale, djandi awu asyeme na asungeme. Va yivinze yandi, dumavonde musughe wudjeyise yikongu.
ACT 3:15 Mu dyoni, dumaboke oyive monyu, tumbe Nzambi atsimurambuse o dufu, tudji bambedji.
