ACT 3:16 Kaboghu, dwilabi mutu éwuwu na dwimudjabi. Mu dine di Djesu atsiwarusulu, mumbari djetu twivali Djesu yitu. Mu yitu mu Djesu atsibelusu djandi wotsu, va wusu djetu botsu.
ACT 3:17 Na vave, baane ba tadji, nyidjabi yiri dutsighambu na dudjabu mu nzalesulu tsyenu, nane bivunde byenu.
ACT 3:18 Nzambi amadidughusu nane djabeni amadikunzile va dibandu mu munu babiyitsi botsu yi Kirisete adji otinde, otsoghusu.
ACT 3:19 Kaboghu, fungulanu mabi menu na ghabughanu manzinzimze, mumbari mabi menu maketsindulu.
ACT 3:20 Anane Fumu oduveghile duvotsu, na odutindile djandi awu amasolu, Djesu Kirisete.
ACT 3:21 Diwelimine bwé Djesu mbé olebe o djulu na Nzambi, tena yilumbu ayi mambu motsu moghabuyile maghone, nane Nzambi amavosile mu munu babighitsi bandi basyeme.
ACT 3:22 Dingenze Moyise amavose: “Fumu Nzambi enu odupalisile va ghari mukute enu mubiyitsi nane menu. Dumuwululu mu motsu ame odutsingule.
ACT 3:23 Wotsu owubuse uwulu mubiyitsi, oboku na obungu va ghari mukute Nzambi.”
ACT 3:24 Babiyitsi botsu, ubandile va Samwele na botsu abamarughe va yinzime yandi, bamavose djowandi mu temu adjidji tuvu anu.
ACT 3:25 Djenu dudji baane ba babiyitsi, mba bibyalile bi disyale adi Nzambi amavangene na baghulu betu. Lanu adi Nzambi amatsingule Aberaame: “Bifumbe byotsu bi butambe na bakule bowu, bodile myule.”
ACT 3:26 Pangini édjidji adji enu, adjimarombise Nzambi utinde musalitsi andi muduveghe myule, nodukakene mu mabi menu.»
ACT 4:1 Bavaghulitsi ba paghu na yivunde yi baghore abamakelisaange ndaghu Nzambi, na bise dibuli di baSadisi bamaruyile ave Pyere djone San bamavosilaange mughungi.
ACT 4:2 Djobotsu bamabase na kabu djineni, mumbari bamalabe Pyere djone San ulonze mukute yi: botsu abafu wandi boghabughe monyu, nane Djesu amaghabuyile monyu.
ACT 4:3 Bakebaghaange na bakebabwaghe o tsughu tena kedi, mumbari wisi mbé wumatsime.
ACT 4:4 Tumbe, bapwele va ghari botsu abamawulu mbembu Nzambi, bakesinge ube bango yitu. Durangu dwowu dumabe tangudji tosini-yiranu (5 000) tsi batu.
ACT 4:5 Va kedi, bidjeti, bivunde bi baSwife na milonzi mi mighaghe bakeghukeme o Serusaleme.
ACT 4:6 Va ghari owu vamabe: Ane yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, Kayife, San, Alesandere na botsu abamabe mu mukute yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu.
ACT 4:7 Bakebeghe bilumbi va wusu owu na bakebawivule rye: «Mu musughe nyi vo mu dine di nyi dutsidivayile?»
ACT 4:8 Pyere, abasulungu na Yinyuni Yisyeme, akebatsingule rye: «Djenu bidjeti bi mukute na bivunde bi baSwife,
ACT 4:9 djetu tutsivaghe diboti ombu djandi awu abetsi yikoyi. Na nyangu yike wuwivule dwituwivuli, tsyeni dibaale dyédine ditsidilile dubelusu?
ACT 4:10 Djenu botsu na mukute wotsu wu Yisrayele, dune dyambu dimosi adi mbé durungule udjabe: mu dine di Djesu Kirisete mwise Nasarete, dibaale adivu va wusu enu atsi dilile dubelusu. Djesu Kirisete adji djenu dumaghomine va kurusu, Nzambi akemughabuse monyu.
ACT 4:11 Mu Dibuku di Mbembu Nzambi direndu: “Dimani adi djenu barungitsi dumabwaghe, dimakalughe yike dimani, adi neni adi siki yibughe yi ndaghu.” Djesu la dimani dyeni.
ACT 4:12 Djandi wandi pinze, awu orungulu wutughobule. Adine, mu bulongu bwotsu, Nzambi asamaveghe mutu susu, awu djetu botwanu tughobululu.»
ACT 4:13 Bidjeti byeni bike kambulu, binolabe Pyere djone San bévosi na musighe. Vane-vane, bimabwélabe yiri badji batu ba kulini, abasamanenge mba baghane dudjabu. Djowu, bamabadjabaange bwé bamayenewendaange na Djesu.
ACT 4:14 Tumbe, ave bamalabilaange yikoyi ayi mabelusu, diteli va mughule bilumbi, bidjeti byeni bisamadile adi uvose.
ACT 4:15 Kaboghu, baketsingule bilumbi yi: «Palanu o ndaghu dusosusu!» Na bakesyale djobeni notsunde.
ACT 4:16 Bakewivusenaange: «Yike tsyeni turungule wuvayile batu bebabe? Dingenze, bamavaghe yimaghe, batu botsu ba musyengi Serusaleme bamadidjabe, na tughorungule udighale.
ACT 4:17 Tumbe, turungule uvaghe yiri yilumbi yéyine yikényave va ghari mukute. Kaboghu, tubaghandisyanu nobanyangile bwé bayabwé bile uvosile mutu wotsu mu dine di Djesu.»
ACT 4:18 Lake bakenengile Pyere na San, nobatsingule rye: «Duyabwévose vo ulonze mu dine di Djesu.»
ACT 4:19 Tumbe Pyere na San bamabawaghule rye: «Va wusu Nzambi, yi yisungeme: wudughobise djenu, vo wughobise Nzambi? Sosanu djenubeni!
ACT 4:20 Tumbe mu djetu, tughorungule ubuse uvose nolonze mu motsu ame tumalabe nowulu.»
ACT 4:21 Bidjeti byeni bike bwévale Pyere na San mapemi maghone na bakebadunde, basamadile tonu djubakilisile. Yike mukute wotsu wumawimbilaange noyitse bundumbe bu Nzambi dibandu yimaghe ayimalabene.
ACT 4:22 Dibaale adimabelusu na yimaghe yéyine mbé amavyoghe maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime bi duburu.
ACT 4:23 Pyere djone San banodundu, bamawende kwase uyélabe bambatsi bowu, noyebatsingule motsu ame bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, na bivunde bi baSwife bamabatsingule.
ACT 4:24 Banomane ughuwulu ame Pyere na San bamabatsingule, djobotsu bamasambile Nzambi na murime wumosi, novose rye: «Mulonzi, ndedju wumasunde djulu, butambe, mubu na byotsu abivu mune.
ACT 4:25 Ndedju, mu munu Davide kaaghe etu, musatsi aghu awumabase na Yinyuni Yisyeme, wumavose rye: “Mumbari yi mikute mimanyoyile? Mba mitungili Nzambi fundu, tumbe mambu motsu mane ma nzolu.
ACT 4:26 Bakaghe ba butambe bamakunzeme mutoghe divite, bidjeti bimawulusunu mube mimbini mi Fumu Nzambi na Kirisete andi.”
ACT 4:27 Dingenze, Yirode ayi Atipa na Ponze Pilate djowandi, bamaghukeme o musyengi éwuwu, djone beni na mukute Yisrayele, mu toyise Djesu. Djandi awu amabe musatsi awusyeme, awu ndebeni wumasole nane Kirisete.
ACT 4:28 Yike bamadughusu motsu ame ndebeni, mu matase na mangolu maghu, wumakunze vane dibandu.
ACT 4:29 Avave Fumu, labe nane bétukwanini, na veghe bisatsi byaghu mangolu moyenetsingulaange nolonze mbembu aghu na duvotsu vo na musighe.
ACT 4:30 Kaboghu, lase mangolu maghu yi va ghari etu vakelabene biryaryamu, bimaghe, dubelusu na bilimbe bimosi mu dine di musalitsi aghu Djesu, djandi odjivu asyeme.»
ACT 4:31 Ave bamamanine wusambile, butambe bumaregheme va mbure adji bamabe. Djobotsu bakebase na Yinyuni Yisyeme na bamayenetsingulaange mbembu Nzambi na musighe.
ACT 4:32 Botsu abamakalughe bango yitu, bamawulusunungu, na dinonge di murime na ditase dimabe diware va ghari owu. Vagha mutu amavosaange rye: «Bime abibi, abyami!» Tumbe, bamaghabenaange byotsu abi bamadilaange.
ACT 4:33 Yike na mangolu maneni, bilumbi bamayenesamunaange durambughulu du Fumu Djesu o dufu. Mba yese yi Nzambi yimalabenaange na mangolu mu kale mutu.
ACT 4:34 Vasamabe mutu va ghari owu amaghambu na yime, mumbari botsu abamabe na banungi vo mandaghu, bamamasumbisaange na bamabeghaange badoli beni botsu
ACT 4:35 ombu bilumbi. Lake djowu bamatsighabaange, na kale mutu amadilaange dyandi dikabu.
ACT 4:36 Nane yibaghunu yi dibaale bamanengilaange Sosefe, amabe na nungi. Djandi awu bilumbi bamalughe yike Barenabase, diwendili yi: «Mutu awiwarisi», amabaange musalitsi wu dilongu di Levi, mwise Sipere.
ACT 4:37 Akesumbise nungi andi, akebeghe madila na akimaveghe bilumbi.
ACT 5:1 Tumbe dibaale dimanengulungu Ananyase, na mughatsi andi Safire, bakesumbise nungi mosi.
ACT 5:2 Banowulusunu, bakesweghe dikabu di mbongu, na bakelase dikabu adimasyale ombu bilumbi.
ACT 5:3 Pyere akemuwivule rye: «Ananyase, tsyé dyabu amabasile murime aghu nane? Wumafure Yinyuni Yisyeme, mba wumasweghe dikabu di mbongu atsi dutsidile mu nungi enu.
ACT 5:4 Ne wukedjisumbise tsya djibetsi djaghu? Wuno dji sumbise, ughabetsi na musughu wubonge badoli baghu? Yike tsyeni, wutsibile na ditase divelughe nane o ghari murime aghu? Tsi batu wutsifure, tumbe Nzambi!»
ACT 5:5 Yike edighulu, Ananyase akeberughe na akesuke muvumu. Mba botsu abamadiwulu bakeghangu na dunzyenzi.
ACT 5:6 Minzambu bakibonge mvumbi, bakedji pyete noyetswighe.
ACT 5:7 Tangudji maweru maryeru manovyoghe, mughatsi Ananyase akerughe, asamadjabe adimavyoghe.
ACT 5:8 Pyere akemuwivule yi: «Nzinguli, dufunu adu dutsisumbisile nungi enu adudu?» Akewake: «Yine, adune.»
ACT 5:9 Kaboghu Pyere akemutsingule rye: «Tsyé dutsiwulusununu mumange Yinyuni yi Fumu? Wulu! Abatsiyetswighe mulumi aghu, bake va mune ndaghu, bowubeghe ndewandi.»
ACT 5:10 Vane-vane akeberughe va makulu ma Pyere na akesuke muvumu. Minzambu mikekote, mikemurasunu amafu, mikemunangule na bakeyémutswighe va mughule mulumi andi.
ACT 5:11 Dibundu dyotsu na botsu abamamawulu bakeghangu tindi na dunzyenzi.
ACT 5:12 Bimaghe na bilimbe bipwele bimavaghungu na bilumbi va ghari mughungi. Bango yitu bamatsanaange va mosi o Pyasu Salemu.
ACT 5:13 Djobotsu bamabaghobisaange pwele, yotsu yine, vagha ne mutu wumosi wumarondaange wusobene nowu.
ACT 5:14 Baghetu na babaale bapwele, abamavayile Fumu yitu bamafunaange temu tsyotsu.
ACT 5:15 Adine bamabeyilaange bibedu, mba bakebasunzaange mu tsyengi vo mu matoghu mu manzile. Bamavayilaange nane, mumbari ave Pyere ovyoyile, yidumbitsi yandi yikewumbe ne wumosi va ghari owu.
ACT 5:16 Yinombu yineni yimarughaange o misyengi amibambene na Serusaleme. Yinombu yeni yimaghukeme o musyengi Serusaleme. Aghune, bamabeghaange bibedu, na batu abamakwanungu na binyuni bibive, na botsu bamabelughaange.
ACT 5:17 Kaboghu, yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na botsu abamabe nandi, diwendi yi na dibuli di baSadisi, bakebalabe ngusu na bakeghane kake.
ACT 5:18 Va wusu batu botsu, bakebaghaange na bakebabwaghe o tsughu.
ACT 5:19 Tumbe, vane mukolu, yanze yi Fumu yikedibule mune ndaghu, yikebapalise. Yanze yeni, yikebatsingule rye:
ACT 5:20 «Wendanu o ndaghu Nzambi, na tsingulanu mukute mambu motsu ma monyu wughone.»
ACT 5:21 Bilumbi banomawulu, bamawende kedi neni o ndaghu Nzambi na bamalonzaange. Yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na botsu abamabe nandi, bakerughe na bakeghukighe fundu dji banzonzi ba baSwife na bivunde bi dibundu di mukute Yisrayele. Bamatinde batu muyélande bilumbi o tsughu.
ACT 5:22 Tumbe baghore banotole, basamabarasune o tsughu. Bakeghabughe ombu bidjeti muyebatsingule bikumbu. Na bakevose yi:
ACT 5:23 «Tutsirasene tsughu dji dibeme na burange, kale ghore abe va mbure andi va wusu byabutsu. Tumbe ave tutsidjidibulile, tugharasene mutu o ghari.»
ACT 5:24 Banodighulu, yivunde yi baghore ba ndaghu Nzambi na yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu bakekambulu nokewivule adimavyoghe.
ACT 5:25 Mba mutu akibatsingule yi: «Wulwanu! Batu abe dutsisunze o tsughu, badji o ndaghu Nzambi obélonzili batu mambu mowu.»
ACT 5:26 Vane-vane yivunde yi baghore ba ndaghu Nzambi akewende na batu bandi muyéghange bilumbi. Tumbe basamavaghe buvape, mumba bamadumange yi mughungi wukébatinde mamani.
ACT 5:27 Banobabeghe, bakebawakise ombu fundu dji banzonzi. Yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu akebafundise.
ACT 5:28 Djandi akebatsingule yi: «Tumadughandise kile-kingi ulonze mu dine di mutu ewune. Tumbe yi dumavaghe? Dumanyavise ndonzulu enu ombu batu botsu abetsani o musyengi Serusaleme, mba dwirondi usunze dufu du Djesu va djulu muru etu!»
ACT 5:29 Pyere na bilumbi bimosi, bakebawaghule yi: «Diwelimine yi tughobisaange Nzambi, tsiri batu.
ACT 5:30 Nzambi baghulu betu amarambuse Djesu adji djenu dumaghomine va kurusu mu muboke.
ACT 5:31 Nzambi amamumatise o mabaale mandi, mba amamubyatse Yidjeti na Mughobutsi. Amavayile nane, muveghe Yisrayele yese yukalughe dyele nodile dutandu du mabi mandi.
ACT 5:32 Tudji bambedji ba mambu meni, djetu na Yinyuni Yisyeme ayi Nzambi amaveghe abemughobisi.»
ACT 5:33 Bivunde bi fundu dji banzonzi banowulu nane, bakenyoghe tinde unyoghe tena bamaronde ubabokise.
ACT 5:34 Tumbe va ghari owu, vamabe muFarisi wumanengulungu Ghamalyele, mulonzi mighaghe wumaghobusungu na batu botsu. Djandi akereleme va ghari fundu dji banzonzi na akevaghe bakepalise bilumbi mwa temu.
ACT 5:35 Mba aketsingule dibundu yi: «Bise Yisrayele, kebenanu na adi dwirondi uvaghe batu beni bane.
ACT 5:36 Vasekabe yitsingu tumalabe Tedase ureleme vave, amavumbaange wube yidjeti. Tangudji vamabe ne kame-djine (400) tsi batu bamasobene nandi. Tumbe akeboku, botsu abamamuduke baketsyamughe mba vasamasyale ne yisalu mu dighane dyandi.
ACT 5:37 Va djulu vane, va temu sanzeme, tumalabe Sudase mwise Ngalile, amadute tinde bapwele nandi. Tumbe akeboku djawandi, na botsu abamamuduke baketsyamughe.
ACT 5:38 Vave nyidutsinguli: duyamwéghengile ame bévayi, basilyanu bayenewende. Mumba payi matase mowu na bisalu birambuyili ombu batu, byutsyemughe.
ACT 5:39 Tumbe payi birambuyili ombu Nzambi, dughorungule ubipanze. Duyakubene utoghe na Nzambi». Bise dibuli dyeni bakeghululu Ghamalyele.
ACT 5:40 Bakenengile bilumbi, bakebadimbise na mangwangu, bakebaghandise urangune dine di Djesu mba bakebadunde.
ACT 5:41 Bilumbi banodusughe o ndaghu dusosusu. Bamayene wende na nzangu mumbari, bamadjabe yiri Nzambi atsibalabe yi bawelimine ukwanu mu dine di Djesu.
ACT 5:42 Mba kale yilumbu, va dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi na mu ndaghu mowu, bamabwelaange ulonze na uwanze musamu wuboti wu Djesu Kirisete.
ACT 6:1 Mu temu eni, durangu du badukitsi dumafunaange. Kaboghu baSwife abamavosaange mbembu baNgereke, bakengugerene mu djowu abamavosaange mbembu baEberu. Mumbari bakwili ba baNgereke, bamafwimbungu mu bighudji abimaghabungu kale yilumbu.
ACT 6:2 Dighumi na babedji bakenengile yinombu yi badukitsi nobatsingule riye: «Dighadiwelimine yi tukedunde ulonze musamu wu Nzambi mughabaange bighudji.
ACT 6:3 Ladibandu, baane ba tadji, solanu yisambwali yi babaale bavu na bumbedji buboti, babase na Yinyuni Yisyeme na dyele. Tukebaveghe yisalu yeni yine.
ACT 6:4 Tumbe djetu, tuvyosaange temu mu dusambu nolonze musamu Nzambi.»
ACT 6:5 Dibundu dyotsu dikesinge ditase dyeni. Bakesole Yityene, dibaale dibase na Yinyuni Yisyeme, divu na yitu yandi yotsu mu Nzambi. Bakemwésole Filipe, Porekore, Nikanore, Timone, Paremenase na Nikolase, mwise Atyose dji Siri, djandi awu amasinge Nzambi baSwife.
ACT 6:6 Bakebawakise ombu bilumbi, bakebasambilile nobasakighe makake.
ACT 6:7 Mbembu Nzambi djimanyavaange. Durangu du badukitsi dumafunaange o Serusaleme, na pwele bavaghulitsi ba paghu bamavayilaange Djesu yitu.
ACT 6:8 Na mangolu na yese yi Nzambi amamuveghe, Yityene amalasaange bilimbe novaghe bimaghe bineni va ghari mukute.
ACT 6:9 Mwa dikabu di batu, bakemutsundise. Djowu batu ba ndaghu dusambu adjimanengulu «Bavighe abamadjeghusu». Mu ndaweni, mumabe baSwife ba misyengi mi Sirene na Alesanderi. Dikabu dimosi baSwife ba binange bi Silisi na Asi.
ACT 6:10 Tumbe basamarungule ughaghene nandi, mumbari amavosaange na dyele di Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 6:11 Kaboghu bakefute batu muyéfure bumbedji yi: «Tutsimughulu esyengi Moyise na Nzambi.»
ACT 6:12 Anane bamarulile batu botsu, bivunde bi mukute na milonzi mi mighaghe. Mba bakesutusu Yityene nomughange, bakemubeghe va wusu fundu dji banzonzi.
ACT 6:13 Bakebeghe bambedji ba ufure, abamavose yi: «Mutu éwuwu aghedundi ulenze ndaghu adjisyeme dji Nzambi, na mughaghe Moyise!
ACT 6:14 Tutsimughulu evosi yi Djesu mwise Nasarete, opanze ndaghu Nzambi na osanze mutsanu awu Moyise amasile.»
ACT 6:15 Batu botsu abamabe va ghari fundu dji banzonzi, bamalabe yinzi yi Yityene yimabaghunu nane ayi yanze.
ACT 7:1 Mulonzi awuvu yivunde akemuwivule: «Adibevosi mu ndedju, dingenze?»
ACT 7:2 Yityene akewaghule yiri: «Baane ba ngudji na batate nkululwanu, Nzambi bundumbe amalabene na kaaghe etu Aberaame, ave amabile o yinange yi Mesopotami ne akewende o musyengi Arane.
ACT 7:3 Nzambi akemutsingule yiri: “Sile bulongu bwaghu na yifumbe yaghu, na wende o bulongu abu nyuwulase.”
ACT 7:4 Na vane Aberaame akedjusughe bulongu bu Babilone na akewende oyétsane o musyengi Arane. Mba tadji Aberaame anofu, Nzambi akemubeghe o bulongu bughone abu dwitsanini na nyangu.
ACT 7:5 Nzambi asamamuveghe disyale, ne mwa mbure djusunzile ditambi o bulongu bweni. Tumbe, amamuveghe pangini djudile bulongu bwotsu, djandi na bakule bandi. Yotsu yine, Aberaame mbé asekabe na baane.
ACT 7:6 Nzambi amamutsingule rye: “Baane na bateghule baghu boyétsane o bulongu bu bweni, awu bobile bavighe na botsoghusulu mu kame-djine (400) tsi bilime.
ACT 7:7 Tumbe menu Nzambi, nyusosise mukute awu djowu bobile bavighe. Na vane, bopale o bulongu bu buvighe, na bondumise va mbure eni djidji.”
ACT 7:8 Nzambi amatunge pangini na Aberaame. Yilimbe yi pangini eni, urebe mwane. Mbana, Aberaame akerebe mwane andi Yisaake mu yilumbu yi munana. Yisake akerebe Sakobe wandi. Sakobe akerebe bandi baane, abavu dighumi na bifumbe bibedji bi bakaaghe betu.
ACT 7:9 Bakaaghe betu bamavine mwane tadji owu Sosefe na bakemusumbise. Sosefe akenebeghu o bulongu bu Yisipete. Tumbe Nzambi amabe nandi.
ACT 7:10 Akemughobule mu ditsoghe. Akemuveghe dyele na yese va wusu Farawu, kaghe Yisipete omamusole murumitsi Yisipete na ndaghu andi djotsu.
ACT 7:11 Dungosu du nzale dukerughe o bulongu bu Yisipete na bu Kanane. Batu bamatsoghe pwele, ladibandu batadji betu basamamwédile bighudji.
ACT 7:12 Sakobe anowulu yiri wudji bighudji o Yisipete, aketinde bane bandi wune, bakaaghe betu kumbu adji teghe.
ACT 7:13 Adjimubedji, Sosefe akekedjabise na baane ba ngudji bandi. Na yilombi yandi yikedjabunu na Kaghe Farawu.
ACT 7:14 Sosefe akenengile tadji andi Sakobe na yifumbe yandi yotsu. Djobotsu bamabe maghumi-dusambwali ma batu na batu baranu (75).
ACT 7:15 Sakobe akewende o Yisipete. Akefwile wune, na bakaaghe betu wandi.
ACT 7:16 Bakenebeghe bivisi bi bakaaghe bowu o musyengi Siseme noyétsighe o ngile adji Aberaame amasumbe na dufunu du mbongu na baane ba Emore tadji Siseme.
ACT 7:17 Temu adji Nzambi amavangene na Aberaame djinobambene, mukute etu wumafune o Yisipete.
ACT 7:18 Mba kaghe djighone adjisamadjabe Sosefe, akebonge yitsighe yi bukaghe bu Yisipete.
ACT 7:19 Kaghe eni akedyonge bakaaghe betu, akebatsoyise o buvighe, tena amasile bane bowu ufu.
ACT 7:20 Va temu eni, Moyise akeburu, mwane wumabe tinde ubwedji va wusu Nzambi. Amabungulu mu miweli miryeru va kane tadji andi.
ACT 7:21 Anopalusu na biburu byandi, mwane mughetu wu Kaghe Farawu akemubonge na akemubungule nane mwane andi.
ACT 7:22 Moyise akebungulu na dyele di bise Yisipete, mbana akebe dibaale dighobusu mu posulu na bisalu byandi.
ACT 7:23 Anobe na maghumi-mana ma bilime (40), akeghane kake djuyélabe baane ba ngudji andi bandi, baYisrayele.
ACT 7:24 Anolabe yiri mwise Yisipete yike wandi etsoyisi, akemuwamuse notoyise mwise Yisipete nomuboke.
ACT 7:25 Amatase yiri baane ba ngudji bandi bowulu yiri Nzambi obaveghe dughobutsu mu djandi, tumbe basamadidjabe.
ACT 7:26 Yilumbu ayimaduke, Moyise akebengune na batu babedji bamatoghaange. Anoronde ughabuse duvotsu va ghari owu, akebatsingule rye: “Bambatsi, dudji baane ba ngudji, dibandu yi dibokisini nane?”
ACT 7:27 Omatsoyisaange mbatsi andi, akesindile Moyise novose: “Anyi atsyusole mube yivunde na nzonzi va ghari etu?
ACT 7:28 Wirondi umboke menu wandi, nane wutsibokile mwise Yisipete masighe?”
ACT 7:29 Mu posulu tsyeni, Moyise akerine, aketsane o bulongu bu Madyane. Akebure bane babedji wune.
ACT 7:30 Maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime manovyoghe, o kumu dukange beli na mukongu wu Sinayi, yanze yi Nzambi yikelabene nandi o ghari mulutsu diningi adimalulaange.
ACT 7:31 Moyise akesutu mune amalabile nane, tumbe ave amabambenine mu labe burange, akewulu dyufi di Fumu dimavosaange yi:
ACT 7:32 “Menu nyidji Nzambi baghulu baghu, Nzambi Aberaame, Nzambi Yisaake na Nzambi Sakobe.” Noregheme, Moyise asamarungule ughengile.
ACT 7:33 Kaboghu Fumu akemuvaghe yi: “Vule bapondu baghu, mumba wudji va mbure djisyeme.
ACT 7:34 Nyimalabe nane batu bami bétsoghusulu o bulongu bu Yisipete. Nyimawulu mighamu myowu, nyirughe muyibaghobule. Tsyéwendi, nyiwutindi o Yisipete.”
ACT 7:35 Awuwu, Moyise, dibaale adi baane ba Yisrayele bamaghale novose yi: “Anyi atsyusole mube yivunde na nzonzi va ghari etu?” Nzambi amamutinde nane yivunde na mughobutsi wu mukute andi, va yinzime yi yanze ayimalabene nandi mu diningi.
ACT 7:36 Moyise omapalise baane ba Yisrayele o bulongu bu Yisipete, novaghe bimaghe na bilimbe bipwele o bulongu bweni, o Mubu Wubenge, teno dukange. Mambu motsu mane, mamadughusu mu maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime.
ACT 7:37 Moyise, dibaale adimatsingule mukute Yisrayele yi: “Va ghari mukute enu, Nzambi opalise mubiyitsi nane menu.”
ACT 7:38 Ave mughungi wu Yisrayele wumabile o dukange, Moyise djandi amabe va ghari baghulu betu na yanze, ayimavosaange nandi o mukongu wu Sinayi. Akedile musamu Nzambi awiveyi monyu, mu tudjabise woni.
ACT 7:39 Tumbe baghulu betu basamaronde umuwululu. Bakemuwengule na nzale ughabughe o Yisipete.
ACT 7:40 Baketsingule Arone: “Tuvayili banyambi aboyenewendaange va wusu etu, mumbari tughedjabi aditsiruyile Moyise, otsitupalise o Yisipete.”
ACT 7:41 Baketule kosi mu yibaghunu yi mwane ngombi na bakevaghule paghu va wusu andi. Bakevaghe mumengu mu yime ayi djobeni bamatule.
ACT 7:42 Nzambi akebaliyili nzime, nobasile uyitse batsungi na bambwelili, nane disonunu mu mughande babiyitsi: “Mukute Yisrayele, tsiri ombu menu dumayivaghulili paghu tsyenu na bisaku, mu temu adjidumabile, mu maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime o dukange.
ACT 7:43 Nesi, dumabeghe disambe di nyambi enu Moloke, na yibaghunu yi mbwelili nyambi enu Refane. Abine, bime abi dumatule mu biyitsaange. Ladibandu, nyudubeyile nane bise tsughu o vale, uvyoghe bulongu bu Babilone.”
ACT 7:44 Mu kumu dukange, baghulu betu bamabe na ndaghu yibengunu. Moyise amadjirunge nane Nzambi amamusindiyile bwé akedjivaghe, mu yibaghunu ayi amalabe.
ACT 7:45 Baghulu betu bamadile ndaghu eni. Mu dirume di Sosye, bakedjibeghe o bulongu bu batu abe Nzambi amasanze va wusu owu. Djikebe vane tena temu kaghe Davide.
ACT 7:46 Djandi wughu akedile yese va wusu Nzambi. Akevonde musughe wurunge ndaghu djisyeme dji Nzambi Sakobe.
ACT 7:47 Tumbe mwane andi Salemu amamurungile djoni.
ACT 7:48 Yotsu yine Nzambi-Pungu, aghétsani mu mandaghu amarungu na makake ma batu. Mubiyitsi evosi yi:
ACT 7:49 “Divose Fumu Nzambi rye: Djulu yitsighe yi bukaghe bwami, Butambe yisunzulu yi makulu mami. Munongu ndaghu yi durungule utungile? Vo mbure yi djurungule ube yivumunu yami?
ACT 7:50 Byotsu bine, tsiri mebeni nyimabisunde na makake mami?”
ACT 7:51 Dune kande, mirime myenu mighale na matudji menu madibe va wusu mbile Nzambi! Dughededili Yinyuni Yisyeme! Dudji nane bakaaghe benu.
ACT 7:52 Mubiyitsi awu batadji benu basamakwane anyi? Bamaboke abamabighe durughulu du Mutu awusungeme. Mutu eni wune, dumamusumbise nomuboke.
ACT 7:53 Byanze bimaduveghe mughaghe Nzambi, tumbe dumabuse uwughobise!»
ACT 7:54 Ave bamawululu posulu tsyeni, fundu dji banzonzi djikenyoyile Yityene. Na kabu, bakevaghaange duweriti na minu mowu.
ACT 7:55 Tumbe Yityene, abasilange na Yinyuni Yisyeme, akeghengile o djulu, akelabe kembu Nzambi na Djesu diteli va mabaale mandi.
ACT 7:56 Akevaghe yi: «Wulwanu, nyilabi djulu djidibughe na Mwane mutu diteli va mabaale ma Nzambi!»
ACT 7:57 Kaboghu, bakebwaghe mughamu wuneni nodibighe matudji. Bakeyémuvike djowu botsu.
ACT 7:58 Bakemupalise o musyengi nomutinde mamani bakemuboke. Bambedji bamasile bidwaru byowu na mwa mwane dibaale, wumanengulungu Sole.
ACT 7:59 Ave bamamutindilaange mamani, Yityene akesambilaange yi: «Fumu Djesu, wake yinyuni yami!»
ACT 7:60 Mba akekuteme noghamughe na mangolu mandi motsu: «Fumu, batandi dibi dyédidi!» Yikemani, akefu.
ACT 8:1 Mba Sole amarondaange dufu du Yityene. Mune yilumbu akevyosulile ukwane dibundu di Serusaleme. Badukitsi botsu, uvenguse bilumbi, bakepanzighe mu byari byotsu bi Sudé na Samari.
ACT 8:2 Batu abamaghobisaange Nzambi baketswighe Yityene na bakemulile tinde na munyongu.
ACT 8:3 Sole, djandi, akevataange upanze dibundu. Amawendaange ndaghu na ndaghu, akeghangaange bango yitu, na baghetu na babaale, akebabwaghaange o tsughu.
ACT 8:4 Bango yitu abamatsyamughe bamanangaange bulongu, noyenelonzaange musamu wuboti.
ACT 8:5 Filipe akewende o musyengi Samari, akebasamunine Kirisete.
ACT 8:6 Mighungi na mighungi va mosi mimawulu posulu tsi Filipe, mumba mimawulu nolabe bilimbe bi bimaghe abi amavaghaange.
ACT 8:7 Na mighamu mineni, binyuni bibive bipwele bimapalaange mu batu. Bibomfi bipwele na bitsondu bimabelusu.
ACT 8:8 Kaboghu nzangu djikebe djineni mu musyengi eni.
ACT 8:9 Mutu winengulu Simu amaba vane kale o musyengi eni, amavandaange. Mavande mandi mamasutusungu mughungi wotsu wu Samari. Amakelabange nderi adji muneni.
ACT 8:10 Mba botsu, ubongile o bangebi teno bivunde, bamamughobisaange pwele. Bamavosaange yi: «Mutu éwuwu mangolu ma Nzambi, amenengulu “Mboboghe”.»
ACT 8:11 Bamamughobisaange pwele, mumba mbé amatsinge nobasutusu na mavande mandi.
ACT 8:12 Tumbe banosinge musamu wuboti awu Filipe amasamunaange, mu dyambu di Bukaghe bu Nzambi na mu dine di Djesu Kirisete, baghetu na babaale bakebatusu.
ACT 8:13 Djabeni Simu akesinge Djesu na akebatusu. Mune amalabilaange bimaghe bineni na bilimbe abi Filipe amavaghaange, amasutu na asamamwékakenange nandi.
ACT 8:14 Bilumbi o Serusaleme bakewulu yi bise Samari bamadile musamu Nzambi na nzangu. Adine bamabatindile Pyere na San.
ACT 8:15 Banotole o Samari, bakesambilile mu djowu abamasinge Nzambi, mumbari bakedile Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 8:16 Ne vane babatusulungu mu dine di Fumu Djesu, Yinyuni Yisyeme mbé yisekasundughe ne mu wumosi va ghari owu.
ACT 8:17 Pyere na San bakebasakighe makake na bakedile Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 8:18 Simu anolabe yi Yinyuni Yisyeme yiveghu ombu bango yitu ave bilumbi bebasakiyili makake akeronde ubaveghe badoli.
ACT 8:19 Amabavaghe yi: «Peyanu ngudu, yi abe nyusakighaange makake bakedilaange Yinyuni Yisyeme.»
ACT 8:20 Tumbe Pyere akemuwaghule yi: «Badoli baghu babungini na ndebeni, mumba wutsitase bwé peghulu dji Nzambi djisumbu na mbongu!
ACT 8:21 Wughane dikabu vo musughe mu yisalu yéyiyi, mumba murime aghu wughaa wusungeme va wusu Nzambi.
ACT 8:22 Vughule ditase dyaghu dibive na lende Fumu, lake pa dyurungule uvaghu, akewutande mu ditase dyédine.
ACT 8:23 Mumba nyilabi na ngenze, yi wudji wubase na mele mabive mba wune mutsanu wubi.»
ACT 8:24 Kaboghu Simu akevaghe Pyere na San yi: «Djenubeni lendanu Fumu, yiri motsu dutsivose makétuyile.»
ACT 8:25 Yikebémani ughabuse bumbedji nosamune Musamu wu Fumu, bilumbi bibedji bakeghabughe o Serusaleme. Mu nzile bakeyenelonzaange Musamu Wuboti mu mimbu mapwele ma Samari.
ACT 8:26 Yanze yi Fumu yikevaghe Filipe yiri: «Releme, wende o yari yibande, mu nzile adjirambuyili o Serusaleme teno musyengi Ghase. Nzile adjivu mududu, djighémwévyoghulu na batu.»
ACT 8:27 Filipe akereleme, akewende na maswasu. Mu nzile, akebengune na muvangu wu Yityopi, yidjeti yineni yimakelisaange yilundulu yi Kandase, kaghe mughetu dji Yityopi. Djandi amarughe o Serusaleme mu yiyitse Nzambi,
ACT 8:28 na yikewughabughe amaghabughaange o dimbu dyandi. Amabe atsane va djulu dikalu dyandi dimayenedutungu na kabele. Na vane, amarangaange yibuku yi musamu wu mubiyitsi Yisayi.
ACT 8:29 Yinyuni Yisyeme yiketsingule Filipe bwé: «Bambene na dikalu dyédine.»
ACT 8:30 Filipe amabambene mbangu-mbangu na akewulu yidjeti yi Yityopi, yimarangaange dibuku di mubiyitsi Yisayi na dyufi dineni. Akemuwivule yi: «Wighulu na bureti amewirangi?»
ACT 8:31 Yidjeti yeni akemuwaghule yiri: «Tsyeni nyurungulile uwulu, ta vagha mutu wupindiyile?» Vane-vane, amavaghe Filipe akenangeme notsane va mughule andi.
ACT 8:32 Yibuku yi Bisonu ayi amarangaange ayiyi: «Amaba nane yindombu ayi bébeyi o uboke, Nane mwane yindombu awibi dibabe va wusu mufuyitsi, asamadibule munu andi.
ACT 8:33 Amalenzu mba musughe andi wumadesu. Kule andi, anyi odjirangemine? Mumba batsimutabule monyu va butambe.»
ACT 8:34 Yidjeti akewivule Filipe yi: «Kokolu, nzinguli anyi mubiyitsi eranguni nane, djabeni ekevosile vo mutu susu?»
ACT 8:35 Filipe akemuwaghule, akemutsingule musamu wuboti wu Djesu, ubandile vane dibandu di Yibuku yeni yi Bisonu.
ACT 8:36 Bakebwele wuwende na baketole va mbure djimabe mambe. Yidjeti akevaghe yi: «Labati mudjambe! Kaboghu wurungule umbatise, mbeyé?» [
ACT 8:37 Filipe akemuvaghe yi: «Payi wune tinde yitu, wurungule ubatusu.» Yidjeti akewaghule yi: «Yine, nine yitu mu Djesu Kirisete, Mwane Nzambi.»]
ACT 8:38 Yidjeti akesikighe dikalu, bakesundughe djone Filipe mu mudjambe. Na Filipe akemubatise.
ACT 8:39 Banosabughe, Yinyuni yi Fumu yiketsyemuse Filipe. Yidjeti asamamwémulabe, tumbe akeduke nzile andi na nzangu.
ACT 8:40 Filipe akepalile o dimbu di Asote, mba akevyoghe misyengi na misyengi, noyenesamunaange Musamu Wuboti mbure tsyotsu tena ave amatole o yisyeni yi Sesaré.
ACT 9:1 Mu temu eni, Sole amakwanaange pwele na amaghanaange uboke badukitsi ba Fumu. Amayérasene yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu,
ACT 9:2 nomuvonde mighande mi musughe wuwendile o mandaghu ma tsambu ma baSwife mu musyengi Damase. Na payi atsirasene babaale vo baghetu abeduki nzile Djesu, obaghange nobabeghe o Serusaleme.
ACT 9:3 Abilaange mu nzile Damase, akebambene beli na musyengi. Sundile, yidjalale yinene ayi masundughe o djulu yikemuvedemine.
ACT 9:4 Akeyideme vatsi, na akewulu dyufi dimavosile rye: «Sole, Sole, dibandu yi winkwanini?»
ACT 9:5 Akewivule: «Nde la nyi, Fumu?» Na dyufi dimamuwawule rye: «Menu la Djesu, awu wikwani.
ACT 9:6 Tumbe releme, kote o musyengi, aghune bowutsingule adiwudusu.»
ACT 9:7 Bambatsi ba mulingu ba Sole bamasikeme, bamaghambu na dyambu dyuvose. Bamawulu dyufi, tumbe basamalabe mutu.
ACT 9:8 Sole amareleme na amadibule misu, tumbe asamamwélabaange ne yime. Bamamughange mu dikake mu mubeghe o Damase.
ACT 9:9 Mu bilumbu biryeru, asamarungule ulabe na amatsane nane, vagha wudji nonu.
ACT 9:10 Wumabe o Damase mudukitsi wumosi dine dyandi Nanyase. Fumu amalabene nandi mu yiryaryamu na akemunengile: «Nanyase!» Akewaghule: «Me djanduwu, Fumu.»
ACT 9:11 Fumu akemutsingule rye: «Lenge nowende mu nzile adjinengulu “Nzile Djisungeme”, o ndaghu Sudase. Aghune, wuyéwivule dibaale, mwise Tarese oyinengulu Sole. Usambile esambili.
ACT 9:12 Mu yiryaryamu, atsilabe dibaale dinengulu Nanyase, atsikotaange nomusakighe makake mumba akebwélabe.»
ACT 9:13 Nanyase amawaghule rye: «Fumu, batu bapwele bamaposile mu dibaale dyeni na nyidjabi dibi adi amavaghe mu bango yitu o Serusaleme.
ACT 9:14 Na atsirughe wunu na musughe awu amasingusulu na bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, muyighange botsu abeyitsi dine dyaghu.»
ACT 9:15 Tumbe Fumu aketsingule Nanyase: «Wende, mumbari nyimasole dibaale dyédine, mube musalitsi ami. Na djandi odjabise dine dyami mu malongu masusu, na bakaghe bowu, na mu mukute Yisrayele.
ACT 9:16 Nyumulase mebeni maghughe motsu ame olabe mu dyambu dyami.»
ACT 9:17 Yike Nanyase amawende. Akekote o ghari ndaghu, akemusakighe makake, na akemutsingule rye: «Sole, mwane tadji ami, Fumu Djesu otsilabene naghu mu nzile ave wutsiruyilaange, atsinzindighe ombu aghu. Motsu mane, mumba wukebwélabe na wukebasu na Yinyuni Yisyeme.»
ACT 9:18 Vane-vane, bime bibaghunu na maghaghele bimabondughe mu misu ma Sole na amamwélabe. Amareleme na amabatusu.
ACT 9:19 Anodji, mangolu mandi, mamamughabuyile. Sole amatsane mwa bilumbu na badukitsi abamabe o Damase.
ACT 9:20 Vane-vane, Sole amabande ulonze mu mandaghu ma tsambu ma baSwife, yiri Djesu adji mwane Nzambi.
ACT 9:21 Botsu abamamuwulungu bamakambulu na bamawivulaange: «Tsi djandi otsikwanaange o Serusaleme botsu abamarangunaange dine di Djesu? Na agharughe wunu mu yibaghange nobabeghe va wusu bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu?»
ACT 9:22 Sole mu posulu tsyandi, amakewarisaange kale yilumbu. Tumbe baSwife ba Damase basamamwébe na dyukale mumbari djandi amabalasaange na kengili yiri Djesu la Kirisete.
ACT 9:23 Mwa pesu temu, baSwife bamaghane kake muboke Sole,
ACT 9:24 tumbe amalubusu mu fundu owu. Makotulu motsu ma musyengi mamakelusungu nyangu na mukolu, mu mubokise.
ACT 9:25 Kaboghu badukitsi ba Sole bamamubeghe mukolu mu muvyose disimu dimosi di yivaghe yi musyengi, na bamamusunduse mu ponzi.
ACT 9:26 Ave Sole amatolile o Serusaleme, djandi mbé aronde ufubene mu dighuki di badukitsi. Tumbe djobotsu bamabe na ghome andi, mumbari vasamabe ne wumosi wumatasaange yiri ngenze Sole amakalughe mudukitsi.
ACT 9:27 Adine Barenabase amamubongile nandi, akemubeghe ombu bilumbi. Barenabase akebwébatsingule nane mu nzile, Sole amalabinine na Fumu, na nane Fumu amavosile nandi. Barenabase amabwese ubatsingule nane Sole o musyengi Damase, amasamunine na musighe mu dine di Djesu.
ACT 9:28 Yike Sole amayenewendaange noghabughe nowu o Serusaleme, na amasamunaange na musighe mu dine di Fumu.
ACT 9:29 Djandi amavosaange notsunde na baSwife abamavosaange mbembu baNgereke, tumbe djowu bamarondaange umubokise.
ACT 9:30 Baane ba tadji bandi banodidjabe, bamabeghe Sole o yisyeni yi Sesaré, na bakemuwendise o yisyeni yi Tarese.
ACT 9:31 Dibundu mu musyengi wotsu wu Sudé, wu Ngalile na wu Samari, dimabe mu duvotsu. Dimaneghaange mu yitu, dimabéghaange monyu mu dighobe di Fumu na dimafunaange na dwamusu du Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 9:32 Pyere wandi, amayenevyoyilangaange mbure tsyotsu, akesundughe ombu bango yitu abamatsanaange o musyengi Lide.
ACT 9:33 Aghune, akerasene dibaale dinengulu Ené dimabe disileme va ditoghu mu yinane yi bilime, mumbari amabe yimbolutu.
ACT 9:34 Yike Pyere akemutsingule: «Ené, Djesu Kirisete eghubelusi! Releme, kunze ditoghu dyaghu.» Sundile Ené akereleme.
ACT 9:35 Ave bamamulabile, batu botsu bamatsanaange o musyengi Lide na kumu Sarone, bamasinge Fumu.
ACT 9:36 Wumabe o musyengi Sopé, mudukitsi mughetu wumanengulu Tabite, vo «Dorkase» o mbembu Ngereke, diwendili bwé «Tsyesi». Amavyosaange temu andi novaghaange bisalu biboti nowamuse bidjaghe.
ACT 9:37 Mu temu eni, amadimbene ubele na akefu. Dunyuru dunobwitsu, dumasunzu o yibuku yi ndaghu ayi djulu.
ACT 9:38 Badukitsi abamabe o musyengi Sopé, badjabilaange yiri Pyere amabe o musyengi Lide, awuvu bébeli na Sopé, Bakemutindile babaale babedji muyémulende: «Wuyabwétsinge, lenge norughe ombu ghetu.»
ACT 9:39 Pyere amawende nowu. Anotole, bamamubeghe o yibuku yi ndaghu ayi djulu. Bakwili botsu bamabambene nandi nolile. Bamamulase bikutu na bilinge, abi Dorkase amavaghaange ave amabilaange monyu.
ACT 9:40 Pyere akepalise batu botsu, akekuteme na akesambile. Mba amaghelughe o yari yi mvumbi novose rye: «Tabite, releme!» Lake Tabite akedibule misu, anolabe Pyere, akesimbughe na aketsane.
ACT 9:41 Pyere amamuveghe dikake na akemuwamuse ureleme. Amanengile bango yitu na bakwili, na amabalase Tabite monyu.
ACT 9:42 Dimadjabunu mu musyengi wotsu wu Sopé na bapwele bamavayile Fumu yitu.
ACT 9:43 O musyengi eni, Pyere amatsane yitsingu yineni ombu Ngele-Bibande, djinengulu Simu.
ACT 10:1 O Sesaré wumabe dibaale dimanengulungu Korneye. Amabe yivunde yi kame baghore mu dibuli adimanengulungu «Mughungi baghore ba Yitali.»
ACT 10:2 Amabe na dinonge na amadumaange Nzambi na kane andi djotsu. Amawamusaange bidjaghe bi baSwife na amasambilaange Nzambi temu tsyotsu.
ACT 10:3 Mwa yilumbu, va murekemunu wisi va tsisighe, beli na maweru maryeru, amadile yiryaryamu. Na tsiyiri akelabe yanze yi Nzambi ukote ombu wandi na akemunengile yi: «Korneye!»
ACT 10:4 Akeghengile na dunzyenzi na akewaghule rye: «Fumu, dyambu yi?» Yanze nomuwaghule yi: «Nzambi atsironde tsambu tsyaghu na dwamusu adu wiveyi bidjaghe, na eghurangemini.
ACT 10:5 Tumbe, sindighe batu o musyengi Sopé, bakénengile Simu awu bénengili Pyere.
ACT 10:6 Etsani ombu Simu Ngele-Bibande, ndaghu andi djidji va mughule mubu.»
ACT 10:7 Yike yanze ayimavose nandi yiwendi, Korneye akenengile basatsi bandi babedji na ghore mosi djimamusalilaange, adjimabe mutu wunonge na Nzambi.
ACT 10:8 Akebatsingule motsu amamavyoghe mba akebatinde o Sopé.
ACT 10:9 Yilumbu ayimaduke, yotsu yine mbé baki mu nzile ave bamabambeninaange na musyengi Sopé, Pyere akemate o djulu ndaghu mu yésambile, va diweru di mwangulu.
ACT 10:10 Akewulu nzale, mbé aronde udji. Temu adji bamamulambilaange bighudji, akelabe yiryaryamu.
ACT 10:11 Amalabe djulu djimadibughe, na yime yimasundughaange. Yime yeni yimabe nane yibuku yi tsande djineni, djighangu mu kodu tsyotsu tsi djine, adjimasundughe tena vatsi.
ACT 10:12 Mu tsande eni, mumabe minongu myotsu mi bibulu abivu na biname bina, minongu myotsu mi bilandile bi butambe, na minongu myotsu mi batsoli.
ACT 10:13 Akewulu dyufi dimamuvosile yiri: «Pyere, releme! Boke bibulu byébibi na djange!»
ACT 10:14 Tumbe Pyere akewake: «Tsatsabi! Fumu ami, nyisekadjangaange abivu yingitsi vo binzoruru.»
ACT 10:15 Dyufi dikemwéghulunu nandi adi mubedji, na dikevose yiri: «Abi Nzambi amalyomise, ndedju wuyabilabe nzoruru.»
ACT 10:16 Dyoni dimalabene kumbu yiryeru, mba yime yeni yikematusu o djulu.
ACT 10:17 Pyere amakewivulaange divindughulu di yiryaryamu ayi abenolabe. Vane-vane, batu abe Korneye amatinde, banomane uwivule mu djabe ave ndaghu Simu Ngele-Bibande djivu, baketole va dikotulu.
ACT 10:18 Bamadukise na bamawivule rye: «Avave Simu adjinengulu Pyere etsanini?»
ACT 10:19 Pyere wukelule mbé akikelule yiryaryamu yandi, ave Yinyuni yimamutsingulile yiri: «Wulu, vadji batu baryeru béwurombi.
ACT 10:20 Releme, vindeme na wende nowu, wuyatsikedene, mumba menu nyibasindiyi.»
ACT 10:21 Pyere akevindeme ombu batu beni nobatsingule yi: «Nyidjandughu, menu dirombi. Dibandu yi dutsiruyile?»
ACT 10:22 Bakewaghule yi: «Tutsitindu na Korneye, yivunde yi baghore. Dibaale disungeme, didumi Nzambi, na baSwife botsu bémurondi. Yanze yi Nzambi yimayimuveghe dilongi dyédidi: “Nengile Pyere o ndaghu aghu na wulu motsu ame owutsingule.”»
ACT 10:23 Pyere akebakotise o ghari ndaghu na akebaveghe bitsighe byuvyosile mukolu. Va kedi dji yilumbu ayimadukaange, Pyere amasimbughe na amawende nowu. Baane ba tadji bamosi ba Sopé bamawende nandi.
ACT 10:24 Djowu bamatole o musyengi Sesaré mu yilumbu ayi mubedji. Korneye amabavivaange na biburu byandi na bambatsi bandi ba murime, abe amanengile.
ACT 10:25 Ave Pyere amatolile, Korneye akémubengusunu, amakébwaghe va makulu mandi mu muyitse.
ACT 10:26 Tumbe Pyere akemurelighe nomutsingule yi: «Releme! Mumbari menu nyidji mutu nane ndedju.»
ACT 10:27 Va djulu vane, amayenevosaange na Korneye. Anokote o ghari ndaghu, amarasunu batu bapwele baghukeme.
ACT 10:28 Akebatsingule rye: «Dwidjabi yi muSwife aghane musughe wube mbatsi mweni, vo mu ukote o ndaghu andi. Tumbe Nzambi atsindonze yi, vagha mutu awu menu nyurungule wulabe yiri adji nzoruru vo agha awelimine ufwamu.
ACT 10:29 Ladibandu, ave dutsitindile batu o wuyindengile, ngalabe diweru mu urughe. Kaboghu, nyirondi udjabe adi dutsindengilile.»
ACT 10:30 Korneye akewaghule yiri: «Vake bilumbu bina, va temu dji maweru maryeru ma tsisighe, nyimasambilaange. Suka, mutu na bikutu bikademi akepale va wusu ami.
ACT 10:31 Akenzingule: “Korneye, dusambu dwaghu dumadughusu, na Nzambi atsirangemine dwamusu du maboti amewivayili bidjaghe.
ACT 10:32 Kaboghu sindighe mutu o Sopé mu uyenengile Simu awu bénengili Pyere. Etsani ombu Simu mosi, Ngele-Bibande adjitsani va mughule mubu.”
ACT 10:33 Nzilenge notinde batu mu yiwulande na wutsisinge urughe. Vave, tudji djetu botsu va wusu Nzambi, mughulu motsu ame Fumu atsiwurume mu yitutsingule.»
ACT 10:34 Anane Pyere amabongile mbembu novose yiri: «Mba nyimawulu bwé Nzambi aghane dupasu du batu.
ACT 10:35 Mu malongu motsu, mutu awidumi Nzambi na avu asungeme, awune awelimine usingu nandi.
ACT 10:36 Amatindile bise Yisrayele mbembu andi, mu yitusamune Musamu Wuboti wu duvotsu adutumadile mu Djesu Kirisete, odjivu Fumu batu botsu.
ACT 10:37 Dwidjabi adimarele uvyoghe o Ngalile, mba dikebwélabene mu Sudé djotsu. Motsu mane mamavyoyile, yike San emani usamune musamu wu dubatusu.
ACT 10:38 Dwidjabi nane Nzambi amasolile Djesu mwise Nasarete, nomuveghe mangolu ma Yinyuni Yisyeme. Dwidjabi wandi nane Djesu amanangile bulongu, noyenevaghaange diboti noghobulaange botsu abamabe baghangu na dyabu, mumba Nzambi amabe nandi.
ACT 10:39 Mba djetu, tudji bambedji ba motsu ame amavaghe o bulongu bu baSwife, teno Serusaleme. Djandi awu bamabokise, nomulelighe va kurusu.
ACT 10:40 Tumbe Nzambi, amamurambuse o dufu yilumbu ayimuryeru, na amavaghe yi akelabene.
ACT 10:41 Asamalabene na mikute myotsu, tumbe yike na djetu abe Nzambi amasole vane dibandu mube bambedji. Anorambughe, tumadji nonu nandi.
ACT 10:42 Amaturume ulonze Musamu Wuboti, ombu mukute na utsiyise yi, adji mutu awu Nzambi amabyatse, mu ufundise abavu monyu na abafu.
ACT 10:43 Babiyitsi botsu bamavose mu djandi, botsu abemuvayili yitu, bodile dutandu du mabi dibandu djandi.»
ACT 10:44 Pyere uvose mbé akivose, Yinyuni Yisyeme yikesundughe mu botsu abamawulungu musamu Nzambi.
ACT 10:45 Bango yitu abamabe barebu, abamarughe na Pyere, bakekambulu mu ulabe yi, peghulu Yinyuni Yisyeme djimaghabulu djowu botsu abasamabe baSwife.
ACT 10:46 Ngenze, bango yitu abarebu, bamabawulungu uvose mu mambembu masusu noyitse Nzambi. Kaboghu Pyere akevose yi:
ACT 10:47 «Tughorungule ughandise batu bébabe dubatusu du mambe, badililaange Yinyuni Yisyeme nane djetu!»
ACT 10:48 Na akeveghe musughe ubabatise mu dine di Djesu Kirisete. Kaboghu bakemuwivule aketsane mwa bilumbu nowu.
ACT 11:1 Bilumbi na baane ba tadji abamabe o yinange yi Sudé, bakewulu bwendiri bise malongu wandi bamadile musamu Nzambi.
ACT 11:2 Ave Pyere amamatile o Serusaleme, bango yitu abarebu bamamutsundise
ACT 11:3 novose rye: «Ndedju wutsikote ombu batu abagha batabulu, na wutsidji va mosi nowu!»
ACT 11:4 Yike Pyere akebatsingule na musighe, mambu motsu, ubongile o dibandu teno disukusulu, akebatsingule rye:
ACT 11:5 «Menu, nyimabe o musyengi Sopé na nyimasambililaange, nganingelene na ngadile yiryaryamu. Lake ngalabe yime nane yibuku yi tsande djineni, djighangu mu kodu tsyotsu tsi djine, djimasundughaange o djulu na djikerughe tena va wusu ami.
ACT 11:6 Nyimadjitsune na burange na nyimalabe bibulu abivu na biname bina, minongu myotsu mi bibulu bi musiru, minongu myotsu mi bilandile bi butambe na batsoli.
ACT 11:7 Mba nyimawulu dyufi dimapaghe yi: “Pyere, releme! Boke bibulu byébibi na djange!”
ACT 11:8 Tumbe nyimawaghule yi: “Tsatsabi! Fumu ami, mumbari nyiburulu, nyisekadjangaange bibabi vo abivu yingitsi. Mumba byoni, bighorungule ukote o munu ami.”
ACT 11:9 Mu dyoni, mbembu eni djimawulunu o djulu, djimabwéposile adi mubedji yi: “Abi Nzambi amalyomise, ndedju wuyabilabe nzoruru.”
ACT 11:10 Dyoni dimalabene kumbu yiryeru, mba byotsu bikeghabughe o djulu.»
ACT 11:11 Pyere akebwese uvose: «Vane-vane, babaale baryeru bamarughesene o musyengi Sesaré mu yimbonge, bamatole va wusu ndaghu adjitumabe.
ACT 11:12 Yike, Yinyuni yimanzingule bwé wende nowu, wuyabe némwapesu na keri. Na baane ba tadji ba syamunu ababe, bamayinkelise, na tumakote djetu botsu ombu dibaale dyédidi.
ACT 11:13 Djandi amatutsingule nane amalabile yanze o ghari ndaghu andi, ayi yimabe vane, na yimamutsingule yiri: “Sindighe mutu o musyengi Sopé, akéwunengilile Simu awu bénengili Pyere.
ACT 11:14 Djandi oyiwutsingule musamu, awu ndedju na ndaghu aghu djotsu, dughobululu.”
ACT 11:15 Ave nyimabandile uvose, Yinyuni Yisyeme yikesundughe mu djowu botsu, nane yimasunduyile mu djetu va dibandu.
ACT 11:16 Yike nyimarangemine mbembu Fumu adjimavosaange yi: “San amabatise mu mambe, tumbe djenu, dubatusu mu Yinyuni Yisyeme.”
ACT 11:17 Nzambi amabaveghe yisaku yine yimosi, nane amatuveyile djetu wandi, ave tumasunzile yitu yetu mu Fumu Djesu Kirisete. Tumbe anyi menu mbé nyimabe, murungule ughaghene na Nzambi?»
ACT 11:18 Banowulu yilombi yeni, bango yitu abamabe barebu, bakevole «swii», bakesigheme. Djowu botsu bakeyitse Nzambi novose rye: «Kaboghu dingenze, Nzambi amaveghe bise malongu wandi abagha barebu, yese yukalughe mutsanu wubive, mu dile monyu mutubu na mutubu.»
ACT 11:19 Yityene anoboku, bango yitu bamapanzighe dibandu dikwane, adimaduke dufu dwandi. Na djobotsu bamawende yari na yari: abane o yinange Fenisi, bamosi o ningi dji Sipere na o musyengi Antyose. Tumbe bamayenesamunaange musamu Nzambi, yike ombu djowu abamabe baSwife.
ACT 11:20 Yike va ghari owu, vamabe bise Sipere na Sirene, djowu bakerughe o musyengi Antyose. Bamayenesamunaange Musamu Wuboti wu Fumu Djesu ombu djowu abamavosaange mbembu baNgereke.
ACT 11:21 Mangolu ma Fumu mamabe nowu, adine bapwele bamasinge Fumu Djesu na bamakalughe mutsanu owu.
ACT 11:22 Bivunde bi dibundu di Serusaleme banowulu yilumbi yeni, baketinde Barenabase o musyengi Antyose.
ACT 11:23 Anotole wune, ave amalabile motsu ame yese yi Nzambi yimadughusu, amabase na nzangu djineni. Na vane, amawarise bango yitu botsu bakesunze yitu yowu mu Fumu, na bakébwéghabughe manzinzime.
ACT 11:24 Barenabase amabangaange dibaale adisungeme, dibase na Yinyuni Yisyeme, divu na yitu yandi yotsu mu Nzambi. Yinombu yineni yimasinge Fumu Djesu mu monyu owu.
ACT 11:25 Mba Barenabase amawende o musyengi Tarese oyérombe Sole.
ACT 11:26 Ave amamulabile, akemubeghe o musyengi Antyose. Djobotsu bakevyose yilime yifwimbe o dibundu, nolonzaange batu bapwele yitu mu Nzambi. Aghune dibundu di Antyose, badukitsi bamanengululu aditeghe: «Bakereti».
ACT 11:27 Mune temu eni, babiyitsi bamadusughe musyengi Serusaleme mu wende o musyengi Antyose.
ACT 11:28 Mubiyitsi wumosi wumanengulu Aghabise, abasu na Yinyuni Yisyeme, amabighe bwé nzale djineni djube mu butambe bwotsu. Yike nzale eni djimalabene va temu adji Kolode amabile kaghe.
ACT 11:29 Badukitsi bamakape disite, bwé kale mutu mbé oveghaange nane odilile na mangolu mandi, mu wamuse baane ba tadji abamatsanaange o yinange yi Sudé.
ACT 11:30 Anane bamavayile. Baketinde Barenabase djone Sole bakebeghe dwamusu dweni, ombu bivunde bi dibundu di Sudé.
ACT 12:1 Va temu eni, kaghe Yirode akeghangise mwa dikabu di batu ba dibundu mu bakwane.
ACT 12:2 Na didjenge akebokise Sake, mwane ngudji San.
ACT 12:3 Anolabe yi baSwife bamadironde, akeghangise Pyere va temu mumengu wu bapembi abagha dufunusu.
ACT 12:4 Yirode akemughaange nomusunze o tsughu. Akesindighe binombu bine bi baghore mu mukelisaange. Kadi yinombu yimabe ghore djine. Amabe na ditase dyumufundise, va ghari batu yike mumengu Pake wivyoyi.
ACT 12:5 Pyere abilange o tsughu, bise dibundu bamasambile Nzambi na yikanene mu djandi.
ACT 12:6 Yirode amabe na ditase dyumubeghe va wusu banzonzi. Tumbe mune mukolu, Pyere amabe atungu pange bedji, na amabe yilu va ghari ghore bedji. Baghore bamosi, bamamoghaange va wusu mune ndaghu tsughu.
ACT 12:7 Sundile, yanze yi Fumu yikekote mba tsughu djotsu djikekademe na yidjalale. Yanze yikekungise Pyere nomudimbe mbate o maghetu, mba akemutsingule yi: «Lenge noreleme!» Na bapange baketudughe mu makake mandi.
ACT 12:8 Yanze yike muvaghe yiri: «Tunge beleti aghu na dware bapondu baghu.» Akedivaghe. Yanze yikemwémuvaghe yi: «Dware yikutu yaghu na nduki.»
ACT 12:9 Pyere akeduke yanze na akepale o tsughu. Asamadjabaange yiri adi yanze amavaghaange dingenze, amatasaange yiri yiryaryamu.
ACT 12:10 Bakevyoghe yinombu yi baghore ayiteghe, bakevyoghe ayi mubedji, baketole va yabutsu yi madilu ayi mune ndaghu awumusitu. Yabutsu yeni yikedibughe pinze va wusu owu na bakepale. Banosupughe mu nzile, yanze yikekakene nandi.
ACT 12:11 Kaboghu Pyere akewulu adimavyoghaange, na akekévosile yi: «Mba nyimadjabe yi dingenze: Fumu atsitinde yanze yandi, na djandi, atsinkaghule va makake ma Yirode, na ame bivunde bi baSwife mbé baronde undase.»
ACT 12:12 Ave amadiwululu nane, akewende o ndaghu Mari, ngudji San adjinengulu Mareke. Aghune, batu bapwele bamabe baghukeme na bamasambililaange.
ACT 12:13 Ave Pyere amakokemunine mu yabutsu yi mune ndaghu, musatsi mughetu, awinengulu Rode, akebambene mughulu.
ACT 12:14 Akedjabe dyufi di Pyere, tumbe na kini asamadibule, aketsingule abamabe o ghari yi Pyere adji va dulombili.
ACT 12:15 Bakemuvaghe yi: «Wune bulaghu!» Tumbe amatsiyisaange yi ngenze. Kaboghu bakevaghe yi: «Awune tangudji yanze yandi.»
ACT 12:16 Yotsu yina, Pyere ukokemune mbé akikokemune. Bakemudibulile yabutsu, na bakesutu ave bamamulabile.
ACT 12:17 Akesambe dikake mubavotse, akebatsingule nane Fumu amamupalisile o tsughu, mba akebasindighe yiri: «Wendanu yétsingulanu Sake na baane ba tadji basusu.» Anomane, akepale nowende yari yisusu.
ACT 12:18 Wisi anotebughe, vakebe nkumfu neni va ghari baghore. Djowu bamakewivulaange: «Pyere akewuke?»
ACT 12:19 Yirode akeveghe dirume dyumurombe, tumbe basamamulabe. Akewave baghore, na akeveghe musughe wu baboke. Va djulu vane, akeghusughe o yinange yi Sudé novindeme o musyengi Sesaré mu yévume mwa temu.
ACT 12:20 Yirode amabe na kabu neni na bise Tire na bise Sidone. Djowu bakewulusunu va mosi mu sumbe yivunde, ayimakelisaange bime byotsu bi kaghe, dine dyandi Balesetose. Bamavayile nane, mumbari bamarondaange uvonde duvotsu na kaghe Yirode, dibilaange yiri bighudji byowu byotsu, bimarughesenaange o bulongu bwandi.
ACT 12:21 Mu yilumbu ayi bamasikighe, Yirode akedware yidjunge yi bukaghe, aketsane va yitsighe yandi yi bufumu, mba akebavosilaange.
ACT 12:22 Yike yinombu yimaghamughe yiri: «Djandi evosi nane nyambi, tsiri nane mutu!»
ACT 12:23 Tumbe vane-vane, yanze yi Fumu yikemudimbe, mumba amabonge bundumbe bu Nzambi: akelighu na misobe, na akefu.
ACT 12:24 Musamu wu Nzambi wumanyavaange laviri.
ACT 12:25 Barenabase na Sole yikebemani yisalu yowu o musyengi Serusaleme, bakeyeneghabughe, na bamabeghe nowu San awu amanengulungu Mareke.
ACT 13:1 Mu dibundu ayimabe o musyengi Antyose, vamabe babiyitsi na milonzi: Barenabase, Simewu adjinengulu «Munombi», Lususe mwise Sirene, Manayene omabungughe va mosi na kaghe Yirode, na Sole.
ACT 13:2 Mwa yilumbu ayi bamayitsilaange Fumu nowarile nzale, Yinyuni Yisyeme akebavaghe yiri: «Vengighanu Barenabase na Sole va mughule, bakedughusungu yisalu ayi nyimabanengilile.»
ACT 13:3 Kaboghu, banomane uwarile nzale nosambile, bakebasakighe makake na bakebasile uyenewende.
ACT 13:4 Banotindu na Yinyuni Yisyeme, Barenabase na Sole bakevindeme o disabu di Selesi. Avane, bamanangemine mu watange muwende o ningi dji Sipere.
ACT 13:5 Ave bamatolile o Salemine, bamasamune musamu Nzambi mu mandaghu ma tsambu ma baSwife. San adjinengulu Mareke amabe nowu nane mukange.
ACT 13:6 Vane wusu, banosabughe ningi djotsu bamatole o musyengi Pafose, bamayerasene muSwife, dibaale dimavagha bulosi. Dibaale dyeni dimabe mubiyitsi wumfurulu, dimanengulu «Bare-Djesu».
ACT 13:7 Djandi, amabe yisatsi yi yidjeti yineni ayimarumisaange yinange, yi manenguluungu Sersyo Poluse, dibaale dimabe na dudjabu. Djandi akenengile Barenabase na Sole, mumbari amabe na nzale uwulu musamu Nzambi.
ACT 13:8 Tumbe mulosi eni, awu bamanengilaange o mbembu Ngereke «Limase», amabalase maghughe. Adine djandi amabaghubitsilaange yi yidjeti akéwulu musamu Djesu.
ACT 13:9 Kaboghu Sole omanengulungu «Pole» wandi, amabe abase na Yinyuni Yisyeme. Djandi akemughengile yiswisu mu misu,
ACT 13:10 mba akemutsingule rye: «Ndedju awubase na mele na bikumbu, mwane dyabu, mumbini! Ngenze, ndedju wusekamane urekighe manzile ma Fumu amasungeme?
ACT 13:11 Avave, dikake di Fumu dike mu ndedju, wube yidunge. Mu mwa pesu temu, wughobwélabe dyénini di nyangu.» Sundila, misu ma Limase mamatsime, na piseme djimamughumbe, lake akeyenetsukemaange yari na yari, norombe mutu wumulonge nzile.
ACT 13:12 Ave yidjeti yeni amalabile dyambu adibenovyoghe va wusu andi, djandi amavayile Djesu yitu. Vane-vane, ndonzulu musamu Fumu djimabembe murime andi.
ACT 13:13 Pole na bambatsi bandi bamadusughe Pafose mu bwatu, muwendesene o disabu di Perse mu yinange yi Pafili. Aghune, San Mareke akebasile na akeghabughe o Serusaleme.
ACT 13:14 Banodusughe musyengi Perse, Pole na bambatsi bandi bamatole o musyengi Antyose dji yinange yi Pisidi. Mu yilumbu yuvume, bakekote o ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife na baketsane.
ACT 13:15 Banomane urange mughaghe Moyise na babiyitsi, bivunde bi ndaghu dusambu bakesindighe mutu muyebawivule rye: «Baane ba ngudji, payi dune mwa musamu mu warise batu, tsyévosyanu!»
ACT 13:16 Pole akereleme, akenangule dikake mubaghebule mba akevose yi: «Bise Yisrayele na djenu abedwidumi Nzambi, nkulwanu!
ACT 13:17 Nzambi baane ba Yisrayele, amasole baghulu betu. Amaroyise mukute eni, ave wumabilaange o bulongu bu Yisipete. Mba akewupalise na mangolu mandi o bulongu bweni.
ACT 13:18 Mba Nzambi amabasinge na bingulu byowu mu maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime, ave bamenewendilaange mu kumu dukange.
ACT 13:19 Va djulu vane, amadyamise yisambwali yi mikute o bulongu bu Kanane, na amaveghe mukute Yisrayele bulongu bweni nane disyale.
ACT 13:20 Motsu mane mamatsinge tangudji kame-djina na maghumi-maranu (450) ma bilime.» «Va djulu vane, amaveghe bakaaghe betu banzonzi tena va temu mubyitsi Samwele.
ACT 13:21 Kaboghu, bakaaghe betu bamavonde kaghe djubabeyise. Nzambi akebaveghe Sawule, mwane Kise, mu yifumbe yi Binzame. Djandi amarumise mukute Yisrayele mu maghumi-mana (40) ma bilime.
ACT 13:22 Nzambi anodjusule Sawule va yitsighe yi bukaghe, amabaveghe Davide nane kaghe owu va yivinze yi Sawule. Nzambi amamughabusile bumbedji novose rye: “Menu nyimadile Davide, mwane Djese, dibaale diwelimine, adimpeyi nzangu o murime ami, odughusu mambu motsu ame nyirondi akedughusu.”
ACT 13:23 Yike mu mukute Davide, Nzambi amasole muteghule andi wumosi, Djesu mube Mughobutsi wu baane ba Yisrayele, nane amabaveyile pangini.
ACT 13:24 Ne Djesu akerughe, San-Batise amalonze mukute wotsu wu Yisrayele bwendiri: mbé boléfungule mabi mowu, nobatusu mu lase yiri bamakalughe myonu.
ACT 13:25 Ave yisalu yi San yimabile bebeli nosuke, djandi amabawivule rye: “Anyi dwitasi yiri nyivu? Menu, nga djandi awu dwikelisi. Tumbe wulwanu! Djandi oyiruyi, djabanu yiri: menu nga nyiwelmine, nesi yike mu munyangule mikudu mi bapondu bandi.”»
ACT 13:26 «Bane ba tadji, djenu abe duvu baane ba Aberaame, na djenu wandi, adwiruyi mu mikute misusu mba dwidumi Nzambi, musamu éwuwu wu dughobutsu wutsitutindulu djetu botsu anu.
ACT 13:27 Batu abamatsanaange o Serusaleme na bivunde byowu bamaghale Djesu, na djowu basamatsiyise malongi ma babiyitsi amamarangu mu kale yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife. Tumbe ave bamafundisile Djesu, bamadughusu motsu ame babiyitsi bamabighaange.
ACT 13:28 Ne nane basamabe na tonu djumubokile, djowu bamavaghe Pilate yiri akeveghe musughe wumuboke.
ACT 13:29 Ave bamamanine udughusu mambu motsu ame Bisonu bi Nzambi bimavosaange mu djandi, bamasunduse yibindi yandi va kurusu na bakemusunze o ngile.
ACT 13:30 Tumbe Nzambi amamurambuse o dufu.
ACT 13:31 Mu bilumbu bipwele, Djesu amalabene ombu djowu abamayenewendaange nandi ubandile o Ngalile teno Serusaleme. Avave, djowu bakevu bambedji ba Djesu va wusu baane ba Yisrayele.
ACT 13:32 Na djetu, twidudjabisi Musamu Wuboti, pangini adji Nzambi amavangene na baghulu betu.
ACT 13:33 Djandi amadjidughusu ombu djetu abe tuvu bateghule bowu, ave amarambusile Djesu o dufu. Nane direndulu mu mughande Nimbu awu mubedji yi: “Ndedju wudji mwane ami, na muni, nyimawubure.”
ACT 13:34 Nzambi amarambuse Djesu va ghari djowu abafu, mumba dunyuru dwandi dukeyébole o ghari mbine. Djandi amavose rye: “Nyuduveghe myule, ami nyimavangene na Davide, amisyeme na mi ngenze.”
ACT 13:35 Ladibandu, mbembu Nzambi djivosili mu kapu mosi yiri: “Ndedju wughosile Yibyatsi yaghu Yisyeme, yikebole o ghari mbine.”
ACT 13:36 Yike Davide, anomane udughusu mu temu andi bisalu byotsu abi Nzambi amaronde bwé akedughusu, djandi amafu. Aketswighu mbure mosi adji bamatswiyile batadji bandi, na dunyuru dwandi dumabole.
ACT 13:37 Tumbe Djesu awu Nzambi amarambuse o dufu, dunyuru dwandi dusamabole.
ACT 13:38 Baane ba ngudji, djabanu yiri: mu djandi, dutandu du mabi dwidulonzulu. Mu djandi, mutu wotsu awimuvayili yitu, eghobulu mu mabi motsu, ame ne mighaghe mi Moyise mbé mighorungule utande.
ACT 13:40 Kaboghu, mbé dukebene yiri motsu amamabighu na babiyitsi makéduruyile. Djowu bamavose rye:
ACT 13:41 “Tsunanu, djenu abe dubase na dilenze. Sutwanu na fwanu! Mu temu adji dukidubile monyu, nyuvaghe mwa yisalu. Yisalu ayi mbé dughorungule usinge, ne mutu atsidutsingule yoni.”»
ACT 13:42 Ave Pole djone Barenabase bamapalilaange o ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife, batu bamabawivule yeri, mbé bomwérughe oyibalonze mambu meni, mu yilumbu yuvume.
ACT 13:43 Ave yibengunu yimasukile, baSwife bapwele na batu abamasinge Nzambi baSwife nomuyitse, bamayevetsighe Pole na Barenabase. Mu nzile, mubedji eni wumayenevosaange nowu, mu bawarise yiri bayakakene na yese yi Nzambi.
ACT 13:44 Yilumbu yuvume ayimadukaange, batu botsu ba musyengi bamaghukeme mu yéwulu musamu wu mbembu Fumu.
ACT 13:45 Ave baSwife bamalabile mughungi, djowu bamabase na ngusu, mba bamatumune bakemi mu mambu motsu Pole amavosaange na bamamusyenge.
ACT 13:46 Yike Pole djone Barenabase bakebatsingule na musighe rye: «Mbembu Nzambi djimatindulu va téteghe ombu djenu baSwife. Tumbe dudjibusilaange, dwilasi yiri dughaduwelmine mudile monyu mutubu na mutubu! Adine djetu, tughéluyile yike ombu djowu abagha baSwife.
ACT 13:47 Djabeni Fumu eturumi ave evosili rye: “Nyimawubyatse nane yidjalale yi malongu masusu, mubeghe dughobutsu teno masukusulu ma butambe!”»
ACT 13:48 Ave bamadighululu, botsu abasamabe baSwife bakebase na nzangu, bakeyitsaange musamu Fumu. Na botsu abamasolu kale, mudile monyu mutubu na mutubu, bamavayile Djesu yitu.
ACT 13:49 Musamu Fumu wumanyavaange mu bulongu bwotsu.
ACT 13:50 Tumbe baSwife bakesibise bidjeti bi baghetu abamayitsaange Nzambi na bivunde bi musyengi. Djobotsu bakekwane Pole djone Barenabase, mba bakebasyanze o yinange yowu.
ACT 13:51 Pole na Barenabase bakekuke difufundu di makulu mowu na bakewende o musyengi Yikonyome.
ACT 13:52 Yotsu yine, badukitsi abamabe o musyengi Antyose, bamabase na nzangu djineni na Yinyuni Yisyeme.
ACT 14:1 O Yikonyome wandi Pole na Barenabase bakekote o ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife. Bamasamune musamu Nzambi, lake baSwife na baNgereke bapwele bamasinge musamu Djesu.
ACT 14:2 Tumbe baSwife abasamasinge Nzambi, bakerombise matase mabive ombu djowu abasamabe baSwife, na bakebasibise bwé bakéwululu bango yitu.
ACT 14:3 Tumbe dikalewube nane, Pole na Barenabase bamatsinge o musyengi Yikonyome. Bamasamunaange musamu Nzambi na musighe. Fumu amabaveghaange mangolu movaghe bimaghe na bilimbe bineni na makake mowu, mu ulase yiri, musamu awu bamalonzaange mu yese yandi, wungenze.
ACT 14:4 O musyengi Yikonyome, vakebe dupasu va ghari yinombu yi batu ba musyengi. Bamosi bakebe o yari yi baSwife, mba bane o yari yi bilumbi.
ACT 14:5 Tumbe baSwife na bo basamabe baSwife na bivunde byowu bakekunzeme mukwane notinde mamani mu uboke bilumbi.
ACT 14:6 Djowu badidjabilaange, bakeyesweme o misyengi mi Likoni, Lisetere na Derebe, na mu mighule myowu.
ACT 14:7 Aghune, bakesamune Musamu Wuboti.
ACT 14:8 O musyengi Lisetere wumabe yikoyi, yimaburu mambolutu, asamarungulaange uwende diteli. Matsane,
ACT 14:9 amawulu nane Pole amavosilaange. Pole anomughengile, akelabe yiri ane yitu yiwelimine yughobululu.
ACT 14:10 Pole akemutsingule rye: «Releme, sumbiti mu makulu maghu!» Yikoyi yeni akesundile ureleme na akevaghe mwa batake.
ACT 14:11 Mughungi wunolabe adi Pole amavaghe, wukevose o mbembu dji bise Likoni yi: «Banyambi bamabonge manyuru ma batu na bamavindeme ombu etu!».
ACT 14:12 Bamanengile Barenabase «Sese», mumbari Sese amabe yivunde yi banzambi bowu. Pole bakemunengile «Yirmese», mumba amabe djandi omavosaange pwele.
ACT 14:13 Ndaghu dji nyambi Sese djimabe beli na dikotulu di musyengi. Anowulu mambu meni, muvaghulitsi paghu wu nyambi eni akebeghe bangombi abebamadwise na kembu, va wusu mughungi eni. Bamarondaange yi bangombi beni bakeveghu nane paghu ombu Barenabase djone Pole mu baghobise.
ACT 14:14 Bilumbi Pole na Barenabase, banodidjabe, bakepase bikutu byowu mu kevongule na bakesobene mu mughungi, noghamughe:
ACT 14:15 «Bambatsi betu, mubayi dwivayili nane? Tudji batu nane djenu. Twidubeyili Musamu Wuboti, muvaghe yiri dukesanze mutsanu enu. Mbé dusile bakosi abaghane tsongu, nosinge Nzambi-Pungu omasunde djulu, butambe, mubu na byotsu abivu mune.
ACT 14:16 Mu temu atsimavyoghe, Nzambi amasile malongu motsu wuyenewendaange kulini-kulini.
ACT 14:17 Ne vane, Nzambi asamadunde udulase maboti mandi. Adine, amadutindilaange mamvule na bivaru mu temu adjiwelimine. Amabwéduveghe bighudji na amabase mirime myenu na nzangu.»
ACT 14:18 Yike bakale uvose nane, bilumbi bamalabe diweru dyughandise mughungi, bwé akébavaghulile paghu.
ACT 14:19 Va djulu vane, mwa baSwife bamosi bakerughesene o musyengi Antyose no Yikonyome, bakesibise mughungi mu kwane Pole djone Barenabase. Mba baketinde Pole mamani mu muboke. Na ditase yi Pole amafu, bakemudute mu mupalise o musyengi owu.
ACT 14:20 Tumbe badukitsi banomukande, akereleme na akekote nowu o musyengi. Va kedi, akewende na Barenabase o musyengi Derebe.
ACT 14:21 Pole na Barenabase bamasamune Musamu Wuboti o musyengi Derebe, awu bamadilile badukitsi bapwele. Mba bakeghabughe o Lisetere, o Yikonyome na Antyose.
ACT 14:22 Bamayenewarisaange badukitsi, nobalonzaange ube na yikanene mu yitu ombu Nzambi. Na bamabwébalubusaange yi: «Tuvyolanu mu maghughe mapwele ne tukekote mu Bukaghe bu Nzambi.»
ACT 14:23 Mu kale dibundu bamababyatsile bivunde, mba yikebemani uwarile nzale nosambile, bakebawakise va makake ma Fumu adji bamavayile yitu.
ACT 14:24 Bakevyole o yinange yi Pisidi, na baketole o yinange yi Pafili.
ACT 14:25 Banomane ulonze mbembu Nzambi o musyengi Perse, bamavindeme o musyengi Atali.
ACT 14:26 Va djulu vane, bakenangeme mu watange mu wende o musyengi Antyose dji Siri, musyengi awu bamabyatsulu mu yese yi Nzambi dibandu yisalu ayi bamavaghe.
ACT 14:27 Banotole o Antyose, Pole djone Barenabase bakeghukighe dibundu. Bakebatsingule motsu ame Nzambi amavaghe mu kake mowu, na nane amaghobulile batu bapwele abasamabe baSwife.
ACT 14:28 Pole djone Barenabase bamavyose temu djineni va ghari badukitsi ba yinange yi Antyose.
ACT 15:1 Mwa batu bamarughesene o musyengi Sudé, baketole o musyengi Antyose. Djowu bamalonzaange baane ba tadji botsu, novose rye: «Pa dugharebu nane mughaghe Moyise wivosili, dughorungule ughobulu.»
ACT 15:2 Pole na Barenabase basamasinge ame djowu bamavosaange, na bamatsunde nowu. Ladibandu, bamawulusunu yi Pole na Barenabase na bango yitu ba musyengi Antyose, mbé bowende o Serusaleme oyevose dyambu dyeni ombu bilumbi na bivunde bi dibundu.
ACT 15:3 Dibundu dimabaghanine nobasyende. Djowu bamavyoyile o yinange yi Fenisi teno Samari, noyenetsingulaange nane batu abasamabe baSwife, bamadilile duburu du ghone. Na dyoni, dimaveghe nzangu neni ombu baane ba ngudji botsu.
ACT 15:4 Ave bamatolile o Serusaleme, bakesangulu na dibundu, na bilumbi na bivunde bi dibundu. Lake djowu bakebatsingule motsu ame Nzambi amadughusu nowu.
ACT 15:5 Tumbe, mwa bamosi mu yinombu yi baFarisi, abamavayile Djesu yitu bamareleme. Djowu bamavose rye: «Bise malongu abagha baSwife vengu mbé borebu, nobaveghe dirume dyughobise mughaghe Moyise.»
ACT 15:6 Bilumbi na bivunde bi ndaghu Nzambi bikeghukeme mu ukelule dyambu dyeni.
ACT 15:7 Va djulu mutsundu eni wune, Pyere akereleme nobatsingule rye: «Baane ba ngudji, dwididjabi yi mu bilumbu abiteghe, Nzambi amanzole va ghari enu. Djandi amaronde yi ngalonze Musamu Wuboti ombu djowu abagha baSwife, bakewughuwulu na bakewusinge.
ACT 15:8 Na Nzambi, oyidjabi mirime mi batu, amabalase yiri ebasingi, na amabaveghe Yinyuni Yisyeme nane amavayile netu.
ACT 15:9 Nzambi asamavaghe duvyakusunu va ghari djowu na djetu. Bano vayile Nzambi yitu akebalyomise mirime.
ACT 15:10 Mumbari yi dwimangili Nzambi? Dwirondi usunze mufune ewune mu masambeke ma badukitsi? Mufune awuwu, ne bakaaghe betu, ne djetubeni tusamarungule unangule!
ACT 15:11 Mu dyoni, tune yitu yiri djetu botsu twighobululu mu yese yi Fumu Djesu, nane djowandi.»
ACT 15:12 Yinombu yotsu yi batu yikevole «swii», mughulu Barenabase na Pole abamabatsingulaange bimaghe na bilimbe, abi Nzambi amadughusu nowu va ghari abasamabe baSwife.
ACT 15:13 Yike bévoli, Sake akebonge mbembu novose rye: «Baane ba ngudji, kulwetyanu!
ACT 15:14 Simewu amatutasise mwa dyambu: vane dibandu, Nzambi amasolile va ghari abasamabe baSwife, mukute awube wandi.
ACT 15:15 Posulu babiyitsi djiwelmine na dyambu dyeni. Direndulu mu Bisonu rye:
ACT 15:16 “Fumu Nzambi amavose yi: Va djulu vane nyubwérughe. Nyurelighe ndaghu Davide adjimaberughe. Nyurungulile abimapanzighe, nyudjikunze na djubwéreleme,
ACT 15:17 mba batu bamosi ba bulongu bakerombe Fumu. Nine, mikute myotsu ami nyimanengili mikebe myami. Lanu adi Fumu evosi.
ACT 15:18 Djandi amadughusu mambu meni mane, vane kale.”»
ACT 15:19 Sake akebwévosi yi: «Lanu adi menu nyitasi: diwelemine yi tuyamwékambise abagha baSwife, abekaluyi dyele na uduke Nzambi.
ACT 15:20 Tumbe tubarendisilyanu mughande, mu ubatsingule rye: “Duyabwebile udji banyame abaveghu nane paghu ombu bakosi. Silanu monyu wu nzoruru na bumbembu, duyabwebile udji banyame abaghaghewu kingu mu upalise malungu.”
ACT 15:21 Vaghanu nane mumbari, ubandile vane kale, mu kale musyengi awu batu bélonzili mughaghe Moyise, mughaghe eni wirangu kale yilumbu yuvume mu mandaghu ma tsambu ma baSwife.»
ACT 15:22 Kaboghu, dimawelmine yiri bilumbi na bivunde, na dibundu dyotsu, bakesole va ghari owu, batu botinde na Pole djone Barenabase o musyengi Antyose. Bakesole baane ba tadji babedji va ghari bivunde bi dibundu: Silase na Sudase omanengulungu Barenabase, babaale bamaghobusungu.
ACT 15:23 Bakebaveghe mughande eni awumabe wusonughu nane: «Djetu bilumbi na bivunde bi dibundu tudji baane ba ngudji benu. Yike twidutindili mughande éwuwu, djenu baane ngudji betu abagha baSwife, djenu adwitsani o musyengi Antyose o yinange yi Siri na Silisi, mbolwanu!
ACT 15:24 Tumawulu yi bamosi va ghari etu bamayédupupise mirime na posulu tsyowu. Yotsu yine, tsiri djetu tumabasindighe.
ACT 15:25 Ladibandu, tutsisolile batu bébane, nobasindighe ombu wenu na baane ba tadji betu ba murime, Barenabase na Pole.
ACT 15:26 Djowu abamasumbise monyu owu mu dine di Fumu etu Djesu Kirisete.
ACT 15:27 Na twidutindili Sudase na Silase, aboyidutsingule na musighe, mambu mane mamosi ame tutsidurendili mu mughande eni wune.
ACT 15:28 Adine Yinyuni Yisyeme na djetubeni, tutsilabile yi tughobwérungule uduveghe mufune wumosi va djulu mambu meni ametumadurendili. Tumbe vengu, mbé dudedile mighaghe myeni mimi:
ACT 15:29 duyabwedji banyame abavaghulu ombu bakosi, silanu monyu wu nzoruru na bumbembu, duyabwebile udji banyame abaghaghewu kingu mu upalise malungu. Payi dutsivaghe nane mu byotsu bine, diwelimine yiri dutsisungighe. Kangwalyanu, yike vane wusu.»
ACT 15:30 Banoghanine bise dibundu, bakewende o musyengi Antyose. Ave bamatolile wune, bakeghukighe dibundu dyotsu mba bakebaveghe mughande eni.
ACT 15:31 Mughande eni wukerangu, na botsu bamabase na nzangu, mu duwarusu adu bamadile mu motsu amamabe marendu mune.
ACT 15:32 Sudase na Silase, babilange djobeni babiyitsi, bamawamuse baane tadji na malongi mapwele, mu bawarise mu yitu yowu.
ACT 15:33 Bamatsane nowu mwa temu, mba baane ba tadji yikebemani ubaveghe myule, bamabaghanine nobasile ughabughe ombu djowu abamabasindighe.[
ACT 15:34 Yike, Silase amaronde usyale o musyengi Antyose.]
ACT 15:35 Pole na Barenabase bakesyale o Antyose. Djowu na batu bamosi, bamayenelonzaange mbembu Fumu nosamune Musamu Wuboti.
ACT 15:36 Mwa temu djinovyoghe, Pole aketsingule Barenabase yi: «Twendi tughabuyi o uyélingule misyengi myotsu ami tumayenesamunine musamu wu Fumu, mu uyélabe nane baane ba tadji bakevu.»
ACT 15:37 Barenabase mbé aronde ubeghe nowu, San omanengulungu Mareke.
ACT 15:38 Tumbe Pole amadibuse, mumbari San Mareke djawandi, amabuse uwende nowu. Adine amakakenine nowu vo bamabile o yinange yi Pafili, mumbari amabuse ubawamuse mu yisalu yowu.
ACT 15:39 Mutsundu wumabe wuneni va ghari owu, la dibandu bamakakenine. Barenabase akebonge Mareke nandi, bakenangeme mu watange na bakeyenewende o ningi dji Sipere.
ACT 15:40 Tumbe Pole akesole Silase, bakewakusu na baane ba tadji va makake na yese yi Fumu, mba bakeyenewende.
ACT 15:41 Bamavyoyile o yinange yi Siri na yo yi Silisi, noyenewarisaange yitu yi mabundu.
ACT 16:1 Pole aketole o misyengi mi Derebe na Lisetere. Vane vamabe mudukitsi dine dyandi Timote, ngudji andi mughetu muSwife awumasinge Djesu, tadji andi amabe muNgereke.
ACT 16:2 Baane ba ngudji bise Lisetere na Yikonyome, bamamughabusilaange bumbedji buboti.
ACT 16:3 Pole mbé aronde umubeghe nowu mu mulingu, adine amarebelu. Djandi amavayile nane, dibandu baSwife abamabe mu binange byeni, mumbari batu botsu bamadjabaange yiri tadji andi adji mwise Ngereke.
ACT 16:4 Mu misyengi myotsu ami bamayenevyoyilaange, bamenelonzaange baane ba tadji mighaghe ami bilumbi na bivunde bi Serusaleme bamabonge, na bamatsiyisaange mumbari mikeghobusu.
ACT 16:5 Mabundu mamawarusungu mu yitu, na durangu dwowu dumaneghaange kale yilumbu.
ACT 16:6 Pole na bambatsi bandi ba mulingu, bamavyoyile o yinange yi Firisi na o Ghalasi, mumbari Yinyuni Yisyeme yimabaghandise ulonze musamu Nzambi o yari yi Asi.
ACT 16:7 Ave bamatolile va mughule yinange yi Misi, bakedile ditase dyuwende o Bitini, tumbe Yinyuni yi Djesu yisamabagharusu.
ACT 16:8 Adine bamavyole kwase yinange yi Misi tenave bamayesunduyile o disabu di Torwase.
ACT 16:9 Va mukolu, Pole akebe na dulase. Akelabe sumbiti dibaale diteli, mwise Masedwane amamulendaange yi: «Vyoyile o Masedwane na rughe oyituwamuse!»
ACT 16:10 Va djulu dulasu dweni, tumakunzeme mu uwende o Masedwane, mumbari tumalabe yiri Nzambi amatunengilaange wune, mu yésamune Musamu andi Wuboti.
ACT 16:11 Yike, tunonangeme mu watange o Torwase, na tumawende sungingi o ningi dji Samotarase, mba yilumbu ayi mubedji, tumatole o musyengi Napolise.
ACT 16:12 Tunodusughe vane, tumawende o musyengi Filipe, musyengi wuteghe wu yinange yi Masedwane, awumabe otsi durumu du Rome. Tumavyose mwa bilumbu va musyengi eni.
ACT 16:13 Yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, tumapale o musyengi mu wende o mughule mudjambe na ditase dyurasunu mbure adji batu bamasambililaange Nzambi. Tumatsane mu uvosile mwa baghetu, abamabe baghukeme vane.
ACT 16:14 Mughetu wumosi va ghari owu amanengulungu Lidi, mwise Tyatire. Djandi amabe kooli tsande tsiboti tsimabe tsibenge. Mughetu eni amayitsaange Nzambi, adine amatuwululuungu. Na Fumu amamudibule murime, mumbari akewulu na musighe mambu ame Pole amalonzaange.
ACT 16:15 Djandi amabatusu na batu botsu abamatsanaange mu ndaghu andi. Na amatunengile novose rye: «Payi dwitasi yiri menu wandi nyivayili Fumu yitu nane djenu, rughanu yitsananu mu ndaghu ami.» Amatunengile na yiswebiri na tumasinge uwende.
ACT 16:16 Mwa yilumbu, ave tumawendilaange o mbure dusambu, tumabengunu na musatsi mughetu munzambu, amabe na yinyuni yi mbome. Yinyuni yeni ayi amayenebiyilaange, nodilisaange mbongu tsipwele ombu bafumu bandi.
ACT 16:17 Munzambu eni amayenetudukaange, Pole na djetu, na amayeneghamughaange yiri: «Batu bebabe basatsi ba Nzambi djulu! Djowu bodulonze nzile dughobutsu!»
ACT 16:18 Dyambu dyeni dikebe yike nane yiswebiri bilumbu byotsu. Va disukusulu, Pole akenyoghe, akeghelughe na akenyangile yinyuni yibi novose rye: «Mu dine di Djesu Kirisete, nyiwurumi lenge nopale mu djandi!» Na yinyuni yibi yimapale va temu eni.
ACT 16:19 Vo bafumu ba munzambu eni bamalabile yiri mulilu owu wumatsyemughe, bakeghange Pole na Silase na bakebabeghe va mbure mughungi, va wusu fundu banzonzi mu utabule dyambu.
ACT 16:20 Bakebabeghe va wusu banzonzi ba mighaghe na bakevose rye: «Batu bebabe bamayirombise dimbunge mu musyengi etu. Badji baSwife
ACT 16:21 na bélonzi mutsanu awughawuwelimine na mighaghe myetu, djetu abe tuvu bise Rome. Na tughane musughe wusinge vo wusalise moni.»
ACT 16:22 Mughungi wukenyoyile Pole djone Silase. Banzonzi bamasindighe batu bakebavule bikutu, nobadimbise mikase.
ACT 16:23 Banomane wubadimbise, bakebabwaghe o tsughu na baketsingule mukelitsi tsughu, yiri akebakelisaange babindeme o ghari tsughu.
ACT 16:24 Anodile dirume dyeni, mukelitsi tsughu akebasunze o yibuku ayi ghari na akebavaghe makulu mu bivangu bi miri.
ACT 16:25 Va ghari mukolu, Pole na Silase bamasambilaange na bamawimbilaange muyitse Nzambi. Botsu abamabe o tsughu bamabawulungu.
ACT 16:26 Vane-vane, butambe bukeregheme norakule yibughe yi ndaghu tsughu. Myune mi ndaghu myotsu mikedibughe na bapange ba bise tsughu botsu bakenyangughe.
ACT 16:27 Mukelitsi tsughu akerambughe. Anolabe yiri myune mi ndaghu mi tsughu midibughe, akedute didjenge dyandi mukéboke, mumbari amatase yi bise tsughu bamarine.
ACT 16:28 Tumbe Pole akebwaghe mughamu wuneni novose rye: «Wuyakéboke! Djetu botsu tudji vave!»
ACT 16:29 Mukelitsi tsughu akevonde mutotu paghe, akewemaswasu o tsughu noregheme, akekebwaghe va makulu ma Pole na Silase.
ACT 16:30 Akebapalise o yibuku yi ndaghu na akebawivule: «Bafumu bami, tsyeni nyurungule uvayile mu ughobughe?»
ACT 16:31 Bakemuwaghule yiri: «Vayile Fumu Djesu yitu, wughobulu, ndedju na mukute aghu wotsu.»
ACT 16:32 Mba bakebalonze musamu Fumu, djabeni na botsu abamabe mu ndaghu andi.
ACT 16:33 Mune mukolu eni, mukelitsi tsughu akebabeghe o ndawandi, akebasuse mapure na akebabughe. Vane-vane amabatusu, na mukute andi wotsu.
ACT 16:34 Mukelitsi amabeghe Pole na Silase o ndaghu andi, amalambise, bakedji va mosi. Djandi na mukute andi, bamabase na nzangu djineni mumbari bamasinge Nzambi djobotsu.
ACT 16:35 Wisi anotebughe, banzonzi baketinde baghore mu uyétsingule mukelitsi tsughu yi: «Palise batu bebane.»
ACT 16:36 Mukelitsi tsughu aketsingule Pole rye: «Banzonzi batsitinde musughe wududjeyise. Kabo tsyewendyanu na duvotsu.»
ACT 16:37 Tumbe Pole akebawaghule rye: «Djowu batsitudimbise va ghari batu. Wendanu dukebatsingule, bamatubwaghe o tsughu ne bunzonzi uvaghu. Djetu abe tuvu bise Rome! Mba vave, bérondi utudjeyise yike o musweghe? Nesi! Baruyi djobeni mu uyitudjeyise!»
ACT 16:38 Baghore baketsingule banzonzi mambu meni, na djowu bakeregheme, badjabilaange yiri Pole na Silase bise Rome.
ACT 16:39 Banzonzi bakerughe mu uyibavonde kokolu, bakebapalise o tsughu na bakebavaghe bwé bakedusughe musyengi.
ACT 16:40 Banopale o tsughu, Pole na Silase bakewende ombu Lidi. Banomane uwarise baane ba tadji mu yitu, bamayenewende.
ACT 17:1 Banovyoyile o misyengi mi Afipolise na Apoloni, Pole djone Silase bamatole o musyengi Tesalonike, tena ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife.
ACT 17:2 Mu yuku yandi, Pole amakote o ndaghu dusambu. Kale yilumbu yuvumine, mu tsone yiryeru, amamoghe na amatsunde nowu mu dyambu di Bisonu bi Nzambi.
ACT 17:3 Adine amabavindiyilaange nobalonzaange nane Bisonu bi Nzambi, bimalasilaange na kengili yiri, Kirisete mbé otsoghusu, akeboku, mbana va djulu vane, mbé orambughe o dufu. Pole akebwébatsingule rye: «Djesu adji menu nyidulonzi, djandi la Kirisete.»
ACT 17:4 Mwa pesu baSwife bakesinge musamu eni, bamasobene na Pole djone Silase. Vamabe yinombu yineni yi baNgereke bamabande uyitse Nzambi, baghetu bapwele wandi bamabe bidjeti.
ACT 17:5 Tumbe baSwife bakebase na ngusu. Bakeghukighe yinombu yi makwilisi bamarasunu mu mimbambe, bakesibisi dimbunge mu musyengi. Bakewende o ndaghu dji Sason mu yenerombe Pole na Silase, mubabeghe va wusu mukute.
ACT 17:6 Basamarasunu Pole na Silase. Ladibandu, bamabeyile Sason na baane ba ngudji bamosi va wusu bivunde bi musyengi. Bakeghamughe, novose rye: «Batu bebabe batsisisene bulongu, bamatole wunu!
ACT 17:7 Sason amabadile ombu wandi! Batu botsu babe bésalisi na duvyakusunu du mighaghe mi kaghe Sesare, mumbari bévayi yi vadji kaghe mosi, djinengulu Djesu.»
ACT 17:8 Posulu eni, djikenyoyise mughungi na bivunde bi musyengi.
ACT 17:9 Sason na batu bandi bakefute yisingu yi dyambu ombu bivunde ne bakebasile.
ACT 17:10 Na mukolu witoli, baane ba tadji bakewendise Pole na Silase o musyengi Bere. Banotole, bakewende o ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife.
ACT 17:11 Djobane bamabe na mutsanu wuboti tsinane baSwife ba Tesalonike. Bakedile Musamu Nzambi na durondu dwotsu. Kale yilumbu, bamakelulange Bisonu bi Nzambi mu ukelule yiri ame bamabatsingulaange mangenze.
ACT 17:12 Durangu duneni du batu bakevayile yitu, na va ghari baNgereke: pwele baghetu baghobe na babaale djowandi bakevayile Djesu yitu.
ACT 17:13 Tumbe ave baSwife ba Tesalonike bamawulu bwé Pole yike mbembu Nzambi elonzi o musyengi Bere wandi, bakesundili urughe mu yisibise dimbunge va ghari mughungi.
ACT 17:14 Vane-vane, baane ba tadji bakewendise Pole o yari yi mubu. Silase na Timote bakesyale o musyengi Bere.
ACT 17:15 Pole, amabatsingule djowu abaménebeghaange yi Silase djone Timote batasunu mbangu-mbangu. Bakemutolise o musyengi Atene, mba bakeghabughe o musyengi Bere.
ACT 17:16 Temu adji Pole amakelisile Silase na Timote o musyengi Atene, amatsire murime mumbari musyengi wumabe wubase na bakosi.
ACT 17:17 Amalonzaange baSwife o ndaghu dusambu na botsu abasamabe baSwife, tumbe bamadumaange Nzambi. Kale yilumbu, amayenelonzaange botsu abamenebengunu nandi.
ACT 17:18 Balonzi ba dyele ba Pikire na ba Senu bakerughe muyivose nandi. Bamosi bakevose rye: «Yivovi ayiyi! Yi erondi ututsingule vave?» Abane bakewaghule rye: «Etubuli banyambi ba beni!» Djowu bamavosile nane, mumbari Pole amasamune Musamu Wuboti wu Djesu na durambughulu o dufu.
ACT 17:19 Bakemubeghe nowu, tena va wusu fundu dji banzonzi ba musyengi owu, bamanengilaange «Yiropase». Bakemuwivule: «Turungule udjabe divindughulu di musamu éwuwu wughone witubeyili?
ACT 17:20 Mumbari yitutsinguli mambu maghone, na twirondi udjabe divindughulu.»
ACT 17:21 Bise Atene botsu na beni abamatsana o musyengi eni, temu djotsu yisalu yowu bu uvose vo uwulu musamu wughone.
ACT 17:22 Pole, diteli va ghari fundu dji Yiropase, akebonge mbembu: «Bise Atene, nyimalabe yiri dudji batu, abe bédjabi tinde wuyitse bakosi benu.
ACT 17:23 Ave nyiyene vyengililaange mu mimbambe myenu, nyiyenelabaange bitumbe bi dighobe abidwiyitsi, na nzirasunu ne yinyenzulu yi paghu na yisonu yéyiyi: “Ombu nyambi adjighédjabunu.” Adji dwiyitsi mba dughedjidjabi, adjine menu nyiruyi oyidulonze.
ACT 17:24 Nzambi, djandi omavaghe bulongu na byobivu mune, adji Fumu djulu na butambe, djandi aghetsani mu mandaghu amarungu na batu.
ACT 17:25 Aghésalulu na makake ma batu, mba aghane nzale yisalu wotsu. Mumbari djandi oyiveyi botsu monyu, muvumu na byotsu.
ACT 17:26 Mu mutu wumosi, amasunde mikute myotsu yiri djowu bakebase butambe bwotsu. Mu bufumu bwandi, Nzambi amasikighe yitsingu yi monyu, na bandilu ma mbure motsanine.
ACT 17:27 Nzambi amavaghe nane, yiri bakemurombe ne vadji diweru dyumulabe. Yotsu yine, Nzambi aghavale netu,
ACT 17:28 mumbari batu bévosi rye: “Mu djandi twivumini, twikungili, tubile monyu.” Dyoni dimavosu na bivovi byenu: “Djetu wandi tudji bakule bandi.”
ACT 17:29 Kaboghu tubilange bakule ba Nzambi, toghorungule ubaghusunu Nzambi na bakosi ba lore, ba madilu vo ba mamani, abitulu na matase ma batu.
ACT 17:30 Nzambi aghékipi temu adji mbé bakamudjabile, tumbe erondi yiri batu botsu, mu mbure tsyotsu, bakesanze mutsanu na umughobise.
ACT 17:31 Mumbari Nzambi, amasikighe yilumbu ayi mutu awu djabeni amasole, ososisile batu botsu mu butambe mu dusungughu dwandi. Nzambi amalase kengili kake andi, ave amamurambusile o dufu.»
ACT 17:32 Ave djowu bamawululu dyambu di batu abafu bwé boghabughe monyu, abane bamamupedji. Bamosi bamavose rye: «Djetu tuwuwululu mu dyoni temu susu.»
ACT 17:33 Na vane, Pole akebasile.
ACT 17:34 Va djulu vane, mwa dikabu di batu bamasobene nandi na bamakalughe bakereti. Mu yinombu yeni, vamabe dibaale dimosi mu fundu banzonzi bamanengilaange Deni, mughetu dine dyandi Damarise, na bamosi wandi.
ACT 18:1 Va djulu vane, Pole akeghusughe musyengi Atene mu wende o musyengi Korinte.
ACT 18:2 Akebengunu na muSwife dine dyandi Akilase, mwise Pon. Amabe na mughatsi andi Pirisile. Djowu mbé basekatsinge nobotughe o bulongu bu Yitali, mumbari kaghe Kolode amaveghe dirume ombu baSwife botsu bakedusughe musyengi Rome. Pole amasobene nowu,
ACT 18:3 mumbari avu na yisalu yimosi nowu, bamarungaange masambe. Adine Pole amatsanine nowu, lake bakesalaange va mosi.
ACT 18:4 Kale yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, Pole amalonzaange o ndaghu dusambu, na djandi amarombaange udute baSwife viri viri baNgereke ombu Fumu.
ACT 18:5 Ave Silase na Timote bamadusuyile o yinange yi Masedwane mu tole o Korinte, Pole akesingene yike na yisalu yusamunaange Musamu Wuboti wu Nzambi. Djandi akevindighaange va wusu baSwife yiri Djesu adji Kirisete.
ACT 18:6 Tumbe baSwife bamabuse musamu awu Pole, amabasamuninaange na bamamusyenge. Kaboghu Pole amakuke difufundu di bikutu byandi na amabatsingule yi: «Malungu menu mabi mu myuru myenu! Menu nyisyeme. Mudjonge enu bakole. Ubandile na nyangu, nyuwende ombu djowu abagha baSwife.»
ACT 18:7 Akebotughe vane na akewende ombu dibaale dine dyandi Tityuse Susutuse, amayitsaange Nzambi. Ndaghu wandi djimabe va mughule ndaghu dusambu dji baSwife.
ACT 18:8 Kirisepuse yivunde yi ndaghu dusambu, akevayile yitu ombu Fumu, na mukute andi wotsu. Batu bapwele bise Korinte, bamawululu Pole. Bakevayile yitu yowu mu Nzambi na bakebatusu.
ACT 18:9 Mukolu mosi, Pole akedile dulasu, mune Fumu emutsinguli didi: «Wuyala ghome. Tumbe bwela uvose, wuyavole:
