ACT 18:10 nyidji naghu. Vagha mutu oghudimbise vo oghukambise, mumbari bapwele bavu bami mu musyengi ewuwu.»
ACT 18:11 Pole aketsane yilime yimosi na yibuku o Korinte, amalonzaange ombu botsu musamu Nzambi.
ACT 18:12 Mu temu adji Ghalyone amabilaange yivunde yi musyengi Rome mu yinange yi Akaye, baSwife bamawulusunu mu ufwengilile Pole. Bakemubeghe o ndaghu bunzonzi.
ACT 18:13 Baketubule yi: «Dibaale dyédidi erondi utsotse batu mu yitsaange Nzambi mu duvyakusunu du mughaghe etu.»
ACT 18:14 Pole mbé aronde uvose, ave Ghalyone amawaghulili baSwife: «Djenu baSwife, mbé yi mutu atsiboke vo dyambu dibi atsivaghe, mbé nubo temu djuduwulu, notabule bunzonzi.
ACT 18:15 Tumbe dibila yiri, mutsundu mu dyambu di bighume, mine, vo di mughaghe djenubeni, dyoni didutsuni. Nyibusi ube nzonzi dji mambu nane!»
ACT 18:16 Na akebapalise.
ACT 18:17 Kaboghu, botsu bakeghange Sosetene, yivunde yi ndaghu dusambu, na bakemudimbe va mune ndaghu mighaghe. Tumbe Ghalyone asamadilabe yi dyambu.
ACT 18:18 Pole akesyale mu yitsingu o Korinte. Akekakene na baane ba ngudji, akenangeme mu watange djone Pirisile na Akilase na bakewende o Siri. Ne akebotughe musyengi, mu disabu di Senkire, amafughe muru, mumbari amava pangini ombu Nzambi.
ACT 18:19 Banotole o musyengi Yifese, Pole akesile Pirsile na Akilase. Akewende o ndaghu dusambu na akevose na baSwife.
ACT 18:20 Djowu bakemuwivule usyale yitsingu, tumbe asamasinge.
ACT 18:21 Akebasile novose: «Nughabughe ombu wenu, pa Nzambi atsisinge.» Akenangeme mu watange mu botughe Yifese, na akewende.
ACT 18:22 Anotole o musyengi Sesaré, akelewé o Serusaleme musimbe dibundu, mba akewende o Antyose.
ACT 18:23 Akevyose mwa pesu temu o Antyose, mba akewende. Aketabe yinange yi Ghalasi na Firisi, mu warise yitu yi badukitsi botsu.
ACT 18:24 Mu temu édjine, vamabe muSwife dine dyandi Apolose, mwise Alesanderi, aketole o Yifese. Amabe dibaale dimavosaange na buketi, amadjabaange burange Bisonu bi Nzambi.
ACT 18:25 Amalongu mu dyambu di Nzile Fumu, amatubulaange nolonze na yusile yotsu mu dyambu di Djesu. Amalonzu yike musamu dubatusu du San.
ACT 18:26 Amavose na ngenze djotsu o ndaghu dusambu. Banomane umuwulu, Pirisile na Akilase bakemubonge mu mutsingule kengili Nzile Nzambi.
ACT 18:27 Va djulu vane, Apolose amaronde uwende o Akaye. Baane ba ngudji bandi ba babaale na baghetu bakemuwarise mu dwendu dweni. Bakerende mughande ombu badukitsi ba yinange yéyine, yiri bakemudile ndilulu djiboti. Na etoli, amawamuse pwele, abamasinge Fumu, bakela ubwedji mu yese yi Nzambi.
ACT 18:28 Amavovene na baSwife mu ubuse mambu mowu va wusu batu botsu. Mu Bisonu bi Nzambi, amabalase yiri Djesu adji Kirisete.
ACT 19:1 Temu adji Apolose abile o Korinte, Pole aketabe yinange yi mukongu na aketole o Yifese. Akerasunu badukitsi
ACT 19:2 na ewivuli: «Dutsidile Yinyuni Yisyeme, ave dutsivayile Fumu yitu?» Bakemuwaghule yi: «Vyaghe! Tukawulu uvose adi Yinyuni Yisyeme.»
ACT 19:3 Kaboghu Pole akebawivule: «Dubatusu yi dumadile?» Bakewaghule: «Dubatusu du San.»
ACT 19:4 Pole ebatsinguli: «San amabatise bobamasinge wukalughe mitsanu noghobise Nzambi. Amatsingule batu yiri: “Vayilanu yitu mu Djesu, owurughe va djulu ami.”»
ACT 19:5 Banomane uwulu bighume byeni, akebabatusu mu dine di Fumu Djesu.
ACT 19:6 Pole akesakighe makake mu djowu na Yinyuni Yisyeme yike baveghu. Bakevose mu mambembu masusu na bakebighe mu dikabu di Nzambi.
ACT 19:7 Babaale beni bamabe dighumi na babedji (12) mu botsu.
ACT 19:8 Kale yilumbu yuvume yi baSwife, Pole amawendaange o ndaghu dusambu. Mu ngondi yiryeru, amabonge mbembu na ngenze. Amavose mu Bukaghe bu Nzambi na amawarise ubawulusu.
ACT 19:9 BaSwife bamosi bamabuse uvayile yitu, bakepedji abamaduke Nzile Fumu va wusu dibundu. Mba Pole akekakene nowu, akenebeghe badukitsi nandi. Bilumbu byotsu akebavosilaange o ndaghu yinenge dji mutu, benengili Tiranuse.
ACT 19:10 Dyoni dimatsinge bilime bibedji. Va disukusulu, batu botsu abamatsana mu yari yi Asi, baSwife na bagha baSwife, bakeghulu musamu Fumu.
ACT 19:11 Nzambi amadughusu bimaghe bineni mu makake ma musatsi andi Pole.
ACT 19:12 Bamasunzaange miswari vo bikutu abimabembaange dunyuru dwandi mu bibedu. Bibedu byeni bimabelughaange mu mali mowu na binyuni bibi bimapala mu djowu.
ACT 19:13 BaSwife bamosi, bamawendaange mbure na mbure mu syanze binyuni bibive. Bamaronde usyanze binyuni bibive mu dine di Fumu Djesu. Bamatsingula binyuni bibi: «Nyiduve dirume, dupale mu dine di Djesu adji Pole etubuli!»
ACT 19:14 Vamabe yivunde yimosi yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu ba baSwife, dine dyandi Seva. Yisambwali yi bane bandi, djowu bamavaghe mambu meni.
ACT 19:15 Tumbe yilumbu yimosi yinyuni yibi yimabawaghule: «Nyidjabi Djesu na nyidjabi anyi avu Pole. Tumbe djenu, bani duvu?»
ACT 19:16 Na djandi omabe na yinyuni yibi, akekébwaghe mu djowu mu lase yi abavyoghulile djobotsu mangolu. Amabatsoyise na bukani, na bakerine ndaghu eni, peni-wangi na mapure.
ACT 19:17 Adimavyoghe dimadjabunu na bise Yifese. BaSwife na baNgereke bamabase na ghome, bakedjabe durumu du Nzambi na buneni bu dine di Fumu Djesu.
ACT 19:18 Bapwele abamavayile yitu, bamarunga mu yidjabise mabi ame bamavaghaange.
ACT 19:19 Yinombu yeni yi batu ayimasalise ngalu, bamabeghe mabuku mowu na bamamanyenze va wusu batu botsu. Tumatale dufunu du mabuku meni: dumaveghe dighumi di senzu (50 000) tsi mbongu.
ACT 19:20 La nane mu mangolu ma Fumu, musamu wumanyavaange na wumalasaange mangolu mapwele.
ACT 19:21 Va djulu mambu meni, Pole akeghane kake djutabe Masedwane na Akaye, nowende o Serusaleme. Amavose nane: «Nyinowende, mbé nyutole o musyengi Rome wandi.»
ACT 19:22 Aketinde o yinange yi Masedwane Timote na Yirase, abamasala yisalu yowu nandi. Tumbe amasyale djabeni mwa temu o yari yi Asi.
ACT 19:23 Va temu eni, vamabe kimbu djineni o Yifese, dibandu djowu abameneduka Nzile Fumu.
ACT 19:24 Vamabe mutulitsi bapange, dine dyane Demeteyuse, amavaghe mandaghu magheyi ma nyambi owu mughetu, dine dyandi Artemise. Mandaghu meni mamavegha madile mapwele ombu batulitsi botsu.
ACT 19:25 Akebaghukighe, na botsu abedjabi yisalu nane yine, na akebatsingule: «Bambatsi, dwidjabi yi maboti meruyili mu yisalu yéyiyi.
ACT 19:26 Tumbe dwilabi na dwiwulu adivyoyi: mutu awu bénengili Pole etubuli yiri, banyambi abevaghu na makake ma batu, bagha banyambi bangenze! Aborungule ubembe bapwele tsike bu ghunu o Yifese, tumbe na mu yari yetu yotsu yi Asi.
ACT 19:27 Dyoni mbé dyubivise yisalu yetu, notsyemuse didume di ndaghu nyambi etu Artemise, obeyitsi mbure tsyotsu mu yari yi Asi na mu bulongu bwotsu.»
ACT 19:28 Mu mambu meni, abamawulu bakebase na kabu na bakeghamughe: «Yivunde djandi, Artemise dji bise Yifese!»
ACT 19:29 Mupuki wukedughunu mu musyengi wotsu. Batu bakenebeghe Ghayise na Arisitareke, bise Masedwane babedji, bamabe nandi mu mulingu na Pole. Yinombu yikewé mbangu o mbure bibengunu bi mighungi.
ACT 19:30 Pole amabe na nzale ulabene va wusu yinombu, tumbe badukitsi bakemughandise.
ACT 19:31 Bidjeti bi Asi bamabe bambatsi bandi, bakemutindile yilumbi yumutsingule, akéwende o mbure bibengunu bi yinombu.
ACT 19:32 Mu temu eni, dibundu bamabe mu nkumfu. Basusu bamaghamugha dyambu dimosi, bamosi dimosi. Bapwele va ghari owu basamadjabaange dibandu yi bamaghukimine.
ACT 19:33 BaSwife bamasindighe mutu o wusu, dine dyandi Alesandere. Akenangule dikake mu votse yinombu, mubavosile nobonge dikabu di baSwife.
ACT 19:34 Tumbe na batu bédjabi yiri muSwife, bakeghamughe djobotsu va mosi mu maweru mabedji: «Yivunde djandi nyambi Artemise dji bise Yifese!»
ACT 19:35 Anomanisile, yirende-rende yi musyengi akerungule usiyighe yinombu novose: «Bise Yifese, batu botsu bédjabi yi bise Yifese bakelitsi ba ndaghu Artemise, yibaghunu yandi yibonduyi o djulu.
ACT 19:36 Vagha mutu wughale. Mu dyoni, mbé dusigheme notase ne duke salise.
ACT 19:37 Dutsibeghe vave batu abaghabunge nosyenge Nzambi etu.
ACT 19:38 Pa Demeteyuse na bambatsi bandi ba bisalu bane mufundu na mutu, bawendi ombu banzonzi aborungule utabule dyambu. Babeyi mufundu ghune.
ACT 19:39 Na pa dune dyambu dimosi duvu na nzale ulase, tudinonze va ghari dibundu adiwelmine.
ACT 19:40 Mbé tufwengululu yiri tudji mimbini, mu dyo ditsivyoghe na nyangu, mbé tughorungule ukekaghule. Va djulu mambu meni, akekungise mughungi.»
ACT 20:1 Musighe wunoghabughe, Pole akeghukighe badukitsi nobawarise, mba akebaghanine nowende o Masedwane.
ACT 20:2 Akesabughe yari yeni, nowarise bakereti bapwele ave amavosilaange nowu. Va djulu vane, akewende o Ngerese
ACT 20:3 o amatsanine miweli miryeru. Mbé aronde unangeme mu watange nowende o Siri, ave amawululu yi baSwife bamamutungile fundu. Kaboghu, akesitighe muvyoyile adu Masedwane.
ACT 20:4 Batu abamawendaange nandi: Sopate mwane Pirise mwise Bere, Arisitareke Sekunduse bise Tesalonike, Ghayise mwise Derebe, Timote, Tisike na Torfime bise yari yi Asi.
ACT 20:5 Bane bakerele notukele o musyengi Torwase.
ACT 20:6 Yoyine djetu tumanangeme mu watange, mu wende o Filipe, yike mumengu wu bapembi abaghane dufunusu wisuki. Bilumbu biranu va djulu, tumabadale o Torwase o tumavyosile tsone mosi.
ACT 20:7 Mu yilumbu yiteghe yi tsone, tumabe tughukeme mudji va mosi. Pole amalonze dibundu, amavose pwele tena ghari wisi, mumba mbé owende va kedi.
ACT 20:8 Balambi bapwele bamabe o kilingu ndaghu adjitumabe.
ACT 20:9 Mwa munzambu wumanengulungu Yitikise amatsane va nele ndaghu. Akewende yilu yineni ave Pole amavosila. Yilu yimavyoghulile, tena ave amabonduyile kilingu adji muryeru teno tsi. Akefu.
ACT 20:10 Pole akevindeme, akemunaghule novose yi: «Dundanu wunyonge, adji monyu.»
ACT 20:11 Mba akemate, akeghabe pembi nodji. Yike emani akemwévose tinde yitsingu tena kedi, mba akewende.
ACT 20:12 Bakeghabuse munzambu monyu na dyoni dikebe tinde duwarusu ombu botsu.
ACT 20:13 Tumarele uwende mu watange adjimatubeghe o musyengi Asose, o mbé tubongile Pole. Anane amakinzile, mumba amabe na nzale uwendile mu mumbambe.
ACT 20:14 Anoturasene o Asose, tukemunangighe mu wende o musyengi Mitilene.
ACT 20:15 Vane, tukewende mu watange. Yilumbu ayimaduke tukebambene na ningi Kyo. Yilumbu yi djulu, tuketole o ningi Samose, mba ayinzime tukedale musyengi Mile.
ACT 20:16 Pole, asamaronde usikeme o musyengi Yifese, mumba diweru dikévyoghe o yari yi Asi. Amavungilaange utole o Serusaleme, pa mbé dyurungule ube yilumbu yi Patekote.
ACT 20:17 O musyengi Mile, Pole aketinde yilumbi o dibundu di Yifese mu yélande bivunde byowu.
ACT 20:18 Banotole va mughule andi, akebatsingule yi: «Dwidjabi nane nyimatsanine nenu, ubongile va yilumbu yiteghe ayi nyimaruyile o yari yi Asi.
ACT 20:19 Nyimasalile Fumu na divole-mbombu, na matsange na maghughe amenyimalabe dibandu bikumbu bi baSwife.
ACT 20:20 Dwidjabi yi nyisamasweghe ne dimosi mu motsu amawelimine. Nyimadulonze notsingule motsu, na va ghari batu na mu mandaghu menu.
ACT 20:21 Nyimanengile baSwife na baNgereke mukalughe dyele na Nzambi, novayile Fumu etu Djesu yitu.
ACT 20:22 Mba vave, yike o Serusaleme nyiwendi, nane Yinyuni Yisyeme yinzindiyili. Tumbe, ngedjabi adyutuyile ghune.
ACT 20:23 Nyidjabi yi mu kale musyengi, Yinyuni Yisyeme yindubusi yiri, tsughu na maghughe bikeli.
ACT 20:24 Tumbe, monyu ami wughane tsongu va wusu ami. Adimbuli murime, uwende teno disukusulu mu manisile yisalu ayi Fumu Djesu amapeghe. Diwendili rye: wulonze Musamu Wuboti wu yese yi Nzambi.»
ACT 20:25 «Nyimavyose temu nolonzange Bukaghe bu Nzambi, tumbe nyimadjabe yi vagha ne wumosi va ghari enu omwéndabe.
ACT 20:26 Ladibandu, nyidubongili na muni nane bambedji: yike wumosi va ghari enu etsyemuyi, nga mune dighénzuni.
ACT 20:27 Mumba nyimadulonze motsu ame Nzambi amasitighe, ne dimosi nyisamasweghe.
ACT 20:28 Dukebene djenubeni, na kelisanu mughambe, awu Yinyuni Yisyeme amaduveghe. Bandekenanu dibundu di Nzambi adi amadile mu malungu ma mwane andi.
ACT 20:29 Nyidjabi yi ave nyuwendile, batu bavu nane baminzi ba bukani bokote va ghari enu mba mughambe wughovengusu.
ACT 20:30 Mba ne va ghari enu, batu bofuraange mu dute badukitsi.
ACT 20:31 Moghanu kaboghu! Rangeminanu yi, mu bilime biryeru, na nyangu na mukolu, nyisamadunde ulile mu ulubuse kale mutu.
ACT 20:32 Vave, nyiduwakise ombu Nzambi na musamu wu yese yandi. Ane musughe uduwarise mu yitu, noduveghe disyale adi asweyile bandi.
ACT 20:33 Nyisamavonde badoli na lore, vo bikutu bi wotsu ke mutu.
ACT 20:34 Dwidjabi yi nyimasale na makake mami, mu dile abimabe biwelimine na abamandukaange.
ACT 20:35 Nyimadulase mu motsu yusale abwedji mu wamuse abadede. Mbé turangiminanu ame djabeni Fumu Djesu amavose: “Uveghe atsivyo uveghu nzangu.”»
ACT 20:36 Yike emani uvose, Pole akekuteme nowu nosambile.
ACT 20:37 Botsu bamalile pwele na matsange mu misu, bakevyunge Pole mu kingu nomughumbesene.
ACT 20:38 Bamaningaange mumba Pole amavose yi aghoghabughe. Bakeyemuvetsighe tena o watange.
ACT 21:1 Tunokakene nowu, tukesungeme o ningi Kose mu watange, yilumbu ayimadukaange tuketole o ningi Rode. Yilumbu ayimaduke tukewende o ningi Patare.
ACT 21:2 Tumadale watange djimawendaange o yinange yi Fenisi, tumabwénangeme noyenewende.
ACT 21:3 Tunolabilile ningi Sipere, tumavyole o maghetu mu wende o yari yi Siri. Tukesikeme o musyengi Tire o watange djimabe na mufune wusunduse.
ACT 21:4 Tumarasene badukitsi na tumatsane tsone nowu. Banolubusu na Yinyuni Yisyeme, bamaghandise Pole uwende o Serusaleme.
ACT 21:5 Tumbe tsone eni djinovyoghe, tukebongulile nzile. Djowu botsu bakétuvetsighe, na baghetu na bane, teno dikotulu di musyengi. Tuke kuteme va disimu di mubu nosambile Nyambi.
ACT 21:6 Tunoghanesene kale mutu, tumanangeme mu watange. Djowu bamaghabughe mu mimbu mowu.
ACT 21:7 Tumamane disabu dyetu, urambuyile o Tire teno musyengi Tolemayise. Tunomane usimbe baane ba ngudji o musyengi eni, tuketsane nowu yilumbu yimosi.
ACT 21:8 Yilumbu ayimaduke, tukesogheme notole o musyengi Sesaré. Vane, tukekote o ndaghu Filipe, musamunitsi wu Musamu Wuboti na tuketsane ombu wandi. Amabe wumosi va ghari yisambwali yi batu, abamasolu o Serusaleme mu wamuse bakwili.
ACT 21:9 Amabe na baane bana ba baghetu bamabe batsyemi, bamabighaange.
ACT 21:10 Mbé tuke bilumbu bipwele vane, ave mubiyitsi winengulu Aghabise amaruyile o Sudé.
ACT 21:11 Akebambene netu, akebonge beleti dji Pole, akekétunge makulu na makake na djoni novose yi: «La adi Yinyuni Yisyeme evosi: “Fumu beleti adjidji otungu nane na bivunde bi baSwife ba Serusaleme, mba bomuwakise ombu beni.”»
ACT 21:12 Tunowulu mane, djetu na baane ba ngudji ba Sesaré tumalende Pole akéwende o Serusaleme.
ACT 21:13 Tumbe akewake yi: «Mumba yi dililili nondetse manyuru? Nyikunzeme mutungu na muboku o Serusaleme dibandu Fumu Djesu.»
ACT 21:14 Dibilaange yi tusamarungule umusanze ditase dyandi, tumadunde utsiyise novose yi: «Durondu du Fumu duvaghu.»
ACT 21:15 Mwa bilumbu binovyoghe, tukekunzeme nomate o Serusaleme.
ACT 21:16 Badukitsi ba Sesaré bamawende netu, baketutsanise ombu Nasone, mwise Sipere, awumabe mudukitsi vane kale.
ACT 21:17 Ave tumatolile o Serusaleme, baane ba ngudji bamatusangile na nzangu.
ACT 21:18 Yilumbu ayimaduke, Pole akewende netu ombu Sake, o bivunde byotsu bi dibundu bimaghukemine.
ACT 21:19 Pole akebasimbe nobatsingule bikumbu byotsu nane Nzambi amasalile ombu abagha baSwife.
ACT 21:20 Banomuwulu bakedodise Nzambi. Mba bakevaghe Pole yi: «Wilabi, mwane-ma, tosini kwe tsi baSwife bamasinge Djesu. Djobotsu baname na Mughaghe Moyise.
ACT 21:21 Yotsu yine la adi bamabatsingule: “Wilongi baSwife botsu abetsani va ghari malongu masusu, yi badundi Mughaghe wu Moyise. Wibatsinguli yi bayamwérebaange baane bowu na bayamwéduke mighulu mi djetu baSwife.”
ACT 21:22 Tsyé tuvale? Bodjabe yi wumarughe.
ACT 21:23 Kaboghu, vaghe adi tiwutsinguli. Vave, vadji babaale bane netu batsi leve pesi ombu Nzambi.
ACT 21:24 Babeyi, djenu botsu yétsyemuswanu va wusu Nzambi. Fute byotsu mumbari bakefughu myuru. Pa dutsivaghe nane, batu botsu bodjabe yi vagha ngenze mu adi batsiwuvosile, tumbe ndewandi wighobisi mughaghe Moyise.
ACT 21:25 Mu bise malongu abamasinge Djesu, tutsibarendisile mu batsingule yi: bayabwedji banyame atsivaghulu ombu bakosi vo banyame atsighaghewu kingu mu palise malungu, mba bayavaghe bumbembu.»
ACT 21:26 Yilumbu ayimaduke, Pole akebeghe batu beni babane bakekésyemise djobotsu. Akewende o ndaghu Nzambi notsingule yilumbu ayi bovaghulile paghu na dutsyemusu du mutu-mutu dusukile.
ACT 21:27 Yisambwali yi bilumbu mbé yike usuke, ave baSwife ba yari yi Asi bamalabile Pole o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi. Bakenangule mughungi wotsu, bakemughange,
ACT 21:28 noghamughe yi: «BaYisrayele, tuwamusyanu! La mutu awilonzi batu botsu mbure tsyotsu dilongi di kondenyonde na mukute Yisrayele, mughaghe etu na mbure djisyeme. Amakotise ne abagha baSwife mu mbure édjidji na bamadjibivise.»
ACT 21:29 Pa bamadisalise, mbari bilumbu abiteghe bamalabe Torfime mwise Yifese djone Pole bamayenewendaange mu musyengi Serusaleme. Bamasingene yi Pole amamukotise o dulombili du baSwife, tumbe bamabe na mbele.
ACT 21:30 Dimbunge dikelave mu musyengi wotsu, mba batu bakepalile yari na yari na bakeghukeme. Batu bakeghange Pole, nomupalise o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi, adji bamalenge nobindighe dikotulu.
ACT 21:31 Mbé baronde uboke Pole, mu temu eni abemoyi bamayétsingule yivunde yi baghore ba Rome, yi Serusaleme djotsu ukunge djikungi.
ACT 21:32 Vane-vane yivunde akebonge baghore na bivunde byowu, nowende mbangu o mughungi. Banolabe yivunde, bakedunde udimbe Pole.
ACT 21:33 Yivunde akebambene nandi, akemughangise nomutungise na pange bedji. Mba akewivulu dine dyandi na dyambu adi amavaghe.
ACT 21:34 Tumbe mu mughungi, abéba bamaghamughaange didi, bane bamaghamughaange disusu. Yivunde mbé aghorungule ughangise dyambu na tsikiri dibandu nkumfu. Akeveghe dirume dyubeghe Pole o ndaghu baghore.
ACT 21:35 Pole anotole vo bande yikadi, baghore bakemunangule, dibandu dikani di mughungi.
ACT 21:36 Mumba batu bapwele bamamudukaange, noghamughe yi: «Afu!»
ACT 21:37 Ave bamakotisilaange Pole o ndaghu baghore, akevaghe yivunde yi: «Nine musughe uvose mwa dyambu?» Yivunde amasutu, nomuwivule yi: «Widjabi uvose mbembu baNgereke?
ACT 21:38 Kaboghu wughaa mwise Yisipete awumarombise didjunge, nobeghe tosini-djina (4 000) tsi batu na bitoghulu byowu o kumu dji ghumughe?»
ACT 21:39 Pole amawaghule yi: «Menu muSwife, uburulu o Tarese dji Silisi, mutsighe musyengi awughélibunu. Kokolu tsyaghu, singe ngavose na mughungi.»
ACT 21:40 Yivunde akemusingile dyoni. Pole, diteli va djulu yikadi, akesambe dikake ombu mughungi mudile duvotsu. Botsu bakevole «swii», mba akebavosile mu mbembu baEberu.
ACT 22:1 Pole akevose na mughungi yi: «Djenu duvu mukute wumosi nami, tséwulwanu adingivose mu kékaghule.»
ACT 22:2 Banowulu yi ebavosili mu mbembu baEberu, bakebwele usigheme. Kaboghu Pole akeghamughe:
ACT 22:3 «Nyidji muSwife, uburulu o Tarese dji Silisi. Tumbe nyimabanguyile vave Serusaleme, na nyimalongu na Ghamalyele omandonze mughaghe ba tadji betu na tsikiri. Nyimabe na yusile mu dyambu di Nzambi, nane duvu na muni.
ACT 22:4 Nyimakwane abamadukaange Nzile Fumu teno dufu. Nyimatinde baghetu na babaale o tsughu.
ACT 22:5 Yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na fundu djotsu dji bivunde bi mukute, borungule ughabuse bumbedji yi dingenze nyivosi. Djobeni bamapeghe ne mighande mi musughe muyéveghe baane ba ngudji ba baSwife ba Damase. Nyimawende o musyengi eni mughange badukitsi ba Nzile Fumu abamabe wune, nobabeghe batungu o Serusaleme mu bakilise.
ACT 22:6 Va mwangulu ave nyangu ebile va djulu muru, nyimabe mu nzile beli na Damase. Suke, yidjalale yineni ayimarambuyile o djulu yimankandile va mbure adji nyimabe.
ACT 22:7 Nyimaberughe vatsi nowulu dyufi dimavose yi: “Sole, Sole, dibandu yi winkwanini?”
ACT 22:8 Nyimawivulu yi: “Nde la nyi, Fumu?” Akekwaghule yi: “Menu la Djesu mwise Nasarete, awu wikwani.”
ACT 22:9 Abamabe nami bamalabe yidjalale, tumbe basamawulu dyufi di djandi omavosaange.
ACT 22:10 Nyimamuwivulie rye: “Yi nyuvaghe, Fumu?” Fumu amapaghe yi: “Releme, wende o musyengi Damase. Mba vane bowutsingule motsu ame wuvaghe.”
ACT 22:11 Dibilaange yi yidjalale yeni yimapaghe yidunge, abamabe konge nami, bamankaange mu dikake teno musyengi Damase.
ACT 22:12 Vane vamabe Nanyase, dibaale dimaghobisaange Nzambi nodedile mughaghe. BaSwife botsu ba Damase bamamughobisaange.
ACT 22:13 Amayitasene, akebe va mughule ami nopaghe yi: “Sole, mwane ngu ami, bongulile ulabe!” Vane temu eni, ngamwélabe.
ACT 22:14 Amabwele yi: “Nzambi bakaaghe betu amawusole kale wukedjabe durondu dwandi, na wukelabe djandi o Asungeme nowulu dyufi dyandi.
ACT 22:15 Mumba wube mbedji andi va wusu batu botsu, mu wanze adi wutsilabe nowulu.
ACT 22:16 Ka mumba yi wumwékelise? Releme, batusu notandu mabi maghu, nonengile dine dyandi.”»
ACT 22:17 «Nyimaghabughe o Serusaleme, yoyine nyimasambilaange o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi, ngadile dulasu du Nzambi.
ACT 22:18 Nyimalabe Fumu omanzingule yi: “Lenge noghusughe Serusaleme, mumba abetsani wune baghosinge bumbedji bwaghu mu menu.”
ACT 22:19 Menu nyimawake yi: “Fumu, bédjabi yi nyimawendaange mu mandaghu motsu ma tsambu ma baSwife, mu dimbise bango yitu mu ndedju, nobatinde o tsughu.
ACT 22:20 Mba ave malungu ma mbedji awu Yityene mamadekila, me wa nyimabe vane. Nyimasingisile abamamubokaange, nyimakele ne bidwaru bi abamamuboke.”
ACT 22:21 Fumu amanzingule yi: “Wende, mumba nyuwutinde vale, ombu mikute misusu!”»
ACT 22:22 Mughungi wuke wulu Pole tena posulu djusite. Mba botsu bakeghamughe: «Tutsyemusyanu mutu eni wughu! Afu! Asawelemine utsane va butambe bwébubu!»
ACT 22:23 Bamaghamughaange, bakevulaange bikutu byowu, mba baketindaange difufundu na djulu.
ACT 22:24 Yivunde yi baghore akeveghe dirume dyukotise Pole o ndaghu baghore nomudimbe mikase, mumba akevose mu udjabe dibandu yi mughungi wimughamuyili.
ACT 22:25 Tumbe ave bamamutungile mu umudimbe, Pole akewivule yivunde ayimabe vane yi: «Dune musughe wu udimbe mwise Rome mikase, awughaa ne wufundusu?»
ACT 22:26 Na ewulu nane, yivunde yi baghore akelubuse yivunde yandi: «Akemuvaghe yi tsyé wuvale? Dibaale dyédidi mwise Rome!»
ACT 22:27 Yivunde yi baghore akeyilabe Pole nomuwivule yi: «Nzinguli, ngenze wudji mwise Rome?» Pole akewaghule yi: «Yine.»
ACT 22:28 Yivunde yi baghore akewake yi: «Nyimaveghe mbongu tsipwele mu udile musughe wunengulu “mwise Rome”.» Tumbe Pole akevose yi: «Menu mwise Rome mu duburulu dwami.»
ACT 22:29 Suke, abe mbé baronde umudimbe mu umuvosise, bakekakene nandi. Djabeni yivunde yi baghore akebe na ghome, ave amadjabile yi amatungise mwise Rome na bapange.
ACT 22:30 Yivunde yi baghore amabe na nzale udjabe tsikiri adibamafwengilile Pole. Ladibandu, va kedi amamunyangulile nonengile bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na fundu djotsu dji banzonzi ba baSwife. Mba akebeghe Pole va wusu owu.
ACT 23:1 Pole akesikighe yiswisu mu fundu dji banzonzi ba baSwife, novose yi: «Bane ba tadji, na matase malyome, nyisalili Nzambi tena na muni.»
ACT 23:2 Yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu Ananyase, akeveghe musughe ombu bobamabe beli na Pole, wumudimbe mu munu.
ACT 23:3 Kaboghu Pole akevaghe yi: «Nzambi aléwudimbe, na deti aghu! Wutsane vane mu ufundise nane mughaghe wirondili, mba wumabise mughaghe noveghe mu usughe wu undimbe!»
ACT 23:4 Abamabe va mughule Pole, bakemutsingule yi: «Yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu yi Nzambi wisyengi!»
ACT 23:5 Pole akewaghule yi, «Bane ba tadji, ngadjabaange yi yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu. Ngenze, Bisonu bi Nzambi bivosi yi: “Wughovose dibi mu yivunde yi mukute aghu!”»
ACT 23:6 Pole amadjabaange yi fundu djimabe djibase yari ayéyi baFarisi, yari ayine baSadisi. Ladibandu, amaghamuyile va wusu fundu dji banzonzi: «Bane ba tadji, nyidji muFarisi, mwane muFarisi. Nyifundusulu, mumba nyivu na yitu mu durambughulu du abafu.»
ACT 23:7 Mbé asekamane ne uvose, baFarisi na baSadisi bakebande utsunde, mba vakebe dupasu va ghari owu.
ACT 23:8 BaSadisi, bévosi yi vagha durambughulu o dufu, bemwévose yi vagha byanze na binyuni. Yotsu yine, baFarisi bémasingi yi mangenze.
ACT 23:9 Mighamu yike la viri. Milonzi mi mighaghe, abamabe na baFarisi, bakereleme notsunde na yikanene: «Tughélabi dibi mu mutu éwuwu. Tangudji yinyuni vo yanze yitsimuvosile?»
ACT 23:10 Mutsundu wukevyoghulile, tena yivunde yi baghore amawulu ghome bakéboke Pole. Ladibandu, amaveyile baghore bandi dirume dyuyébapatule Pole, nomughabuse o ghari ndaghu baghore.
ACT 23:11 Mukolu awumaduke, Fumu akelabene na Pole nomutsingule yi: «Ware! Wutsikabusile bumbedji o Serusaleme, na diwelimine wukelase bumbedji o musyengi Rome wandi.»
ACT 23:12 Va kedi adjimaduke, baSwife baketunge fundu. Bakeleve pesi yi baghodji vo unu, pa bakaboke Pole.
ACT 23:13 Abamatunge fundu eni, bamabe bavyoghe maghumi-mana (40).
ACT 23:14 Bakérasene bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na bivunde bi baSwife, mu batsingule yi: «Tutsileve pesi va wusu Nzambi yi tughodji yisalu, pa tukaboke Pole.
ACT 23:15 Kaboghu, djenu na fundu djotsu dji banzonzi, vaghanu yivunde yi baghore akebeghe Pole, dukefure yi dwirondi ukelule dyambu dyandi na burange. O yetu yari, tukunzeme mu muboke ne aketole vave.»
ACT 23:16 Tumbe mwane-katsi Pole, mwane yibusi yandi, amawulu fundu eni. Akewende o ndaghu baghore, akekote nolubuse Pole.
ACT 23:17 Kaboghu Pole akenengile yivunde yi baghore yimosi nomuvaghe yi: «Beghe munzambu éwuwu ombu yivunde, mumba ane mwa dyambu erondi umutsingule.»
ACT 23:18 Yivunde akemubeghe ombu yivunde yandi, novose yi: «Mwise tsughu winengulu Pole, atsipaghe nga wubeyile munzambu eni wuwu, mungo dyambu dyuwutsingule.»
ACT 23:19 Yivunde yi baghore akebonge munzambu mu dikake, akevengeme nandi nomuwivule yi: «Yi wirondi unzingule?»
ACT 23:20 Akewake yi: «Bidjeti bi baSwife batsiwulusunu mu wuwivule yi wukebeghe Pole mughese va wusu fundu djotsu dji banzonzi. Bofure yi bérondi uwulu dyambu dyandi burange.
ACT 23:21 Tumbe wuyabavayile yitu! Mumba abémutungili fundu bavyoghe ne maghumi-mana (40) ma batu. Batsileve pesi va wusu Nzambi yi baghodji vo unu, pa bakamuboke. Bamakunzeme na békeli yike musughe aghu.»
ACT 23:22 Yike emani urume munzambu yi ayavose dyambu dyeni na mutu, yivunde yi baghore akemughabuse.
ACT 23:23 Mba yivunde yi baghore akenengile batsyengi bandi babedji nobarume yi: «Ghukighanu kame-bedji (200) tsi baghore, na maghumi-dusambwali (70) ma babeyitsi ba bibulu na kame-bedji (200) tsi babaale na makongu, na banu djenu botsu na dubayi duwende o Sesaré, va maweru maryéru ma tsisighe.
ACT 23:24 Kunzanu bibulu duke beghe Pole na burange ombu yivunde yami Felikese.»
ACT 23:25 Mba akerende mughande eni wughu:
ACT 23:26 «Menu Kolode Lisyase, nyiwutindili mughade ewuwu mundumbe Felikese.
ACT 23:27 Dibale dyédidi, BaSwife batsighaange mbé baronde umuboke, kaboghu tutsimupatule na baghore bami va makake mowu, mumba nyimawulu yi adji mwise Rome.
ACT 23:28 Nyimaronde udjabe dibandu adi bamamufwengililaange, ngamubeghe va wusu fundu dji banzonzi ba baSwife.
ACT 23:29 Nyimaghulu yi bémufwengilili mu mighaghe mi djobeni, tumbe aghane mbele dufu vo dji tsughu.
ACT 23:30 Mba nyilubusi yi vadji fundu bamutungile. Nzilenge nomutinde ombu waghu na nyivayi bambeni bandi bakeyimufunde va wusu aghu.»
ACT 23:31 Baghore bakededile marume ame bamadile. Bakebonge Pole nomubeghe mukolu o musyengi Atipareti.
ACT 23:32 Yilumbu ayimaduke, baghore abamabe mu makulu bakeghabughe o ndaghu owu, nosile babeyitsi ba bibulu uwende na Pole.
ACT 23:33 Na bétoli o Sesaré, babeyitsi ba bibulu bakeveghe yivunde mughande, nomuwakise Pole va makake mowu.
ACT 23:34 Dipateme anomane urange mughande, akemuwivule yari yi dimbu dyandi. Anowulu yi mwise Silisi,
ACT 23:35 akemuvaghe yi: «Nyuwusosise pa bambeni baghu bamarughe.» Na akeveghe musughe wukelise Pole o ndaghu kaghe Yirode.
ACT 24:1 Bilumbu biranu binovyoghe, yivunde yi bavaghulitsi ba paghu Ananyase, amarughe o musyengi Sesaré. Amarughaange va mosi na bivunde bi baSwife, na nzonzi mosi omanengulu Tertuluse. Bamayikelase ombu Dipateme Felikese mu ufunde Pole.
ACT 24:2 Pole amanengulu, nzonzi Tertuluse akemufwengilile mu mame. Akevose yi: «Mundumbe, mu yese yaghu tubile na duvotsu duneni, na mu dyele di durumu dwaghu, mambu makaluyile burange mu bulongu bwébubu.
ACT 24:3 Mu byotsu abi twidili temu tsyotsu, twiwughabusili diboti dyneni.
ACT 24:4 Ngérondi wuvyosulile mu diweru dyaghu. Ladibandu, nyighulendi mu maboti maghu, mu utuwulu mwa pesu.
ACT 24:5 Tutsikelule dibaale dyédidi na erombisi kindu. Abilaange yivunde yi mimbini mi dibuli di Nasarete, erombisi mbulighe ombu baSwife botsu ba bulongu.
ACT 24:6 Atsiwélighe ubivise ndaghu Nzambi na tutsimughange. [Tutsironde umusosise mu mughaghe etu,
ACT 24:7 tumbe yivunde Lisyase amarughe. Aketupatule woni na mangolu.
ACT 24:8 Aketuvaghe yi tukemufunde va wusu aghu.] Pa wumuwivule, wulabe ndebeni yi mfwengululu etu djotsu dji ngenze.»
ACT 24:9 BaSwife bamawarise mfwengululu owu, na bamavose yiri dingenze.
ACT 24:10 Dipateme amaveghe Pole musughe uvose na amatubule rye: «Nyidjabi yiri wisalisi bunzonzi bwaghu mu bulongu bwetu mu pwele bilime, kaboghu na musighe nyiruyi mu ukéghanze.
ACT 24:11 Nane wurungulile dikelulile ndebeni, vakavyoghe ne dighumi na bilumbu bibedji, nyimarughe o musyengi Serusaleme, mu ulembiyile Nzambi.
ACT 24:12 Vagha mutu amandabe mbure nyitsundi na batu vo urume mughungi mu dimbunge, nesi o ndaghu Nzambi dji baSwife, vo mu musyengi.
ACT 24:13 Batu bébabe baghorungule ulase dyambu adi béfwengilili.
ACT 24:14 Ne nane, nyidjabi didi va wusu waghu: nyimakéveghe mu Nzile Fumu, adji bévosi yiri duyitsu du mfurulu. Tumbe, nyisalili Nzambi dji baghulu betu, nyivayili yitu mu motsu marendu mu Mabuku ma Mighaghe na ma Babiyitsi.
ACT 24:15 Nyine yitu yi Nzambi orambuse batu botsu o dufu, bakebe baboti vo babi. Na djowu abémfwengilili wandi, bane ditase yi Nzambi obarambuse va ghari abafu.
ACT 24:16 Ladibandu, nyilembinini ube na mutsanu wuwelimine va wusu Nzambi na va wusu batu.»
ACT 24:17 «Nyisamabe va ghari enu mwa bilime, nyimaghabusile o Serusaleme mu wamuse mukute ami na mbongu, nowakise paghu tsyami ombu Nzambi.
ACT 24:18 Nyinomane ughabusile paghu, bamantasunu o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi. Vane mbé nyimamane misusu mi manyuru. Vasamabe mughungi nami ne nkumfu.
ACT 24:19 Tumbe, mwa dibuli di baSwife ba yari yi Asi dimabe vane wandi. Djowu, mbé batsikelase va wusu aghu mu mfwengilile, pa bane dyambu mu menu.
ACT 24:20 Batu bébabe banzinguli dibi adi nyibile na mbele, adi nzibeghulu va wusu fundu dji banzonzi.
ACT 24:21 Muvingu yike mbembu adji nzipalise na dwufi dineni, diteli va wusu owu: “Mumbari nyivayili yitu mu durambughulu du abafu, adine nyimabile na nyangu mu bunzonzi va wusu enu!”»
ACT 24:22 Felikese, omadjabaange burange motsu ametsuni Nzile Fumu. Amavose na abémumfwengilili yi: «Ave yivunde Lisyase oruyile, nyusosise dyambu dyenu.»
ACT 24:23 Amarume yivunde yi baghore mu kelisa Pole o tsughu, nomusingise dudjeghusu na musughe yiri bambatsi bandi bomusalile.
ACT 24:24 Mwa bilumbu binovyoghe, Felikese amarughe na mughatsi andi Duresile, omabe muSwife. Amasindighe unengile Pole nowulu adi amavose mu dyambu di yitu mu Djesu Kirisete.
ACT 24:25 Pole amavosile mu mutsanu wuboti awu Nzambi erondi, ube na murime usunde na mufundu Nzambi awiruyi. Mu temu eni, Felikese, asamalabe ubwedji, amamutsingule rye: «Wurungule uwende. Ave nyudilile temu, nyuwunengile.»
ACT 24:26 Amatase yiri Pole omusumbe na mbongu. Ladibandu, amamunengililaange temu na temu mu vosaange nandi.
ACT 24:27 Bilime bibedji bimavyoghe, va djulu vane Porekuse Fesetuse amavinze Felikese. Djandi, mu ulase baSwife ubwedji, amasile Pole o tsughu.
ACT 25:1 Va djulu bilumbu biryeru bi durughu dwandi mu musyengi Serusaleme, kaghe Fesetuse amaghusughe o Sesaré na amawende o Serusaleme.
ACT 25:2 Bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na barumitsi ba baSwife bamarughe mu ufundise Pole.
ACT 25:3 Bamamuwivule ubasingise yese yi ughabuse Pole o Serusaleme. Na vane, bamatunge fundu mu djandi mu muboke mu nzile.
ACT 25:4 Tumbe Fesetuse amawaghule yiri Pole adji o tsughu o Sesaré, na djabeni aghotambe ughabughe na mapape.
ACT 25:5 Na amabwele: «Bivunde byenu bisobini konge nami o Sesaré na ghune bafwengilili mutu eni, pa atsisalise dibi.»
ACT 25:6 Fesetuse amavyose yinane vo dighumi di bilumbu ombu wowu, mbana amaghabughe o musyengi Sesaré. Ave kedi, amatsane o mbure bunzonzi na amaveghe dirume bakebeghe Pole va wusu andi.
ACT 25:7 Ave bamamubeyile, baSwife abamarughe o Serusaleme bamamutsyengile na bamamufwengilile mambu mapwele, ame djowu baghorungule ulase yi mangenze.
ACT 25:8 Pole amakéghanze novose rye: «Ngasalise ne dibi dimosi: nesi mu mughaghe baSwife, nesi na ndaghu dji Nzambi, vo na kaghe Sesare.»
ACT 25:9 Fesetuse, omaronde ulase baSwife ubwedji, amawivule Pole: «Wirondi uwende o Serusaleme mu usosusu va wusu ami mu dyambu dyeni?»
ACT 25:10 Pole amawake: «Nyidji va ndaghu bunzonzi dji kaghe Sesare, avane nyutabululu bunzonzi. Ngavayile dibi ombu mukute baSwife, nane ndebeni wididjabili.
ACT 25:11 Pa nine mbele na ta nyimasalise dyambu adi nyubokulu, ngébusi ufu. Tumbe pa vagha dyambu di ngenze adi batu beni bémfwengilili, vagha mutu avu na musughe wu ukwakise ombu owu. Nyibwayi mbile ombu kaghe Sesare aketabule dyambu dyami.»
ACT 25:12 Kaboghu Fesetuse, anotabule dyambu na fundu banzonzi bandi, amawake: «Wumabwa mbile ombu kaghe Sesare, uwende va wusu andi.»
ACT 25:13 Mwa bilumbu binovyoghe, kaghe Agheripa na, mwane ngudji andi mughetu Berenise, bamatole o Sesaré mu uyélingulu noyisimbe Fesetuse.
ACT 25:14 Banotsane mwa bilumbu, Fesetuse amatolise dyambu di Pole ombu kaghe Agheripa: «Vadji mutu vave awu Felikese amasile o tsughu.
ACT 25:15 Ave nyimawendile o Serusaleme, bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu na bivunde bi baSwife, bamamufwengilile na bamankwivule umukilise.
ACT 25:16 Nyimabawaghule rye: “Bise Rome baghane yufu yuwakise oyifwengululu ombu banzonzi, pa akaveghu temu djukéghanze va wusu bafwengilitsi.”
ACT 25:17 Batsirughe ghunu nami. Nyisamavyose temu kulini, nyimatsane va mbure bunzonzi, ave kedi, nyimarume yiri babeyi dibaale dyeni.
ACT 25:18 Bafwengilitsi batsikélase, tumbe mu fwengululu owu, ngawulu mabi motsu nyimatase.
ACT 25:19 Babetsi na mitsundu mu dyambu di munongu duyitsu doghu du Nzambi na dibaale dinengulu Djesu adjimafu, adji Pole amatubule yiri aki monyu.
ACT 25:20 Mu menu, nyimakambulu yari ayi ngabe mu mutsundu eni. Adine nyimamuwivule yeri esingi uwende o Serusaleme, mu usosise dyambu dyandi ghune.
ACT 25:21 Tumbe Pole amawivule, yiri dyambu dyandi dyutsonzughu mu kake dji kaghe Sesare. Ladibandu, nyimarumine yiri akekelusu o tsughu, tena nyumusindighe ombu kaghe Sesare.»
ACT 25:22 Agheripa amatsingule Fesetuse rye: «Nyirondi uwulu mebeni mutu eni.» Fesetuse amawaghule yi: «Mughese wumuwulu.»
ACT 25:23 Ave kedi, Agheripa na Berenise bamarughe na mughungi wuneni wumabayitsaange nobasangile na milolu. Yike djowu, bakekote o ndaghu bunzonzi na bivunde bi baghore na bi musyengi. Mu dirume di Fesetuse, Pole amabeghu.
ACT 25:24 Mbana kaghe Fesetuse amavose: «Kaghe Agheripa, na djenu botsu aduvu vave netu, dwilabi dibaale dyédidi. Yinombu yotsu yi baSwife yi tsirughe, ubandile o Serusaleme tena ghunu, noghamughe yi mutu eni ayamwébe monyu.
ACT 25:25 Tumbe menu, nyimalabe yiri asamavaghe dyambu adi mbé ofwile. Va djulu vane, djandi amabwa mbile ombu kaghe Sesare Okisete bwendiri djandi akemusosise. Ladibandu, nyimamutindile ombu kaghe Sesare.
ACT 25:26 Vave, nyisane dyambu disusu dyusonine yivunde yetu mu mutu éwuwu. Ladibandu, nyimutindili va wusu enu, viri va wusu aghu, ndedju kaghe Agheripa. Pa wune bivu byumuwivule, mba nyube na dyambu dyusone.
ACT 25:27 Nyilabi yiri digha diwelimine mu utinde mwise tsughu o Rome, ta vagha tonu adjitsiyisi mfwengululu andi.»
ACT 26:1 Kaghe Agheripa amatsingule Pole: «Wune musughe wu uvose mu kéghanze.» Kaboghu Pole amasambe dikake la nane amakéghanzile.
ACT 26:2 Akevose rye: «Kaghe Agheripa, na muni nyilabi ubwedji mu ukéghanze va wusu aghu, mu motsu ame bivunde bi baSwife bémfwengilili.
ACT 26:3 Mumbari widjabi burange nzalusulu tsyotsu tsi baghulu ba baSwife na nzundulu owu. Kokolu tsyaghu, nyighulendi kululwati na pughu.
ACT 26:4 BaSwife nami botsu bédjabi monyu ami wughulu, ubande bungebi bwami. Bédjabi nane nyimatsanine vane dibandu va ghari mukute ami o Serusaleme.
ACT 26:5 Bénzyabi vane kale na borungule unkabusile bumbedji, pa batsironde. Bédjabi wandi, yiri nyimabeyise monyu ami va ghari mukute ami nodedili mighaghe mi baSwife mi bateme, diwendili yi: ami dibuli di baFarisi.
ACT 26:6 Na muni, nyimasutusu va wusu bunzonzi, mumbari nyivayili yitu mu pangini adji Nzambi amavangene na baghulu betu.
ACT 26:7 Dighumi na bibandu bibedji bi mukute etu, bévivi na yitu yiri pangini djuduwusu, ave béyitsili Nzambi na yikanene nyangu na mukolu. Wulwati kaghe Agheripa! Mu dyambu di yitu yeni, baSwife bémfwengilili.
ACT 26:8 Dibandu yi wumosi va ghari enu, olabile yiri Nzambi aghorungule urambuse djowu abafu?
ACT 26:9 Mebeni, nyimatase utoyise Djesu mwise Nasarete na mangolu mami.
ACT 26:10 Yine, adine nyimavaghe mu batu ba Djesu abamabe o Serusaleme. Nyimadile musughe wu muvingu na bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu, na nyimakotise yinombu yi djowu bango yitu mu djandi o tsughu. Ave bamaveyilaange musughe wu uboke batu beni, nyimabawarisaange.
ACT 26:11 Temu na temu, nyimavyoghaange mu mandaghu mowu ma tsambu, na nyimabakilisaange mbana nyimabaghome ubunze yitu yowu. Mu bukanyi bwami, nyimabakwanaange tena misyengi mi beni.»
ACT 26:12 «Anane nyimawendile o musyengi Damase oyésale yisalu, mu durumu na musughe abimapeghu na bivunde bi bavaghulitsi ba paghu.
ACT 26:13 Kaghe Agheripa, nyimabe mu nzile, mwangulu ave nyimalabile yidjalale yineni ayimaruyile o djulu, uvyolile ne nyangu. Yidjalale yeni yimavedemaange mba yiketughumbe, menu na balinzi nami.
ACT 26:14 Djetu botsu tumaberughe vatsi na nyimawulu dyufi dimavose mu mbembu baEberu: “Sole, Sole, dibandu yi winkwanini? Wa mwenzile wiwarili, nane yibulu ewarili na ngwangu fumu andi.”
ACT 26:15 Nyimawivule: “Nde la nyi, Fumu?” Na Fumu amakwaghule: “Menu la Djesu, awu wikwani.
ACT 26:16 Tumbe simbughe na releme, nyimalabene naghu, nyimawusole mu ube musatsi ami. Wube mbedji ami mu usamune nane wutsilabile na ame nyuwulase o wusu.
ACT 26:17 Nyuwughobule va ghari mukute aghu, baSwife na mikute misusu ami nyuwusindiyile.
ACT 26:18 Nyiwusindiyi mu ubadibule misu, mu ubarambuse o piseme nobaghabuse o yidjalale, na mu ubadusule otsi durumu du Dyabu na mu ubakotise o bundumbe bu Nzambi. Pa batsimpayile yitu, mabi mowu motandu, bodile mbure na djowu abamatsyemusu mu yitu mu menu.”»
ACT 26:19 «Fumu ami Agheripa, va djulu vane, nyisamalenze dirume di yiryaryamu ayimaruyile o djulu.
ACT 26:20 Tumbe téteghe, nyimalonze bise Damase na bise Serusaleme, na djowu abavu o yinange yi Sudé, tena batu ba malongu masusu. Nyimabatsingule yiri: “Kalughanu mutsanu enu, na ghélughanu ombu Nzambi na lasanu dukalughu dwenu mu bisalu byenu.”
ACT 26:21 Ladibandu, baSwife bamakangile ave nyimabile o dulombili du ndaghu Nzambi na bamaronde umboke.
ACT 26:22 Tumbe Nzambi amakaghe tena yilumbu yéyiyi na nyidji vave mu uveghe bumbedji bwami ombu botsu: bagheyi na baneni. Ngévosi masusu yike ame babiyitsi na Moyise bamatubule yiri morughe.
ACT 26:23 Diwendili yiri: Yibyatsi yi Nzambi otsoghe, obe awuteghe mu urambughe va ghari abafu na oyesamune yidjalale yi dughobutsu ombu mukute etu, nombu malongu masusu.»
ACT 26:24 Ave Pole amavosilaange mu kéghanze, Fesetuse amaghamughe: «Nde wumalawughe, Pole! Wumawidji pwele, la dibandu wumalawuyile.»
ACT 26:25 Pole amamuwake rye: «Menu nga dilaghu, mundumbe Fesetuse. Bighume abinyipalisi bingenze tsi mavovose.
ACT 26:26 Kaghe Agheripa amadjabaange dyambu di Djesu adimavyoghe, adine mewandi ni divosili na musighe va wusu andi. Dyambu dyeni dimavyole va misu mandi, nine yitu bwé vagha yime ayi mbé aghorungule udjabe.
ACT 26:27 Kaghe Agheripa, nde wivayili yitu mu motsu amamabighu na babiyitsi? Nyidjabi yiri wimavayili yitu!»
ACT 26:28 Agheripa amatsingule Pole rye: «Witasi wupaghe Kereti, mu mwa pesu temu nane?»
ACT 26:29 Pole amawaghule: «Dikebe na mapape vo vane wusu, nyisambili Nzambi tsike mu nde pinze, tumbe na botsu abénkulu na nyangu, dube nane menu, uvinguse bapange beni babe nyikapulu.»
ACT 26:30 Kaghe na dipateme di musyengi, Berenise na botsu abamabe vane, bamareleme.
ACT 26:31 Banokakene, bamatsingusene djobeni na djobeni: «Mutu éwuwu aghavaghe dibi adyumurombise dufu nokotusu o tsughu.»
ACT 26:32 Na Agheripa amatsingule Fesetuse: «Mutu éwuwu turungule umudjeyise, mbé agharonde yiri kaghe Sesare aketabule dyambu dyandi.»
ACT 27:1 Dinotabulu yiri tuwende mu watange o bulongu bu Yitali, Pole na bise tsughu bamosi, bamawakusu yivunde yi baghore ba Rome, dine dyandi Sulyuse, yivunde mu dibuli di «Batoyitsi ba Kaghe.»
ACT 27:2 Tumanangeme mu watange dji Aderamite, adjimawendesenaange o yisyeni yi Asi, na tumawende. Arisitareke, mwise Masedwane dji Tesalonike, amabe netu.
ACT 27:3 Va kedi tumatole o musyengi Sidone. Sulyuse, omakélisaange Pole na musighe, amamusingise uwende ombu bambatsi bandi, mu udile ayi amabe na nzale.
ACT 27:4 Tunoghusughe vane, tumanangeme mu watange novyoyile mu mughule ningi dji Sipere o yari ayi punge djisamabe djivyoghulile, mumbari djimaruyilaange o wusu yetu.
ACT 27:5 Tunosabughe mubu beli na bulongu bu Silisi na Pafili, na tumatole o musyengi Mire wu Lisi.
ACT 27:6 Vane, yivunde yi baghore ba Rome yimarasunu watange dji Alesanderi, adjimawendaange o bulongu bu Yitali na amatunangise mune.
ACT 27:7 Mu pwele bilumbu, tumawendaange va ghéghéyi. Na maghughe maneni, tumarungulile utole va wusu musyengi Sinide. Tumbe punge djimatuvurise mu uwende na wusu. Tumavyoyile va dinzongi di Salmoné, teno divengi di ningi dji Kerete.
ACT 27:8 Tumawende na maghughe maneni mu mughule disimu na tumatole va mbure djinengule «Masabu Maboti», beli na musyengi Lasé.
ACT 27:9 Mulingu etu tena vave wumabonge pwele bilumbu. Va djulu vane, dimabe divure uwende mu watange na wusu. Yilumbu yimanegulu «yuwarile nzale» mbé yimavyoge. Kale yilime mu temu eni, punge djimabande uvotse pwele. Ladibandu, Pole amalubusili basalitsi ba watange:
ACT 27:10 «Bambatsi bami, nyilabi yiri mulingu wurange. Watange na bime byudyame na djetubeni wandi turungulu utsyemuse myoni.»
ACT 27:11 Tumbe yivunde yi baghore amavayile yitu mu munu fumu watange na mubeyitsi djoni, divyakene na mbembu Pole.
ACT 27:12 Va djulu vane, bapwele abamabe mu watange bamawulusunu mu wusughe vane, mumbari yisyeni yeni yisamabe yiwelimine mu vyosile mvule. Bamaronde utole o yisyeni yi Fenikese dji Kerete, o yari ayi mupunge wughépepili pwele, ayisungesene na awu wisi etsimini. Bamaronde usyale vane, tena mvule djuvyoyile.
ACT 27:13 Mwa dupepi du bande dumavughe, bamatase udughusu mulingu owu. Na bamanyangule kunge adjimaghanga watange na bamavyoghe va mughule disimu di Kerete.
ACT 27:14 Tumbe, punge djineni adjinengulu «Yirakilone», djimasundughe o mikongu mi ningi.
ACT 27:15 Watange djimavevughe: dimabe divure mu djibeyise dibandu mungudi, tena tumakesilile ubeghusu.
ACT 27:16 Tumavyoyile o bande ningi djigheyi djinengulu Koda, o disimu adi mupunge wusamabe mangolu, ave tumadilile yivumunu mwa pesu. Va djulu vane, na purulu tsipwele tumarungule usiyighe bwatu bugheyi abutungu mu watange.
ACT 27:17 Basatsi banodute bwatu, bamabunangule na bamabunangighe o ghari watange, mbana bamavyose mikudu otsi notsyengise watange mu udji warise. Bamadumaange uyékébwaghe mu maghuki ma yisyeke ma Sirete amamabe mu yisyeni yi Lybi, la dibandu bamasundusile kunge mu udetse mwendu watange.
ACT 27:18 Yilumbu ayimaduke, Mungudi wumabwela utupupise na mangolu, la dibandu basatsi bamabande ubwaghe dikabu di maboti amamabe mu watange mu mubu.
ACT 27:19 Yilumbu ayimuryeru, bamabwaghe na makake mowu, bisalulu bi watange.
ACT 27:20 Mu bilumbu bipwele, tusamamwélabaange ne nyangu, ne bambwuélili. Punge djimavyoghulile uvepe na mangolu. Na va djulu vane, tukane yitu yughobulu.
ACT 27:21 Mu temu eni djine, botsu abamabe mu watange, mbé bakeyitsingu yineni nodji. Kaboghu Pole, amareleme va wusu owu na amavose: «Bambatsi bami, mbé dumakululu na mbé dusamarambughe o ningi Kerete, mungudi mbé usamadubembe na mbé tughatsyemuse nobunge bimi.
ACT 27:22 Tumbe vave, nyidunengili mu ube na duwarusu, mumbari vaghobe ne wumosi awutsyemuse monyu. Muvingu yike watange adjubungene.
ACT 27:23 Mu mukolu eni, yanze yi Nzambi adji ndile na adji nyisalili, yike bambene nami.
ACT 27:24 Na yitsinzingule: “Wuyalabe ghome, Pole! Vengu wuvyoghe va wusu kaghe Sesare. Mu maboti mandi mu ndedju, Nzambi ewusingisi monyu batu botsu abavu naghu.”
ACT 27:25 Banu abaware, bambatsi bami, mumbari nyine yitu mu Nzambi. Dyube nane dimanzingululu.
ACT 27:26 Watange djudyame ave tubile beli na mwa ningi.»
ACT 27:27 Dimabe mukolu awu dighumi na mwina (14) bi mungudi wumatusindilaange o mubu wu Méditerane. Beli va ghari wisi, basalitsi ba watange bamatase yiri tuke beli na butambe.
ACT 27:28 Bamawélighe ndonge na bamalabe yiri mambe mamabe madonge mu maghumi-maryeru na yisambwali (37) yi byetsu. Mwa pesu o wusu, bamamwéwélighe na bamalabe maghumi ma bedji na yinane (28) yi byetsu.
ACT 27:29 Bamadumange yiri watange djikéwubene mu dimani. Ladibandu, bamabwayile kunge djine o nzime mu udetse mwendu watange na bakevivaange ditebughulu di wisi.
ACT 27:30 Ne nane, basalitsi bamaronde urine mu watange. La dibandu, bamasunduse bwatu mu mambe na bakerombe yighume yusunzile kunge o wusu watange.
ACT 27:31 Pole amatsingule yivunde na baghore basuse: «Pa batu bébaba baghatsane o ghari watange, dughorungulu ughobulu!»
ACT 27:32 Kaboghu, baghore bamatabule mikudu amimasikigha watange na bamabusile uvevughe.
ACT 27:33 Ne wisi uketébughe, Pole amabarume udji, novose rye: «Lanu, na muni dighumi na bilumbu bina (14), dwivivili na manyoni ughambu udji.
ACT 27:34 Nyiduwarisi mu ubonge bighudji, mumbari dune nzale byonyi dukeghobulu. Vaghobe ne mutu wumosi awutsyemuse ne dunange dumosi du muru!»
ACT 27:35 Anomane uvose, Pole amabonge dipe, amaghabusile Nzambi diboti va wusu botsu, mbana amabaghabile na amabande udji.
ACT 27:36 Botsu bamadile duwarusu, na djowu bamadji.
ACT 27:37 Tumabe mu watange, kame-bedji maghumi dusambwali na batu ba syamunu (276) mu botsu.
ACT 27:38 Ave mutu-mutu amamanine udji na uwukuru, bamabwaghe byotsu abimasyale mu bakomi o mubu mu lengsene watange.
ACT 27:39 Wisi wunotebughe, basalitsi ba watange basamamwédjabe ningi, tumbe bamalabile dukweku na bamaghane kake mu utsyekighe watange mu yisyeyi.
ACT 27:40 Bamanyangule kunge na bamadjisile uwende mu mubu. Bamanyangule va mosi mikudu mi yivepi. Na bamatunge tsande o wusu watange, yiri punge odjisindile na bamawendusu o dukweku.
ACT 27:41 Tumbe bamatole va yinzunze yi yisyeyi na watange djimasikeme. Wusu watange wukekote mu yisyeyi na djisamamwékunge, matine mamapanzighe na mangolu ma mibidji.
ACT 27:42 Baghore bamaronde uboke bise tsughu, yiri ne wumosi aghodile urine noryale.
ACT 27:43 Tumbe yivunde yi baghore, na nzale ughobule Pole, amabaghandise. Amarume botsu abédjabi uryale, bareli mu mambe mu usabughe o disimu.
ACT 27:44 Bane bamabadukaange banangeme va djulu tsimbi na basusu bamaryalaange ubongile ghune watange. Anane djetu botsu tumaghobuyile.
ACT 28:1 Tunoghobulu, tumadjabe yiri ningi eni adjitumabe, djinengulu Malete.
ACT 28:2 Bise ningi abasamavosaange mbembu Ngereke bamatudile na musighe. Mvule djimamwénoghe na wumabe yotsi, kaboghu bamabanze mudji wuneni na bamatudile djetu botsu.
ACT 28:3 Pole anoboole dighuki di batsyenzu mu utume o mudji, pili djimapale na mbabisile na djimaghobe mu dikake dyandi.
ACT 28:4 Ave bise ningi bamalabile pili djivyunge mu dikake di Pole, bamatsingusene yi: «Dibaale dyédidi adji yikongu, mumbari bunzonzi bu Nzambi bughémusingisi udile monyu, ne nana atsighobululu mu mubu.»
ACT 28:5 Tumbe Pole amanyaghule nyoghe o ghari mudji, ne udile bwali.
ACT 28:6 Bamatasa yiri orande vo ufu, tumbe banokélise yitsingu. Bamalabe yiri aghédili dyambu, bamavinze posulu novose, kaboghu adji wumosi va ghari banyambi.
ACT 28:7 Beli na mbure eni vamabe kande dji yivunde yi ningi, dibaale dine dyandi Publyuse. Djandi amatudile burange na amatulatse bilumbu biryeru.
ACT 28:8 Tadji Publyuse amabe va tangi, amabe na dibaghu na amavanze malungu. Pole amawende ombu wandi, anosambile Nzambi, amamusakighe makake na djandi amabelughe.
ACT 28:9 Va djulu vane, batu basusu ba ningi abamabe nobele, bamarughe na bamabelughe.
ACT 28:10 Bamatughobise mu minongu myotsu. Temu djuwende mu watange djinotole, bamatuveghe byotsu abimabe biwelimine na mulingu.
ACT 28:11 Miweli miryeru minovyoghe, tumanaangeme mu watange dji Alesanderi, bamanengilaange «Mavase», djimavyose mvule va yisyeni yi ningi.
ACT 28:12 Tumatole o musyengi Sirakuse, avane tumatsane bilumbu biryeru.
ACT 28:13 Tunoghusughe vane, tumaduke mughule tena tumatole o musyengi Redjo. Ave kedi, punge adji bande dji mapepe, mbana tumatole mu bilumbu bibedji tena o musyengi Puzole otumasunduyile.
ACT 28:14 Mune musyengi eni, tumadale baane ba ngudji, bamatulende uvyose tsone nowu. Anane tumatolile o bulongu bu Rome.
ACT 28:15 Baane ba ngudji ba Rome banowulu bilumbi mu dyambu dyetu, bamayitubengusune va dibaghe dinengulu «Apyuse» na musyengi winengulu «Mandaghu Maryeru ma Beni». Pole anobalabe, amaghabusile Nzambi diboti na amawarusu.
ACT 28:16 Tunotole o Rome, bamasingise Pole ube na djandi mbure vike, na ghore adjimamukelisaange.
ACT 28:17 Bilumbu biryeru binovyoghe, Pole amanengile ombu wandi bivunde bi baSwife abavu o Rome. Banoghukeme, amabatsingule: «Bane batadji, ne nane nyisamavayile dyambu divyakene na mutsanu mukute etu vo na nzalusulu dji baghulu betu. Ne nane, nyimaghangu o Serusaleme, nowakusu ombu bise Rome.
ACT 28:18 Banonkwivule byuvu, basusu mbé baronde undunde, mumbari basamadile dyambu mu menu adyumfundisile vo dyumbokile.
ACT 28:19 Tumbe barumitsi ba baSwife bamabuse, kaboghu nyimanengile Kaghe Sesare. Nyisamabe na ditase dyufwengilili bise bulongu bwami.
ACT 28:20 Ladibandu, nyimarondile ubengunu nenu no duvosile. Va djulu vane, nyitungu na bapange beni babe, dibandu djandi awu mukute Yisrayele wivivi.»
ACT 28:21 Bamamuwawule rye: «Tusamadile mighande mi Sudé mu dyambu dyaghu, ne mwane tadji mosi asamarughesene ghune, mu ututsingule mambu vo mu uvosile dibi.
ACT 28:22 Tumbe, twirondi wuketutsingule ndebeni dyambu adi witasi, mumbari twidjabi yiri mbure tsyotsu, wudji batu bévosi dibi mu nde.»
ACT 28:23 Bamavangene na Pole, na yilumbu yi ndayi, bamarughe yinombu yineni nomurasune va mbure adji amatsanine. Ubande kedi tena tsisighe, Pole amabavindiyile mambu. Amabasamunine Bukaghe bu Nzambi, amarombe ubasungighe mu dyambu di Djesu, na akerangaange na dyufi dineni, mighaghe mi Moyise na mabuku ma Babiyitsi.
ACT 28:24 Bamosi bamabembu na mambu ame amavosaange, tumbe basusu bamabuse umavayile yitu.
ACT 28:25 Ave bamabandile uwende ughambu uwulusunu, Pole amabatsingule didi rye: «Yinyuni Yisyeme yimabe na ndunge, ave amavosilaange na baghulu benu mu munu mubiyitsi Yisayi!
ACT 28:26 Yimavosaange rye: “Yétsingule mukute éwuwu: Duwulu, tumbe dughotsiyise. Dughengile, tumbe dugholabe.
ACT 28:27 Mumbari mukute éwuwu wuke mbike. Bamadibighe matudji, bamatsimise misu, yiri bakélabe na misu mowu, bakéwulu na matudji mowu, bakétsiyise na mirime myowu. Ubuse nane, mbé boghabughe ombu wami, yiri nyubabeluse.”»
ACT 28:28 Pole amabwese rye: «Djabanu didi Nzambi amatinde musamu wu dughobutsu ombu abagha baSwife. Bomuwululu djowu!» [
ACT 28:29 Mu bighume byeni bi Pole, baSwife bamawende notsundaange va ghari owu.]
ACT 28:30 Pole amatsane mipume mibedji mu ndaghu adji amafutaange. Amadile botsu abamarondaange umulabe.
ACT 28:31 Amalonzaange Bukaghe bu Nzambi na mambu ameghéngili Fumu Djesu Kirisete, na musighe wughambu ukungusu.
JAM 1:1 Awu menu Sake nyirendi mughande éwuwu. Nyidji musatsi Nzambi na Fumu Djesu Kirisete. Nyisimbi mukute wotsu wu Nzambi awuvu wupanzighe mu bulongu bwotsu.
JAM 1:2 Baane ba tadji bami! Pa maghughe maminongu mipwele meduruyili, banu mu nzangu dji neni.
JAM 1:3 Djabanu yiri, pa yitu yenu yitsiware mu maghughe, duware tinde uware.
JAM 1:4 Vengu duware teno disukusulu, na dube duwelimine, djowu abamaneghe na bamaware mu yinyuni, mba dughoghambu na yime.
JAM 1:5 Pa wumosi va ghari enu eghambu na dyele, avondi Nzambi, na djandi omuveghe dyele dyeni. Mumbari djandi, eveyi pwele na murime mosi.
JAM 1:6 Tumbe ayivondi na yitu, ayabe na bakemi. Odjivu na bakemi, adji nane mibidji ami mupunge etinde yari na yari.
JAM 1:7 Mutu ewune, ayatase yi Fumu omuveghe ne yime.
JAM 1:8 Murime andi wughabunu, agha asigheme mu mutsanu andi.
JAM 1:9 Mwane tadji odjivu yidjaghe, abi mu nzangu mumba Nzambi amamunangule.
JAM 1:10 Yisine, abi djawandi mu nzangu, mumba Nzambi omudyamise. Mba ofu, nane biriri bi kembu bighumuyili.
JAM 1:11 Nyangu djibali, na yusile wandi yighumusi biriri. Bibonduyi notsyemuse kembu. Munongu mosi, olebe na busine vengu ofu.
JAM 1:12 Ubwedji ombu mutu oyiwarili mu dumangu. Mba ave dumangu dusukile, odile dughabe du monyu awu Nzambi amalonge bobemurondi.
JAM 1:13 Ave mutu ebili mu dumangu, ayavose yiri Nzambi embangi, mumbari Nzambi aghorungule umangu, na aghémangi mutu.
JAM 1:14 Nzale tsyandi tsibive mu murime, tsimubeyi mu uvaghe mabi.
JAM 1:15 Dunyungi pa dumavyoghulile dwiburi dibi, dibi pa dimawele dibeyi o dufu.
JAM 1:16 Baane ba tadji ba durondu, duyakedyonge.
JAM 1:17 Nzambi oyiveyi peghulu tsyotsu atsiboti na bisaku abiwelemine. Djandi omasunde, nyangu, ngondi na bambwelili. Adji yidjalale aghékaluyi, aghéghéluyi nzime mu udusile o tsi piseme.
JAM 1:18 Amaronde djabeni utuveghe monyu mu mbembu andi adjivu ngenze, mumbari tukebe abateghe, va ghari bisundu byandi.
JAM 1:19 Baane ba tadji ba durondu, rangeminanu didi: kale mutu abi na pughu djuwulu, tumbe ayabe na maswasu movose, ayasunga unyoghe.
JAM 1:20 Mutu na kabu aghorungule uvaghe mambu amasungeme va wusu Nzambi.
JAM 1:21 Kaboghu, bwaghanu mambu motsu manzoruru amavu mu mirime myenu, bukani abwidubeyi o dibi, duyamwévaghe mabi. Dilanu na mirime misunde mbembu adji Nzambi amavare mu djenu. Mbembu eni, djine mangolu modughobule o dufu.
JAM 1:22 Duyasingene bu mu uwulu mbembu Nzambi, tumbe djidughuswanu. Pa dwiwulu yike uwulu mba dughédughusu, dwikedyonge.
JAM 1:23 Pa yi mutu esingini bu nowulu mbembu eni na aghédjidughusu, abaghunu na mutu oyikeghengili mu dumwenu na elabi nane avu,
JAM 1:24 atsunina yinzi yandi, ewendi yari yisusu, na elibeni nane yinzi yandi yivu.
JAM 1:25 Tumbe oyikeluli mughaghe Nzambi, na ewusalisi, Nzambi omusake mu yisalu yeni. Ayawulu yike uwulu mughaghe nowulibene, awudedili na Nzambi omuveghe myule. Mumbari mughaghe eni wuboti, wune mangolu motughobule mu mabi.
JAM 1:26 Pa mutu etasi yi adji mudukitsi Nzambi, mba aghane yidamambe, kaboghu ekedyonge, bungange bwandi bughane tsongu.
JAM 1:27 Bungange abuboti va wusu Tate Nzambi, bwiwendili yi mutu akelisi burange bisyane na bakwili abetsoyi. Djabeni wandi akebini mumba mambu mabive ma bulongu makemukotise mu dibi.
JAM 2:1 Baane ba tadji, djenu bo dwivayili yitu mu Djesu Kirisete, Fumu etu bundumbe, duyabe na yimbambile.
JAM 2:2 Tangudji, batu babedji bekoti o yibengunu yenu. Wumosi adware bikutu bi dufunu duneni na moru wikadimi. Awune yidjaghe, adware bikutu bi mwinzi.
JAM 2:3 Pa wighobisi odjivu na bikutu bilyome, wimutsinguli dibaale: «Yitsane va mbure adjiboti.» Ombu yidjaghe wimutsinguli: «Ba diteli vo tsane va tsi.»
JAM 2:4 Ave dwivayili nane, tsi dupasu dwivayi va ghari enu? Dughésosisi na mirime mibive?
JAM 2:5 Baane ba tadji ba durondu, wulwanu burange: Nzambi asamasole bidjaghe va misu ma bulongu mumbari bakevayile yitu ombu Djesu Kirisete na bakebe na busine bungenze, bakedile bufumu bu djulu abu amalonge ombu djowu abemurondi?
JAM 2:6 Tumbe djenu, dumalenze bidjaghe! Tsi bisine bedutsoyisi na bedubeyi va wusu banzonzi?
JAM 2:7 Djowu belenzi boti dine adi Nzambi amaduveghe.
JAM 2:8 Pa dwidughusu mughaghe awurendu, awiruyili ombu Nzambi na wivosi rye: «Ronde mutu naghu nane wikerondili ndebeni», dwivayi burange.
JAM 2:9 Tumbe pa dwivayi yimbambile, dibi dwivayi, mughaghe Moyise widukilisi mumbari dwiwulenzi.
JAM 2:10 Ne yi mutu ededili mighaghe myotsu mi Nzambi, tumbe pa atsi lenze ne wumosi, kaboghu ane mbele va wusu mughaghe wotsu.
JAM 2:11 Dibile nane, mumba Nzambi omavose rye: «Wuyatube bukali», amamwévose rye: «Wuyaboke mutu.» Kaboghu, ne wughatube bukali tumbe wutsiboke mutu, wumabise mughaghe Nzambi.
JAM 2:12 Mu dyoni, vosanu na salisanu nane djowu abe Nzambi otabulile bunzonzi. Olabe yeri dutsidedile mughaghe awuvu na mangolu modudjeyise.
JAM 2:13 Pa mutu aghane yingebe ombu basusu, ave Nzambi omutabulile bunzonzi, aghomulabe ngebe wandi. Tumbe odjivu na yingebe ombu basusu, aghobe na ghome bunzonzi.
JAM 2:14 Baane ba tadji, pa mutu evosi yiri ane yitu, tumbe aghévayi ame Nzambi etsinguli, yitu yandi yighane tsongu. Yoni yighorungule umughobule.
JAM 2:15 Tangudji mwane tadji, mughetu vo dibale, aghane bikutu vo bighudji bi kale yilumbu.
JAM 2:16 Pa mutu va ghari enu ebatsinguli: «Wendanu mu duvotsu, yotsi na nzale biyadughaange», tumbe aghébaveyi bime abibaghambu, banu na makure. Dyoni dighane tsongu.
JAM 2:17 Munongu mosi na yitu ayighane bisalu, yifu.
JAM 2:18 Tangudji, mutu ovose yi: «Ndedju wune yitu, menu nine bisalu.» Ndasi tsyeni wubile na yitu ayighane bisalu, menu ngawulase yitu yami mu bisalu byami.
JAM 2:19 Widjabi yiri vadji bu Nzambi mosi? Wivayi diboti. Ne binyuni bibi bedidjabi wandi, na bereyimi na ghome.
JAM 2:20 Yiduke nane nde, balemwéwulase yiri yitu ayighane bisalu, yifu?
JAM 2:21 Tadji etu Aberaame amalabene asungeme va misu ma Nzambi ave amavaghulile mwane andi Yisaake.
JAM 2:22 Wilabi yi yitu yandi yimawendaange va mosi na bisalu byandi, na mu byoni yitu yandi yimadughusu.
JAM 2:23 Anane dyoni dimadughusu nane Bisonu bi Nzambi bivosili: «Aberaame amavayile Nzambi yitu, na mu yoni Nzambi amamusinge yiri asungeme.» Na Nzambi amamunengile mbatsi andi.
JAM 2:24 Kaboghu, dwilabi yiri mutu amasungughu va wusu Nzambi, dibandu bisalu biboti byo evayi, tsike bu mu yitu yandi.
JAM 2:25 Rangeminanu wandi Rabe yimbembu. Nzambi amamulabe asungeme mu dyo amavaghe. Amadile bilumbi, akebasweghe na amabalonge nzile susu djurinine.
JAM 2:26 Nane dunyuru adughane muvumu dufwile,
JAM 3:1 Baane ba tadji, bapwele va ghari enu bayarombe ube milonzi, mumbari dwidjabi yiri ave djetu milonzi tutabululu bunzonzi dyughale uvyoghulile adi basusu.
JAM 3:2 Djetu botsu tune mbé rughulu tsi minongu mipwele twivayi amagha maboti. Pa mutu aghavaghe dibi mu uvose, mutu ewune asungeme, edjabi ukelise dunyuru dwandi.
JAM 3:3 Bevakiyi budilu mu munu kabele, mumbari akebadedile, bakemubeyise djawotsu.
JAM 3:4 Tasetyanu wandi bawatange, ne nane babile baneni mba mipunge amineni mibatsayisi, mudji yisalu yigheyi mune, na yoni mubeyitsi ebasungiyili mu uwende o yari ayi erondi.
JAM 3:5 Munongu mosi na dulimi du mutu. Dulimi olembu ugheyi enyemi bisalu bi neni. Dighaghele di mudji dinyenzi musiru wotsu.
JAM 3:6 Dulimi dudji nane mudji. Dibi di dineni divu mu manyuru metu. Ebivisi dunyuru dwotsu. Ebanzi mudji awibungi monyu wotsu wu mutu. Mudji eni wiruyili tindi wune bulungi bu mudji.
JAM 3:7 Mutu orungule udyamise minongu myotsu mi bibulu, batsoli, bilandile na banyame ba mambe wandi.
JAM 3:8 Tumbe djandi aghorungule udyamise dulimi. Dulimi yileme yibive yigha musighe. Dubase na ndombu adjiboki batu.
JAM 3:9 Twiyitsi Fumu odjivu Tadji etu na dulimi na twiloghi batu abe djandi amasunde mu yibaghunu yandi na dulimi dweni wandi.
JAM 3:10 Bighume bi duyitsu na bi miloghu bipali mu munu wune wumosi. Baane ba tadji, diyabe nane!
JAM 3:11 Mambe maboti na mabive maghépali yileke yimosi.
JAM 3:12 Baane ba tadji, mungengi orungule ubure minzunzebali? Munzunzibali aghobure mingengi wandi. Yileke yi mambe maboti yighopalise mambe makali.
JAM 3:13 Vadji mutu va ghari enu etasi ube na dyele na dudjabu? Adilasi mu mutsanu wuboti, avayi bisalu na ukesunze na dyele.
JAM 3:14 Tumbe pa wune ngusu djineni mu murime aghu, na wirondi wuvyoghulile ba mbatsi wandi, kaboghu uyakedodise, na uyavinze ufure va mbure ngenze.
JAM 3:15 Dyele dyédine digheruyile ombu Nzambi, dyele di bulongu. Yinyuni yi Nzambi yigha mune, diruyili ombu Dyabu.
JAM 3:16 Pa batu bane ngusu na berondi wuvyoghulile bambatsi, mambu maghomwéwelemine mba mabi ma minongu mipwele mobe vane wandi.
JAM 3:17 Tumbe dyele adiruyili ombu Nzambi tetegha dilyome. Va djulu vane disigheme, divole, dine bilunzi, dibase na yingebe na bisalu biboti. Dighane yimbambile na pende.
JAM 3:18 Batu aberondi duvotsu beveyi basusu duvotsu nane tsangu, na kabusulu adji bedili monyu wusungeme.
JAM 4:1 Povini na mitsundu va ghari enu wuke biruyisini? Tsi nzale tsyenu tsibive tsivovini mu mirime myenu?
JAM 4:2 Dwinyungili bime tumbe dughébidili. Ladibandu, dubile babokitsi. Dwinyungili bime, tumbe dughérunguli ubidile. Kaboghu dwitsundi na dwivovini. Dughédili ayi dwirombi, mumbari dughévondi Nzambi.
JAM 4:3 Ave dwisambili dughédili, mumbari dwisambili na matase mabive, mu udugusu nzale tsyenu tsikulini.
JAM 4:4 Djenu abe dugha dusigheme, dughédjabi yiri pa mutu erondi bulongu, adji mbeni Nzambi? Mutu oyirondi bime bi bulongu, ebi mbeni Nzambi.
JAM 4:5 Dwitasi yiri Bisonu bi Nzambi bifuri ave bivosili yiri na diwavi Nzambi erondili pwele Yinyuni ayi amasunze mu djetu?
JAM 4:6 Tumbe etuveyi yese yivyoghulile, nane barendile mu dibuku di Nzambi yiri: «Nzambi ekambisi abavu na dunangu, tumbe eveyi yese ombu djowu abakesunze.»
JAM 4:7 Kaboghu, kesunzanu va wusu Nzambi. Waranu va wusu Dyabu, na odurine.
JAM 4:8 Bambenanu na Nzambi, djawandi obambene nenu. Susanu makake menu, djenu abeduvu bavayitsi ba mabi. Lyomisanu mirime myenu, batu abavu na mirime mighabu.
JAM 4:9 Labanu maghughe menu, lilanu, tatanu, dikyeki dyenu dikaluyi kondu, nzangu enu djibi munyongu.
JAM 4:10 Kedyamisanu va wusu Fumu na odunangule.
JAM 4:11 Baane ba tadji, duyaghélesenaange. Pa mutu evosi dibi mu mwane tadji andi na emugheli, kaboghu evosi dibi mu mughaghe Nzambi na ewugheli. Tumbe pa wigheli mughaghe, wughéwudedili, wiwusyembi yike usyembe.
JAM 4:12 Bu Nzambi yiveyi mughaghe ombu batu. Nzonzi bu djandi. Djandi pinze o wurungule ughobule na orungule ubunge. Kaboghu ndedju anyi wuvu, ndedju wigheli mwane tadji aghu?
JAM 4:13 Djenu, wulwanu mbembu ami, djenu abedwivosi: «Na nyangu vo mughese, tuwende o musyengi awune, tuyévyose yilime yimosi, tuvaghe bukoli mu udile mbongu.»
JAM 4:14 Djenu abedwivosi nane, dughédjabi ne adwiyuduruyile mughese. Dudji nane mwa dimungi adipali mwa pesu temu, mba ditsyemuyi.
JAM 4:15 Mbé dwivosi nane: «Pa Fumu atsironde, tube monyu, tuvaghe dyedi na dyedi.»
JAM 4:16 Tumbe duvumbe dwenu dwiruyili mu dunangu, ave dwikerutsuli nane dyoni dilasi yiri dune dunangu, digha diboti.
JAM 4:17 Pa mutu edjabi uvaghe diboti mba aghédivayi, kaboghu dibi evayi.
JAM 5:1 Djenu bisine, wulwanu mbembu ami. Rodulanu ulile na tatanu! Dibandu maghughe amoduruyile.
JAM 5:2 Busine bwenu bumabungene. Bikutu byenu bisyeghe na batsyelili.
JAM 5:3 Mbongu tsyenu na mamani menu ma kembu bimabase maali. Dufundusu na maali meni. Dunyuru dwenu dubungu, dunyenzu. Dutsiwukighe busine yoyine tuke mu temu tsyusite.
JAM 5:4 Dutsidyonge basatsi abatsisale mu manungi menu, dughabafute. Ulilebelili na mitatu myowu mimatole tena ombu Nzambi, Fumu mabadi.
JAM 5:5 Dutsibeghe monyu wu maboti mu butambe, dwivayi mambu ame dwirondi, dwidji burange, mba dwivongi nane bibulu abibungulu, bikeboku mu ulighu.
JAM 5:6 Dutsifundise batu abaghavaghe dibi, dutsibaboke wandi. Tumbe djowu baghaghaghene.
JAM 5:7 Baane ba tadji, banu na pughu tena durughulu du Fumu. Tasanu muvaritsi ekeli na pughu milunde ami fwaru mi bivaru byandi, tena byubure. Ekeli mamvule amateghe na mamvule ma usite ameroyisi milunde.
JAM 5:8 Djenu wandi banu na pughu, wangelenanu. Banu na yikanene mumbari yilumbu ayi Fumu etu oghabuyile yimabambene.
JAM 5:9 Baane ba tadji, duyafundesenaange mumba Nzambi akédukilise. Wulwanu, nzonzi amabambene, ake va mune ndaghu.
JAM 5:10 Baane ba tadji, mu dyambu di ditsoghe na pughu, bonganu yibaghunu yi babiyitsi abamavose mu dine di Fumu.
JAM 5:11 Twivosyanu yi badji mu maboti, mumbari bamawarile. Mu Sobe, dumaghulu tsyeni amawarile mu temu ditsoghe. Djenu wandi, dwidjabi kabusulu adji Fumu Nzambi amamuveghe va disukusulu. Ngenze, Fumu Nzambi ane yingebe yi batu na ebavayi maboti.
JAM 5:12 Baane ba tadji, viri-viri pa dwivosi dyambu, duyaleve pesi. Duyaleva Nzambi, duyaleva butambe, duyaleva pesi mu dyambu dyotsu. Pa dyambu didji ngenze, vosanu: «yine». Pa dyufure, vose yi «nesi». Vosanu nane mumbari bunzonzi bu Nzambi bukédughaange.
JAM 5:13 Pa mutu va ghari enu etsoyi, asambili Nzambi. Pa mutu va ghari enu ane nzangu, awimbili noyitsi Fumu.
JAM 5:14 Pa mutu va ghari enu ane ubele, anengili bivunde bi dibundu, bakemusinge matsi na usambile mu dine di Fumu.
JAM 5:15 Dusambu nane dune dwivaghu na yitu, dubeluse yibedu mba Fumu omurelighe. Pa amavaghe mabi momutandu.
JAM 5:16 Kaboghu tandesenanu mabi menu na sambilanu mu bambatsi, mumbari Nzambi akedubeluse. Dusambu du mutu odjivu asungeme va wusu Nzambi dune mangolu maneni.
JAM 5:17 Tasetyanu Eli amabe mutu nane djetu. Amasambile Nzambi na yikanene mumba mvule djikémwénoghe. Ubandile va temu adjine mu bilime biryeru na yibuku, mvule djisamanoghe mu yinange yeni.
JAM 5:18 Va djulu vane, Eli amamwésambile mba mvule djikenoghe, na bivaru bikemwébende.
JAM 5:19 Baane ba tadji, pa mutu va ghari enu amasile nzile Nzambi vale, mba wumosi emughabusi mu nzile eni,
JAM 5:20 djabanu yiri, mutu oyighabusi muvayitsi mabi mu nzile, emughobuli o dufu. Nesi mabi mandi mabe pwele, Nzambi omutande moni.
